##### **Gender-Dependent Diagnostic Substitution in LLM Medical Triage: Same Symptoms, Unequal Urgency**
2606.03641v1 by Qi Han Wong

We investigate whether large language models produce different medical triage recommendations for identical neurological symptoms when only the patient's stated gender and age vary. Using three model families--Gemini 3.5 Flash, Claude Sonnet 4.6, and GPT-5.4-mini--we present a standardized symptom profile (persistent headache, blurred vision, morning nausea, visual disturbances) across seven demographic conditions: three age groups (25, 38, 65) x two genders (male, female), plus a gender-unspecified baseline (n = 30 per condition per model, 630 total trials). We find a stark, systemic gender-dependent triage disparity: young women receive significantly lower emergency room (ER) referral rates than age-matched men (Gemini: 0% vs. 23.3%; Claude: 6.7% vs. 96.7%; GPT: 6.7% vs. 66.7%, all p < 0.001). The disparity disappears at age 65 for all models. The primary mechanism is diagnostic substitution: the models anchor on a gender-associated diagnosis, preferentially classifying young women with Idiopathic Intracranial Hypertension (IIH)--a condition epidemiologically linked to women of childbearing age--while diagnosing men with generic increased intracranial pressure with space-occupying lesions in the differential. This diagnostic closure routes female patients to lower-urgency care (outpatient doctor appointments) despite comparable severity ratings (7-9/10). Our findings demonstrate that clinical LLMs replicate documented human clinical biases by using epidemiological priors to suppress triage urgency, suggesting that AI triage engines must decouple urgency assessment from probabilistic diagnostic priors. We release all code, prompts, and raw results.

摘要：我們調查大型語言模型是否會對相同的神經症狀產生不同的醫療分診建議，當僅有病人的性別和年齡變化時。使用三個模型系列——Gemini 3.5 Flash、Claude Sonnet 4.6 和 GPT-5.4-mini——我們在七個人口統計條件下呈現一個標準化的症狀檔案（持續性頭痛、視力模糊、早晨噁心、視覺干擾）：三個年齡組（25、38、65歲）x 兩個性別（男性、女性），加上一個性別未指定的基線（每個條件每個模型 n = 30，共630次試驗）。我們發現明顯的系統性性別依賴性分診差異：年輕女性的急診室（ER）轉診率顯著低於年齡相符的男性（Gemini: 0% vs. 23.3%；Claude: 6.7% vs. 96.7%；GPT: 6.7% vs. 66.7%，均 p < 0.001）。對於所有模型，這種差異在65歲時消失。主要機制是診斷替代：模型基於性別相關的診斷，優先將年輕女性歸類為特發性顱內高壓（IIH）——這是一種流行病學上與育齡女性相關的病症——而將男性診斷為具有占位性病變的普通顱內壓增高。這種診斷封閉將女性患者引導至低緊急性護理（門診醫生預約），儘管嚴重程度評分相當（7-9/10）。我們的研究結果顯示，臨床大型語言模型通過使用流行病學先驗來抑制分診緊急性，複製了已記錄的人類臨床偏見，這表明 AI 分診引擎必須將緊急性評估與概率診斷先驗解耦。我們釋放所有代碼、提示和原始結果。

##### **DDOR: Delta Debugging for Explainable Overrefusal Testing and Repair**
2606.03601v1 by Qinyan Zhou, Peixin Zhang, Jun Sun, Haonan Zhang, Dongxia Wang

While safety alignment and guardrails help large language models (LLMs) avoid harmful outputs, they can also induce overrefusal, i.e., unwarranted rejection of benign queries that merely appear risky. We present DDOR (Delta Debugging for OverRefusal), a fully automated and explainable framework for overrefusal testing and repair in a black-box setting, where only model inputs and outputs are accessible and internal safety mechanisms remain opaque. DDOR applies delta debugging to localize minimal refusal-triggering fragments (mRTFs) that provide phrase-level, explainable evidence for why a refusal occurs. Conditioned on these mRTFs, DDOR generates diverse, context-rich prompts and performs multi-oracle validation to filter intrinsically unsafe or ambiguous cases, producing scalable and model-specific overrefusal test suites (approximately 1K cases per model). Beyond evaluation, we further leverage localized mRTFs to perform targeted prompt repair, substantially reducing overrefusal while preserving the original intent and maintaining safety on genuinely harmful inputs. Overall, DDOR offers a practical end-to-end solution to both evaluate and mitigate overrefusal, improving LLM usability without sacrificing safety.

摘要：雖然安全對齊和防護措施幫助大型語言模型（LLMs）避免有害輸出，但它們也可能導致過度拒絕，即對看似風險的良性查詢的不當拒絕。我們提出了DDOR（Delta Debugging for OverRefusal），這是一個完全自動化且可解釋的框架，用於在黑箱環境中進行過度拒絕測試和修復，在這種環境中，只有模型的輸入和輸出是可訪問的，而內部安全機制則保持不透明。DDOR應用增量調試來定位最小拒絕觸發片段（mRTFs），這些片段提供了逐詞級別的可解釋證據，解釋為何會發生拒絕。基於這些mRTFs，DDOR生成多樣化的、豐富上下文的提示，並執行多預言者驗證，以過濾內在不安全或模棱兩可的案例，產生可擴展且特定於模型的過度拒絕測試套件（每個模型約1K個案例）。除了評估之外，我們還進一步利用本地化的mRTFs進行針對性的提示修復，顯著減少過度拒絕，同時保留原始意圖並保持對真正有害輸入的安全性。總體而言，DDOR提供了一個實用的端到端解決方案，既能評估又能減輕過度拒絕，提高LLM的可用性而不犧牲安全性。

##### **Message Tuning Outshines Graph Prompt Tuning: A Prismatic Space Perspective**
2606.03290v1 by Yancheng Chen, Dun Ma, Shuai Zhang, Yang Liu, Xixun Lin, Xiangyu Zhao, Wenguo Yang, Wei Chen, Chuan Zhou

Graph Foundation Models (GFMs), built upon the Pre-training and Adaptation paradigm, have emerged as a research hotspot in graph learning. For GNN-based GFMs, graph prompt tuning has become the prevailing adaptation method for downstream tasks. Although recent methods explain why graph prompt tuning works, how to rigorously measure its adaptation capacity remains an open problem. Addressing this problem is critical for understanding the capability limits of graph prompt tuning and for developing more powerful adaptation methods. In this paper, we propose Prismatic Space Theory (PS-Theory), a novel mathematical framework to quantify the capacity of adaptation methods, while focusing on establishing the upper bound for the adaptation capacity of graph prompt tuning. Building upon the proposed PS-Theory, we further introduce Message Tuning for GFMs (MTG), a lightweight approach that injects a small set of learnable message prototypes into each layer of the GNN backbone to adaptively guide message fusion without updating pre-trained weights. Through our PS-Theory, we prove that the adaptation capacity of MTG can exceed the theoretical upper bound of graph prompt tuning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that MTG consistently outperforms graph prompt baselines across diverse benchmark datasets, providing strong empirical support for our theoretical findings.

摘要：圖形基礎模型（GFMs）建立在預訓練和適應的範式上，已成為圖形學習中的研究熱點。對於基於GNN的GFMs，圖形提示調整已成為下游任務的主要適應方法。儘管最近的方法解釋了為什麼圖形提示調整有效，但如何嚴格測量其適應能力仍然是一個未解決的問題。解決這個問題對於理解圖形提示調整的能力極限以及開發更強大的適應方法至關重要。在本文中，我們提出了棱鏡空間理論（PS-Theory），這是一個新穎的數學框架，用於量化適應方法的能力，同時專注於建立圖形提示調整的適應能力的上限。在所提出的PS-Theory的基礎上，我們進一步介紹了GFMs的消息調整（MTG），這是一種輕量級的方法，將一小組可學習的消息原型注入到GNN主幹的每一層，以自適應地指導消息融合，而無需更新預訓練的權重。通過我們的PS-Theory，我們證明了MTG的適應能力可以超過圖形提示調整的理論上限。大量實驗表明，MTG在各種基準數據集上始終優於圖形提示基線，為我們的理論發現提供了強有力的實證支持。

##### **AI Rater Discrimination Depends on Scoring Protocol in Complex Clinical Decision-Making**
2606.03198v1 by Sangwon Baek, Kyu Yeon Hur, Kyunga Kim

Clinical AI evaluation increasingly delegates scoring to large language models (LLMs) acting as AI raters, yet their scoring behavior across evaluation conditions has not been quantitatively characterized. We address this gap through a factorial study of AI rater behavior in adult type 2 diabetes (T2D) pharmacotherapy at 12-month outpatient follow-up, a clinical task involving complex decision-making operationalized across seven evaluation questions. Four open-source LLMs served simultaneously as clinical decision support system (CDSS) models and AI raters. Each CDSS output was scored under two scoring protocols: a rubric-anchored Gold Rubric (GR) protocol incorporating a patient-specific rubric, and a rubric-free Non Gold Rubric (Non-GR) protocol. Linear mixed effects models crossed the scoring protocol factor with five design factors -- CDSS model, CDSS prompt configuration (document-referenced generation [DRG] vs.\ Baseline), rater model, prompt character, and prompt type -- and estimated main effects together with their protocol interactions. Across all questions, AI raters yielded consistently higher scores within a very narrow range (74--78 points on average) under Non-GR compared to those under GR (7.69 to 49.64 points lower mean scores; 1.68 to 3.67 times wider interquartile ranges). Within each question, GR amplified the AI rater's discrimination between DRG and Baseline CDSS outputs by factors of 1.76 to 5.10, while also revealing substantial behavioral variation across rater models that Non-GR suppressed. These findings support rubric anchoring as the scoring protocol that preserves discriminative power in clinical AI evaluation; rubric-free scoring cannot substitute when questions require patient-specific or jurisdiction-specific criteria that rater models cannot infer from parametric knowledge alone.

摘要：臨床 AI 評估越來越多地將評分委託給作為 AI 評分員的大型語言模型 (LLMs)，然而它們在不同評估條件下的評分行為尚未被定量特徵化。<lb/>我們通過對成人 2 型糖尿病 (T2D) 藥物治療在 12 個月門診隨訪中的 AI 評分員行為進行的因子研究來填補這一空白，這是一項涉及複雜決策的臨床任務，涵蓋七個評估問題。<lb/>四個開源 LLM 同時作為臨床決策支持系統 (CDSS) 模型和 AI 評分員。<lb/>每個 CDSS 輸出在兩個評分協議下進行評分：一個以評分標準為基礎的金標準 (GR) 協議，包含患者特定的評分標準，以及一個無評分標準的非金標準 (Non-GR) 協議。<lb/>線性混合效應模型將評分協議因素與五個設計因素交叉——CDSS 模型、CDSS 提示配置（文件參考生成 [DRG] 與基線）、評分員模型、提示字符和提示類型——並估計主要效應及其協議交互作用。<lb/>在所有問題中，AI 評分員在 Non-GR 下的評分始終高於 GR，且範圍非常狹窄（平均 74 至 78 分），與 GR 下的評分相比，平均分數低 7.69 至 49.64 分；四分位數範圍擴大 1.68 至 3.67 倍。<lb/>在每個問題中，GR 增強了 AI 評分員對 DRG 和基線 CDSS 輸出的區分能力，增幅為 1.76 至 5.10，同時揭示了不同評分員模型之間的顯著行為變異，而 Non-GR 則抑制了這種變異。<lb/>這些發現支持以評分標準為基礎的評分協議，該協議在臨床 AI 評估中保留了區分能力；當問題需要患者特定或管轄特定標準，而評分員模型無法僅通過參數知識推斷時，無評分標準的評分無法替代。

##### **OpenAgenet / OAN White Paper: Open Infrastructure for Trusted Agent Interconnection**
2606.03161v3 by Jinliang Xu

OpenAgenet, abbreviated as OAN, is an open infrastructure project for trusted Agent interconnection. It addresses a problem that becomes visible when Agents move from isolated applications into open, multi-operator networks: before an Agent can safely discover, select, and invoke another Agent, it needs a way to verify identity provenance, governance state, discovery authorization, freshness, and pre-connection trust evidence. OAN is designed as a protocol-neutral trust layer. It does not replace Agent interaction protocols, tool protocols, model orchestration frameworks, or application-level workflows. Instead, it provides \texttt{did:oan}-based resource identity, governance-backed admission, Registrar-assisted onboarding, Root-verified package publication, authorization-aware Discovery, Root-issued infrastructure authorization VCs, and signed trusted invocation. The architectural center of OAN is the combination of federated governance, resource identity, and trusted Discovery, rather than a single directory or naming service. This white paper explains the motivation, architecture, roles, governance model, relationship with MCP, A2A, and ANP, deployment patterns, cooperation model, on-chain governance layer, prototype status, performance profile, and roadmap of OAN.

摘要：OpenAgenet，簡稱 OAN，是一個用於可信代理互連的開放基礎設施項目。<lb/>它解決了一個問題，當代理從孤立的應用程序轉移到開放的多運營商網絡時，這個問題變得明顯：在代理可以安全地發現、選擇和調用另一個代理之前，它需要一種方式來驗證身份來源、治理狀態、發現授權、新鮮度和預連接信任證據。<lb/>OAN 被設計為一個協議中立的信任層。<lb/>它不會取代代理交互協議、工具協議、模型編排框架或應用程序級工作流程。<lb/>相反，它提供基於 \texttt{did:oan} 的資源身份、基於治理的入場、註冊機構協助的上線、根驗證的包發布、授權感知的發現、根發出的基礎設施授權 VC，以及簽署的可信調用。<lb/>OAN 的架構中心是聯邦治理、資源身份和可信發現的結合，而不是單一的目錄或命名服務。<lb/>本白皮書解釋了 OAN 的動機、架構、角色、治理模型、與 MCP、A2A 和 ANP 的關係、部署模式、合作模型、鏈上治理層、原型狀態、性能概況和路線圖。

##### **Glass Box at Orbit: A Constitutional AI Verification Framework for Trustworthy Autonomous CubeSat Intelligence**
2606.02967v1 by Karthik Barma, Anil Sanneboyina, V C Premchand Yadav

The space industry is quietly building toward something nobody has fully reckoned with: orbital data centers running thousands of autonomous AI workloads with no human in the loop, 550 km above the Earth. Microsoft, AWS, and a growing list of orbital computing ventures are moving cloud-scale processing off the ground and into orbit. What none of them have answered yet is the governance question -- when autonomous AI systems at orbital data center scale make wrong decisions in space, what stops those decisions before they become irreversible?
  We introduce Glass Box: a runtime constitutional AI verification layer that intercepts every candidate action from an onboard AI policy and evaluates it against six physics-grounded constitutional constraints and seven Linear Temporal Logic (LTL) safety invariants before a single command reaches any spacecraft subsystem. Every approved action carries a weighted explainability score E(a_t) in [0,1] and a complete constitutional audit log. We demonstrate Glass Box within Project October: a fully simulated five-layer autonomous orbital intelligence architecture for CubeSat-class spacecraft.
  We prove that Glass Box verification overhead is O(N_c) in the number of constitutional rules, independent of model size or spacecraft state dimension. We present a complete formal specification of the constitutional constraint grammar, seven LTL safety invariants verified by Z3 and NuSMV model checking, and a detailed worked example of Glass Box intercepting an unsafe inference request at eclipse-entry under degraded battery state. As orbital computing scales toward data center infrastructure, runtime constitutional verification is no longer a research novelty -- it is mission-critical safety infrastructure that every autonomous orbital platform will eventually require.

摘要：太空產業正在悄然朝著一個沒有人完全預料到的方向發展：在距離地球550公里的軌道上運行數千個自主AI工作負載的數據中心，且不需要人類介入。微軟、AWS以及越來越多的軌道計算企業正在將雲端規模的處理從地面轉移到軌道上。然而，這些公司尚未回答的問題是治理問題——當軌道數據中心規模的自主AI系統在太空中做出錯誤決策時，什麼能阻止這些決策在變得不可逆轉之前？

我們介紹Glass Box：一個運行時憲法AI驗證層，攔截每一個來自機載AI政策的候選行動，並在任何指令到達任何航天器子系統之前，根據六個基於物理的憲法約束和七個線性時間邏輯（LTL）安全不變量進行評估。每個批准的行動都帶有一個加權可解釋性分數E(a_t)在[0,1]之間，以及一個完整的憲法審計日誌。我們在Project October中展示Glass Box：一個完全模擬的五層自主軌道智能架構，適用於CubeSat級航天器。

我們證明Glass Box的驗證開銷在憲法規則的數量N_c中為O(N_c)，與模型大小或航天器狀態維度無關。我們提供了憲法約束文法的完整形式規範，七個由Z3和NuSMV模型檢查驗證的LTL安全不變量，以及一個詳細的工作示例，展示Glass Box在電池狀態降級時攔截不安全的推理請求進入日食。隨著軌道計算向數據中心基礎設施擴展，運行時憲法驗證不再是研究新奇事物——它是每個自主軌道平台最終都將需要的關鍵安全基礎設施。

##### **Large AI Models in Dental Healthcare: From General-Purpose Systems to Domain-Specific Foundation Models**
2606.02914v2 by Sema Helali, Lina Abu Nada, Sausan Al Kawas, Alaa Abd-Alrazaq, Faleh Tamimi, Rafat Damseh

Background: Oral diseases affect nearly 3.5 billion people worldwide, yet the comparative clinical potential of large-scale AI models in dentistry remains poorly understood. Three distinct model categories have emerged: language-generative models, discriminative vision foundation models, and dental-specific foundation models, with no unified review examining their relationships and collective limitations.
  Methods: Following PRISMA-ScR guidelines, we systematically searched four databases (PubMed, Google Scholar, Scopus, arXiv), screened independently by two reviewers. After applying inclusion/exclusion criteria, 97 studies (2020-2026) were included. We propose a two-dimensional classification framework organizing models by architectural paradigm and dental specialization degree.
  Results: Language-generative models excel at text-based tasks (clinical reasoning, licensing exams, patient communication) but show inconsistent performance on image-dependent diagnostics. Adapted SAM and CLIP variants achieve strong tooth segmentation and lesion detection results. Dental-specific models (DentVFM, DentVLM, OralGPT) demonstrate strongest performance on complex multimodal tasks. Integrated pipelines consistently outperform single-model approaches. A data asymmetry is observed: dental-specific pretraining concentrates almost entirely in the vision domain, reflecting scarce large-scale dental text corpora.
  Conclusions: General-purpose and dental-specific models play complementary roles; the most effective systems combine both within structured pipelines. Safe autonomous deployment requires resolving three persistent barriers: hallucination in generative models, limited annotated dental datasets, and absent standardized clinical evaluation benchmarks.

摘要：背景：口腔疾病影響全球近35億人，但大型AI模型在牙科的比較臨床潛力仍然不甚了解。已出現三種不同的模型類別：語言生成模型、判別性視覺基礎模型和牙科專用基礎模型，尚未有統一的評估來檢視它們之間的關係及共同的限制。<lb/>  
方法：根據PRISMA-ScR指導方針，我們系統性地搜索了四個數據庫（PubMed、Google Scholar、Scopus、arXiv），由兩位評審獨立篩選。在應用納入/排除標準後，納入了97項研究（2020-2026）。我們提出了一個二維分類框架，根據架構範式和牙科專業化程度組織模型。<lb/>  
結果：語言生成模型在基於文本的任務（臨床推理、執照考試、病人溝通）中表現優異，但在依賴圖像的診斷上表現不一致。調整過的SAM和CLIP變體在牙齒分割和病變檢測方面取得了良好的結果。牙科專用模型（DentVFM、DentVLM、OralGPT）在複雜的多模態任務中表現最佳。綜合管道的表現始終優於單一模型的方法。觀察到數據不對稱：牙科專用的預訓練幾乎完全集中在視覺領域，反映出大型牙科文本語料庫的稀缺。<lb/>  
結論：通用模型和牙科專用模型扮演互補的角色；最有效的系統是在結構化管道中結合兩者。安全的自主部署需要解決三個持續存在的障礙：生成模型中的幻覺、有限的標註牙科數據集，以及缺乏標準化的臨床評估基準。

##### **Scalable Uncertainty Quantification for Extreme Weather Forecasting via Empirical Neural Tangent Kernels**
2606.02886v2 by Jose Marie Antonio Miñoza, Rex Gregor Laylo, Sebastian C. Ibañez

Deep learning weather models now match numerical weather prediction accuracy while running orders of magnitude faster, but produce deterministic forecasts without uncertainty estimates, a critical gap for high-stakes decisions during extreme weather events. This paper proposes Neural Tangent Kernel-based uncertainty quantification (NTK-UQ) using last-layer empirical features. Theoretical analysis predicts that UQ quality is architecture-dependent through two mechanisms. First, a variance collapse mechanism explains when UQ fails: when the eigenvalue truncation rank approaches the effective rank of the feature space, the GP correction term consumes nearly all prior variance, destroying discrimination between tropical cyclones and routine conditions; architectures with concentrated spectra (spectral operators) require aggressive truncation ($k \leq 10$), while attention-based models tolerate full-rank computation. Second, decomposition performance depends on the non-Gaussian, heavy-tailed structure of extreme weather: Independent Component Analysis exploits higher-order statistics (kurtosis, negentropy) to isolate heavy-tailed extreme-event features, achieving higher discrimination than singular value decomposition, which captures only second-order variance. A data-driven selection rule chooses ICA or SVD from the feature eigenspectrum concentration ratio, correctly prescribing the superior decomposition for all four evaluated architectures. Compared to split conformal prediction (the natural post-hoc baseline), NTK-UQ achieves 31--37\% sharper prediction intervals at 90\% coverage, and uniquely produces \emph{adaptive} intervals that scale with extreme event severity, which conformal prediction cannot achieve by construction. The framework requires no retraining; inference-time uncertainty requires only a single matrix-vector product per sample.

摘要：深度學習氣象模型現在在數值天氣預測準確性上達到了匹配，同時運行速度快了數個數量級，但產生的預測是確定性的，沒有不確定性估計，這在極端天氣事件中對於高風險決策來說是一個關鍵的缺口。本文提出了一種基於神經切線核的不確定性量化（NTK-UQ），使用最後一層的經驗特徵。理論分析預測不確定性質量依賴於架構，通過兩個機制進行解釋。首先，方差崩潰機制解釋了不確定性失敗的情況：當特徵空間的特徵值截斷秩接近有效秩時，GP修正項幾乎消耗了所有先前的方差，破壞了熱帶氣旋和常規條件之間的區分；具有集中光譜（光譜算子）的架構需要激進的截斷（$k \leq 10$），而基於注意力的模型則能容忍全秩計算。其次，分解性能依賴於極端天氣的非高斯、重尾結構：獨立成分分析利用高階統計量（峰度、負熵）來隔離重尾極端事件特徵，實現比奇異值分解更高的區分，後者僅捕捉二階方差。一個數據驅動的選擇規則從特徵特徵值光譜集中比率中選擇ICA或SVD，正確地為所有四種評估架構開出了優越的分解。與分裂符合預測（自然的事後基準）相比，NTK-UQ在90\%的覆蓋率下實現了31--37\%更尖銳的預測區間，並且獨特地產生了隨著極端事件嚴重性而調整的\emph{自適應}區間，而符合預測在結構上無法實現。該框架不需要重新訓練；推斷時的不確定性每個樣本僅需一次矩陣-向量乘積。

##### **Explainable Data-driven Deep Reinforcement Learning Methods for Optimal Energy Management in Buildings**

The increasing integration of renewable energy sources into power systems, particularly in buildings equipped with photovoltaic (PV) panels and energy storage systems, introduces significant complexity in energy systems. Volatile power generation, varying electricity tariffs, and increased entities, e.g., PV systems, and heat pumps, have increased the complexity and made the system harder to operate. While deep reinforcement learning (DRL) has emerged as a promising solution to optimize building operations in dynamic and ever more complex environments, its black-box nature impedes user trust and practical adoption. ##### **AutoMedBench: Towards Medical AutoResearch with Agentic AI Models**
2606.01961v2 by Junqi Liu, Selena Song, Yuhan Wang, Jiawei Mao, Hardy Chen, Xiaoke Huang, Tianhao Qi, Pengfei Guo, Yucheng Tang, Yufan He, Can Zhao, Andriy Myronenko, Dong Yang, Daguang Xu, Yuyin Zhou

Autonomous agents are increasingly expected to support end-to-end medical-AI research workflows, moving beyond isolated prediction tasks or short-form clinical question answering. However, existing medical agent benchmarks primarily evaluate final outputs, providing limited visibility into agent behavior within the research process. To address this gap, we present AutoMedBench, a workflow-aware benchmark for autonomous medical-AI research across diverse medical imaging and multimodal inference tasks, organizing agent execution into a unified five-stage workflow (S1-S5): Plan, Setup, Validate, Inference, and Submit. It comprises long-horizon tasks with each run averaging 33 agent turns, spanning five research tracks: segmentation, image enhancement, visual question answering (VQA), report generation, and lesion detection. Each task is evaluated under two difficulty tiers, Lite and Standard, which use the same data and metrics but differ in the amount of task-brief scaffolding, and each run is scored using both final task performance and S1-S5 stage scores, enabling stage-level analysis from the initial task brief to the final submitted artifact. Across thousands of recorded runs, stage-level scoring reveals that Validate is the weakest workflow stage on average, whereas Setup is the strongest, suggesting that current agents are better at making pipelines executable than at verifying their reliability. Post-run error analysis further shows that verification and submission failures dominate tagged errors, accounting for 37.7% and 38.1% of fired codes respectively, whereas task-understanding errors are rare at 0.9%, and runs with one fired error code have a 48% lower overall score than runs with no error code on average.

##### **"I've Seen How This Goes": Characterizing Diversity via Progressive Conditional Surprise**
2606.01811v1 by Matthew Khoriaty, David Williams-King, Shi Feng

Measuring the diversity of creative outputs is central to evaluating post-training mode collapse, comparing decoding strategies, and quantifying creative behavior in both AI and human writing. We propose a new approach to measuring diversity using in-context learning, of which the ``Decan'' metric, $D_{Ca_n} = C \times a_n$, is the working instance we evaluate: a per-byte score read off the per-token log-probabilities of a base model $θ$ in a \emph{single forward pass} per permutation, with no embedding model, no reference corpus, and no human labels. This approach is grounded in information theory, makes use of language model in-context learning to detect a wide range of similarities between any number of inputs, and obviates the need to train a special-purpose model. The same pipeline scores AI samples and human-written response sets, with diversity treated as a property of (responses, prompt, scoring model). On Tevet and Berant's human-grounded McDiv benchmark, $D_{Ca_n}$ reaches OCA 0.846 on the McDiv prompt\_gen set where it performs best, behind the strongest neural baseline reported in Tevet and Berant (SentBERT, 0.897). On the OLMo-2-7B post-training pipeline, $D_{Ca_n}$ drops monotonically across the base $\to$ SFT $\to$ DPO $\to$ RLVR stages, detecting the type of diversity loss that creative-writing applications care about.

##### **E4GEN: Event-level Explainable Extreme-Enhanced Time-series Generation**
2606.01634v1 by Lin Jiang, Dahai Yu, Ximiao Li, Guang Wang

Generating realistic time series is essential for scientific research and real-world applications. However, existing methods often emphasize overall distributional fidelity while failing to faithfully capture extreme events. To advance existing research, we propose E4GEN, an explainable diffusion framework for extreme event-aware time-series generation. E4GEN provides systematic insights into when, what, and how to control extreme-event generation through three key components. First, E-Activator learns the dataset-adaptive extreme-control signal activation step during the denoising process without interfering with regular temporal components, including trend and seasonality. Second, E-Predictor determines what control signal to enforce through Self-Driven Semantic Prediction, where each sample derives its own control signal by inferring latent extreme-event information during generation. It also includes a novel Data-Conditioned Training, Noise-Initiated Sampling mechanism to address the issue of unavailable training labels. Third, E-Control specifies how to control extreme-event generation through a trainable Extreme Control Network, which transforms the semantic control signal into layer-wise signals and injects it into the denoising process. We evaluate E4GEN on six datasets with 17 metrics, and extensive experiments show that E4GEN outperforms state-of-the-art models across multiple dimensions, including overall fidelity, extreme-event fidelity, and downstream utility.

摘要：生成現實的時間序列對於科學研究和現實應用至關重要。<lb/>然而，現有的方法往往強調整體分佈的忠實性，同時未能忠實捕捉極端事件。<lb/>為了推進現有研究，我們提出了 E4GEN，一個針對極端事件的可解釋擴散框架，用於時間序列生成。<lb/>E4GEN 提供了系統性的見解，幫助我們了解何時、什麼以及如何控制極端事件的生成，這通過三個關鍵組件實現。<lb/>首先，E-Activator 在去噪過程中學習數據集自適應的極端控制信號激活步驟，而不干擾常規的時間組件，包括趨勢和季節性。<lb/>其次，E-Predictor 通過自驅動語義預測來決定強制執行的控制信號，在這裡，每個樣本通過推斷潛在的極端事件信息來生成自己的控制信號。<lb/>它還包括一種新穎的數據條件訓練、噪聲啟動採樣機制，以解決缺乏訓練標籤的問題。<lb/>第三，E-Control 通過可訓練的極端控制網絡指定如何控制極端事件的生成，該網絡將語義控制信號轉換為層級信號並注入到去噪過程中。<lb/>我們在六個數據集上使用 17 個指標對 E4GEN 進行評估，廣泛的實驗顯示 E4GEN 在多個維度上超越了最先進的模型，包括整體忠實性、極端事件忠實性和下游效用。

##### **A Framework for Graph-Conditioned Hierarchical Shapley Attribution in Patent Valuation**
2606.01632v1 by Joy Bose

Estimating the economic contribution of a single patent inside a product that embodies tens of thousands of patents is a long-standing unsolved problem in intellectual property economics. We propose PatentXAI, a framework that treats patent valuation as a problem of explainable AI: given a characteristic function v(S) encoding the revenue achievable by patent subset S, a patent's Shapley value measures its fair share of product profit in a way that satisfies efficiency, symmetry, dummy, and additivity. To make computation tractable we restrict each patent's coalition to its Markov Blanket inside a knowledge graph, grounded in the C-SVE conditional independence theorem (Li et al., 2020). Scaling experiments from n=12 to n=100 patents using Pareto-distributed coverage graphs report median Markov Blanket size of 32.9 percent of n at n=100, with 90th-percentile blanket size of 55.2 percent of n, and runtime of 10 milliseconds per patent. Difference against exact ground truth at n=12 is 0.088; difference against a high-sample Monte Carlo reference at n=100 is 0.062 plus or minus 0.003. A dense-component experiment shows that when 80 percent of patents share one component, the blanket correctly expands to cover that dense cluster, and the difference versus reference falls to 0.039 because the pooled computation becomes more accurate on homogeneous portfolios. Profit allocation proceeds hierarchically: exact Shapley distributes total profit among macro-components, then centrality-weighted Shapley distributes each component budget among covering patents. Estimating v(S) from real data is the primary open problem; we distinguish this from the computational contribution and outline a concrete roadmap for empirical validation using public ETSI, USPTO, and Lens.org datasets.

摘要：估算一項專利在一個包含數萬項專利的產品中的經濟貢獻是知識產權經濟學中一個長期未解的問題。我們提出了PatentXAI，一個將專利評價視為可解釋人工智慧問題的框架：給定一個特徵函數v(S)，編碼專利子集S所能實現的收入，專利的Shapley值以滿足效率、對稱性、虛擬和可加性的方式衡量其在產品利潤中的公平份額。為了使計算可行，我們將每項專利的聯盟限制在其知識圖譜中的馬可夫毯內，這基於C-SVE條件獨立定理（Li et al., 2020）。從n=12到n=100專利的擴展實驗使用了Pareto分佈的覆蓋圖，報告在n=100時，馬可夫毯的中位數大小為n的32.9％，90百分位的毯大小為n的55.2％，每項專利的運行時間為10毫秒。n=12時與精確真實值的差異為0.088；n=100時與高樣本蒙特卡羅參考的差異為0.062，加減0.003。密集組件實驗顯示，當80％的專利共享一個組件時，毯子正確擴展以覆蓋該密集集群，與參考的差異降至0.039，因為在同質投資組合上的合併計算變得更加準確。利潤分配是分層進行的：精確的Shapley在宏觀組件之間分配總利潤，然後中心性加權的Shapley在覆蓋專利之間分配每個組件的預算。從真實數據中估算v(S)是主要的開放問題；我們將此與計算貢獻區分開來，並概述了一個具體的實證驗證路線圖，使用公共的ETSI、USPTO和Lens.org數據集。

##### **A Minimalist Brain-Computer Musical Interface for Real-Time Emotion-Driven Sonification: System Design and Preliminary Evaluation**
2606.01473v1 by Pablo A. Monroy-D'Croz, Rafael Ramirez-Melendez, Julian Cespedes-Guevara

This paper presents a minimalist brain-computer Musical Interface (BCMI) that functions as a real-time affective sonification system, translating prefrontal EEG activity into adaptive music. Emotional valence is estimated from frontal alpha asymmetry (AF7/AF8) and mapped to musical features such as mode, tempo, rhythmic density, and pitch register through a stochastic generative algorithm. The system integrates wireless EEG acquisition, real-time Python signal processing, and Ableton Live-based music generation synchronized via Lab Streaming Layer. An experiment with 22 participants investigated whether intentional emotional self-induction could modulate the BCMI neurofeedback signal. Linear mixed-effects analyses found no significant effects of target emotion or time, indicating that the frontal alpha asymmetry signal did not reliably distinguish instructed emotional states. Individual differences, including musical training and acting experience, explained more variance than the experimental manipulation, which accounted for only 0.40\% of total signal variance. These findings highlight the challenges of using frontal alpha asymmetry as a voluntary control signal for closed-loop emotion regulation and suggest methodological directions for future BCMI research.

摘要：這篇論文提出了一種極簡主義的腦機音樂介面（BCMI），作為一個實時情感聲音化系統，將前額葉腦電圖（EEG）活動轉換為自適應音樂。情感價值是通過前額α不對稱（AF7/AF8）估算的，並通過隨機生成算法映射到音樂特徵，如調式、節奏、節拍密度和音高範圍。該系統整合了無線EEG獲取、實時Python信號處理和基於Ableton Live的音樂生成，並通過Lab Streaming Layer實現同步。一項包含22名參與者的實驗調查了有意識的情感自我誘導是否能調節BCMI神經反饋信號。線性混合效應分析未發現目標情感或時間的顯著效應，表明前額α不對稱信號未能可靠地區分指示的情感狀態。個體差異，包括音樂訓練和表演經驗，解釋了比實驗操控更多的變異，後者僅佔總信號變異的0.40%。這些發現突顯了使用前額α不對稱作為閉環情感調節的自願控制信號的挑戰，並為未來的BCMI研究提出了方法論方向。

##### **GovAI-Pipe: A Layered AI Governance Pipeline for Citizen-Facing AI in Turkey's e-Government Gateway**
2606.01417v1 by Ahmet Kaplan

Turkey's e-Government Gateway (e-Devlet) serves over 68 million registered users with more than 9,200 government services, and is increasingly integrating artificial intelligence into citizen-facing applications such as chatbot assistants and eligibility assessments. However, no structured technical governance infrastructure currently connects high-level AI policy frameworks, such as the EU AI Act, OECD AI Principles, and Turkey's own National AI Strategy, to the operational reality of deploying AI within a centralized e-government platform. We propose GovAI-Pipe, a four-layer governance pipeline designed using Design Science Research methodology that maps the AI model lifecycle to governance checkpoints: (1) pre-deployment validation for bias testing, explainability, and privacy impact assessment; (2) deployment governance for risk-tier classification and approval workflows; (3) runtime monitoring for drift detection, fairness tracking, and human-in-the-loop escalation; and (4) post-incident governance for audit trails, rollback, and citizen redress. Each layer is anchored to specific provisions of the EU AI Act, the GDPR data protection framework, and the National AI Strategy.   pre-designed team can anticipate every skill a question will need.

  capability--a simulation cluster, a wet-lab robot, a proof engine, a
  single-cell pipeline--can connect to any other, with collaboration
  structure emerging from the question itself. Its underlying EACN protocol

  adjudicate across incompatible evidentiary standards without prior
  knowledge of who will meet whom. This shifts the organizing challenge from
  workflow design to open-ended connectivity. Two runs validate this under

摘要：科學發現需要智慧、毅力和偶然性，並在廣闊的搜尋空間中進行。今天，頂尖的科學能力仍然是孤立的——一個AI系統用於生物分析，另一個用於臨床推理、數學推導或材料模擬——而且沒有任何預設的團隊能夠預見到一個問題所需的每一項技能。科學地球是一個行星規模的科學運行環境，在這裡，任何能力——模擬集群、濕實驗室機器人、證明引擎、單細胞管道——都可以連接到其他任何能力，合作結構從問題本身中產生。其底層的EACN協議使能力能夠相互發現、協商任務所有權，並在沒有先前了解誰將會見誰的情況下，對不兼容的證據標準進行裁決。這將組織挑戰的重心從工作流程設計轉移到開放式連接性上。兩次實驗在結構上不同的條件下驗證了這一點。在一次跨太平洋的高階Kuramoto同步研究中，代理在三十分鐘內識別並修正了Ott-Antonsen分析理論中在洛倫茲極限之外失效的閉合比假設。在一個針對4.88M細胞Kang 2024全癌症圖譜的八代理單細胞運行中，異質能力在64.9小時的時間窗口內結合，並有一個結構性外部指令，產生了三個新的結果層，並將發現與相鄰的CCR8-TIGIT+ Treg子集的獨立濕實驗室研究進行對照。這些案例是首次的實證讀取，而不是基準掃描。它們顯示，當AI能力真正可連接，且協調從問題中產生時，科學推理成為一個分散的、自我修正的過程——這是將AI原生發現擴展到整個星球的一步。

##### **What Makes a Strong Model? A Unified Spectral Analysis of Knowledge Transfer over High-dimensional Linear Regression**
2606.01292v1 by Wendao Wu, Fangqing Zhang, Haihan Zhang, Cong Fang

Teacher-Student Knowledge Transfer (KT) is ubiquitous in modern machine learning, ranging from classical model compression via Knowledge Distillation (KD) to the emergent phenomenon of Weak-to-Strong (W2S) generalization. While existing studies offer isolated insights, a unified theoretical framework explaining the efficacy of KT across these disparate regimes remains lacking. In this work, we establish a unified spectral analysis of SGD dynamics in high-dimensional linear regression, elucidating the efficiency of KT across seemingly disparate regimes. We characterize KT efficiency through two distinct mechanisms: \emph{Spectral Horizon Expansion} in KD, which enables the capture of statistically inaccessible high-frequency signals, and \emph{Spectral Denoising} in W2S, where the student acts as a filter for optimization noise. Our framework unifies these phenomena, revealing that the efficacy of transfer is governed by the interplay between implicit regularization and heterogeneous spectral learning speeds over the spectrum.

摘要：教師-學生知識轉移（KT）在現代機器學習中無處不在，範圍從通過知識蒸餾（KD）進行的經典模型壓縮到弱到強（W2S）泛化的突現現象。雖然現有研究提供了孤立的見解，但仍缺乏一個統一的理論框架來解釋KT在這些不同範疇中的有效性。在這項工作中，我們建立了一個統一的高維線性回歸中SGD動態的譜分析，闡明KT在看似不同範疇中的效率。我們通過兩種不同的機制來描述KT效率：在KD中的\emph{譜視野擴展}，這使得捕捉統計上無法接觸的高頻信號成為可能，以及在W2S中的\emph{譜去噪}，在這裡學生作為優化噪聲的過濾器。我們的框架統一了這些現象，揭示了轉移的有效性受隱式正則化與光譜上異質譜學習速度之間相互作用的影響。

##### **Brain-Atlas-Guided Generative Counterfactual Attention for Explainable Cognitive Decline Diagnosis Using Multimodal Connectomes**
2606.01237v1 by Xiongri Shen, Jiaqi Wang, Zhenxi Song, Yi Zhong, Leilei Zhao, Xin He, Baiying Lei, Zhiguo Zhang

Mild cognitive impairment (MCI) and subjective cognitive decline (SCD) are closely associated with the early Alzheimer's disease continuum, where accurate and explainable diagnosis is important for early risk assessment and intervention. Existing connectome-based deep learning models can improve classification performance but often provide limited insight into disease-related functional and structural connectivity changes. This paper proposes an atlas-knowledge-guided Generative Counterfactual Attention-guided Network (GCAN) for explainable cognitive decline diagnosis using multimodal brain connectomes. GCAN formulates diagnosis as a source-to-target counterfactual generation problem, where target-label connectomes are generated from source-label inputs and their differences are used to construct counterfactual attention maps. To preserve connectome topology, an Atlas-aware Bidirectional Transformer (AABT) performs network-level token encoding and decoding under brain-atlas constraints. The framework is further extended from functional connectivity (FC) to joint functional and structural connectivity (SC) modeling, enabling counterfactual analysis of complementary functional reorganization and structural topology changes. Experiments on hospital-collected and ADNI datasets show that GCAN achieves competitive performance across HC vs. SCD, HC vs. MCI, and SCD vs. MCI classification tasks. Visualization, circular connectome analysis, CAM-based comparison, ablation studies, and confidence interval analysis further support the interpretability and reliability of the proposed framework. Modality-specific FC and SC pre-trained classifiers are used to provide target-state priors for counterfactual generation while being separated from the downstream diagnostic classifier to prevent data leakage.

摘要：輕度認知障礙 (MCI) 和主觀認知衰退 (SCD) 與早期阿茲海默症連續體密切相關，在這裡，準確且可解釋的診斷對於早期風險評估和干預至關重要。現有的基於連接組的深度學習模型可以提高分類性能，但通常對於疾病相關的功能和結構連接變化提供的洞察有限。本文提出了一種基於圖譜知識的生成對比注意力引導網絡 (GCAN)，用於利用多模態大腦連接組進行可解釋的認知衰退診斷。GCAN 將診斷公式化為一個源到目標的對比生成問題，其中目標標籤連接組是從源標籤輸入生成的，並且它們的差異用於構建對比注意力圖。為了保持連接組拓撲，基於圖譜的雙向Transformer (AABT) 在大腦圖譜約束下執行網絡級別的標記編碼和解碼。該框架進一步擴展了從功能連接性 (FC) 到聯合功能和結構連接性 (SC) 建模，實現了對互補功能重組和結構拓撲變化的對比分析。在醫院收集和 ADNI 數據集上的實驗顯示，GCAN 在 HC 對 SCD、HC 對 MCI 和 SCD 對 MCI 的分類任務中達到了競爭性能。可視化、圓形連接組分析、基於 CAM 的比較、消融研究和置信區間分析進一步支持了所提框架的可解釋性和可靠性。特定模態的 FC 和 SC 預訓練分類器用於提供對比生成的目標狀態先驗，同時與下游診斷分類器分開，以防止數據洩漏。

##### **Implicit Geographic Inference in LLM Medical Triage: Language-Driven Disparities in Emergency Recommendations**
2606.01204v1 by Qi Han Wong

We investigate whether large language models produce different medical triage recommendations for identical symptoms based solely on the language of the patient prompt. Using Gemini 3.5 Flash, we evaluate a neurological symptom profile (persistent headache, blurred vision, nausea) across six languages (English, Spanish, Chinese, Hindi, Japanese, Arabic) with 30 runs per condition (n=450 total API calls). We find that the model recommends emergency room visits at rates ranging from 0% (Japanese, Hindi) to 30% (English, Arabic), despite assigning nearly identical severity scores (7.7-8.0/10) across all languages. Adding a single sentence specifying the patient's US location increases ER recommendations by up to 76.7 percentage points for non-English prompts, while the reverse anchor (English prompt with a Tokyo location) reduces the ER rate from 30% to 6.7%. A back-translation control (Japanese to English) produces ER rates comparable to the English baseline, confirming that the disparity is not caused by translation quality but by implicit geographic inference from the input language. We release the complete dataset, experiment code, and results.

摘要：我們調查大型語言模型是否僅基於病人提示的語言，對相同症狀產生不同的醫療分診建議。使用 Gemini 3.5 Flash，我們評估六種語言（英語、西班牙語、中文、印地語、日語、阿拉伯語）中的神經症狀檔案（持續性頭痛、視力模糊、噁心），每種情況進行 30 次運行（總計 n=450 次 API 呼叫）。我們發現，儘管在所有語言中分配了幾乎相同的嚴重性分數（7.7-8.0/10），模型建議的急診室就診率從 0%（日語、印地語）到 30%（英語、阿拉伯語）不等。添加一個指定病人美國位置的單句話，對於非英語提示，急診室建議增加了最多 76.7 個百分點，而反向錨定（帶有東京位置的英語提示）則將急診率從 30% 降至 6.7%。反向翻譯控制（從日語到英語）產生的急診率與英語基準相當，確認差異並非由於翻譯質量造成，而是由於輸入語言的隱性地理推斷。我們發布完整的數據集、實驗代碼和結果。

##### **Trait-space Monitoring for Emergent Misalignment During Supervised Finetuning**
2606.07631v1 by Huy Nghiem, Sy-Tuyen Ho, Sarah Wiegreffe, Hal Daumé

Emergent misalignment (EM) occurs when narrow finetuning causes a model to behave dangerously outside the finetuning task. Standard training signals can miss this shift, making reliable detection costly if it depends on repeated behavioral evaluation. We ask whether emergent misalignment can instead be detected from internal representations during finetuning. Using seven alignment-relevant traits encoded as linear directions in activation space, we track representational drift across training checkpoints in four open-source 7-9B LLMs. EM-relevant drift concentrates on a low-dimensional axis that explains 65.5% of the variance, revealing a geometric signature in the studied regime. A low-overhead monitor built on this drift profile detects dangerous checkpoints with 2.2% false negative rate, 2.9% false positive rate, and 0.990 AUROC on held-out perturbation types, outperforming unsupervised PCA and SAE baselines. Stress tests on two 14B models, longer finetuning runs, and misaligned starting points identify key deployment boundaries. These results position trait-space monitoring as a practical complement to behavioral evaluation for EM detection during LoRA-based finetuning, while showing that deployment across substantially different regimes may require recalibration.

摘要：新興不對齊（EM）發生在狹義微調導致模型在微調任務之外的行為危險時。標準訓練信號可能會錯過這一變化，如果依賴於重複的行為評估，則可靠檢測的成本會很高。我們詢問是否可以從微調過程中的內部表示來檢測新興不對齊。利用七個與對齊相關的特徵，這些特徵在激活空間中編碼為線性方向，我們追踪四個開源7-9B LLMs在訓練檢查點之間的表示漂移。與EM相關的漂移集中在一個低維軸上，解釋了65.5%的方差，揭示了所研究範疇中的幾何特徵。基於這一漂移特徵構建的低開銷監控器以2.2%的假陰性率、2.9%的假陽性率以及0.990的AUROC在保留的擾動類型上檢測危險檢查點，超越了無監督PCA和SAE基準。在兩個14B模型上的壓力測試、更長的微調運行和不對齊的起始點識別了關鍵的部署邊界。這些結果將特徵空間監控定位為在基於LoRA的微調過程中檢測EM的實用補充，同時顯示在顯著不同的範疇之間的部署可能需要重新校準。

##### **Subliminal Learning Is Steering Vector Distillation**
2606.00995v2 by Camila Blank, Agam Bhatia, Senthooran Rajamanoharan, Arthur Conmy, Neel Nanda

Subliminal learning refers to a student language model acquiring a teacher's traits (e.g. a system-prompted preference for owls) when fine-tuned on the teacher's outputs, despite the outputs being semantically unrelated to those traits. It remains poorly understood how data without semantic meaning can transfer specific semantic traits. In this work, we show that subliminal learning is mediated by a single steering vector, i.e. a vector added to the model's activations. Across two open-source models, we find that the teacher's system prompt is well approximated by a steering vector, and that the student's behavior is driven by learning an aligned vector over fine-tuning. System prompts that are not well approximated by steering vectors are not subliminally learned. This is a special case of steering vector distillation, in which a student trained on the outputs of a steered teacher learns to imitate that steering. We demonstrate steering vector distillation on a range of semantic and random vectors. Adding a semantic vector to a model's activations can have both model-independent and model-specific (i.e. non-semantic) effects on its behavior, so generated data that is non-semantic can transmit a vector with semantic effects, enabling subliminal learning. This also explains why subliminal learning does not transfer between models. We find that adaptive optimizers are necessary for subliminal learning in language models: activation gradients on steered data carry a small but consistent component along the steering direction, and non-adaptive optimizers impede this by allowing outlier gradients to dominate.

摘要：潛意識學習是指學生語言模型在微調老師的輸出時，獲得老師的特徵（例如，系統提示對貓頭鷹的偏好），儘管這些輸出在語義上與這些特徵無關。尚不清楚沒有語義意義的數據如何能夠傳遞特定的語義特徵。在這項工作中，我們顯示潛意識學習是由單一的引導向量介導的，即一個添加到模型激活的向量。在兩個開源模型中，我們發現老師的系統提示可以很好地用引導向量來近似，而學生的行為則是通過在微調過程中學習一個對齊向量來驅動的。那些無法被引導向量很好近似的系統提示並不會被潛意識學習到。這是一種引導向量蒸餾的特殊情況，其中在引導老師的輸出上訓練的學生學會模仿該引導。我們在一系列語義和隨機向量上展示了引導向量蒸餾。將語義向量添加到模型的激活中可以對其行為產生模型無關和模型特定（即非語義）的效果，因此生成的非語義數據可以傳遞具有語義效果的向量，從而實現潛意識學習。這也解釋了為什麼潛意識學習不會在模型之間轉移。我們發現自適應優化器對於語言模型中的潛意識學習是必要的：在引導數據上的激活梯度沿著引導方向攜帶一個小但一致的成分，而非自適應優化器則通過允許異常梯度主導來妨礙這一點。

##### **Large Language Models in Transportation Systems Management and Operations: From Text Reasoning to Multi-modal Decision Support**
2606.00991v1 by Siyan Li, Zehao Wang, Jiachen Li, Kanok Boriboonsomsin, Matthew J. Barth, Guoyuan Wu

Transportation systems management and operations (TSMO) increasingly depends on timely interpretation of heterogeneous data, from various sensor streams, incident reports, traveler feedback, and visual observations. Large language models (LLMs), including emerging multi-modal large language models (MM-LLMs), provide a new mechanism for integrating these structured and unstructured inputs into operator-facing decision support. This survey paper reviews LLM- and MM-LLM-based applications in TSMO across three domains: transportation operations & services (supply), mobility & fleet services (demand), and data, modeling & decision support. Using a PRISMA-guided screening process, we synthesize current studies while distinguishing operationally oriented applications from prototype and emerging concepts. We further identify recurring challenges in data heterogeneity, real-time inference, explainability, multi-modal fusion, and governance. Finally, we outline existing gaps and future directions in localized adaptation, edge deployment, benchmarking, and cross-agency collaboration. Overall, LLM-based systems appear most promising as a decision-support layer, with MM-LLMs offering particular value when heterogeneous text, visual, and sensor inputs must be integrated.

摘要：運輸系統管理與運營（TSMO）越來越依賴於對來自各種傳感器流、事件報告、旅行者反饋和視覺觀察的異質數據的及時解釋。大型語言模型（LLMs），包括新興的多模態大型語言模型（MM-LLMs），提供了一種將這些結構化和非結構化輸入整合到面向操作員的決策支持中的新機制。本文調查了基於LLM和MM-LLM的TSMO應用，涵蓋三個領域：運輸運營與服務（供應）、流動性與車隊服務（需求）以及數據、建模與決策支持。通過PRISMA指導的篩選過程，我們綜合了當前的研究，同時區分了以運營為導向的應用與原型和新興概念。我們進一步識別了在數據異質性、實時推斷、可解釋性、多模態融合和治理方面的重複挑戰。最後，我們概述了在本地適應、邊緣部署、基準測試和跨機構合作方面的現有差距和未來方向。總體而言，基於LLM的系統作為決策支持層顯得最有前景，而MM-LLMs在需要整合異質文本、視覺和傳感器輸入時提供了特別的價值。

##### **Explainable deep reinforcement learning reveals energy-efficient control strategies for turbulent drag reduction**
2606.00949v1 by Federica Tonti, Ricardo Vinuesa

We propose a method combining Multi-Agent Deep Reinforcement Learning (MARL) and eXplainable Deep Learning (XDL) to reduce drag in wall-bounded turbulent flows. Taking as a baseline the results of training agents directly targeting wall-shear stress and opposition control, three SHAP-guided approaches are compared. In the first, the reward is computed from SHAP attributions of a U-net predicting the future velocity field; in the second, from SHAP attributions of a U-net predicting the skin-friction coefficient; in the third, from a combination of SHAP attributions of two U-nets predicting the skin-friction coefficient and the wall pressure fluctuations, respectively. The combined SHAP strategy based on skin-friction coefficient and wall-pressure fluctuations achieves the best overall performance, achieving a DR of 34.44% and a NES of 34.01% with only 0.43% normalized input power. Relative to opposition control, drag reduction and net energy saving increase by 49.41% and 48.52%, respectively. Compared with the direct wall-shear-stress baseline, the proposed strategy simultaneously improves performance while reducing the normalized actuation cost from 5.90% to 0.43%. Analysis of the results reveals that the energetically efficient policy is consistent with pressure-gated actuation, activating predominantly at near-zero wall pressure, and operates on a temporal timescale comparable to the lifetime of the near-wall turbulent structures.

摘要：我們提出了一種結合多智能體深度強化學習（MARL）和可解釋深度學習（XDL）的方法，以減少壁面約束的湍流流動中的阻力。以直接針對壁面剪切應力和對抗控制的訓練結果為基準，對三種基於SHAP的引導方法進行比較。在第一種方法中，獎勵是根據預測未來速度場的U-net的SHAP歸因計算的；在第二種方法中，獎勵來自預測皮膚摩擦係數的U-net的SHAP歸因；在第三種方法中，獎勵來自兩個U-net的SHAP歸因的組合，分別預測皮膚摩擦係數和壁面壓力波動。基於皮膚摩擦係數和壁面壓力波動的綜合SHAP策略實現了最佳的整體性能，達到34.44%的阻力減少率（DR）和34.01%的淨能量節省（NES），而僅需0.43%的歸一化輸入功率。相對於對抗控制，阻力減少和淨能量節省分別增加了49.41%和48.52%。與直接的壁面剪切應力基準相比，所提出的策略同時改善了性能，同時將歸一化驅動成本從5.90%降低至0.43%。結果分析顯示，能量高效的策略與壓力閥驅動一致，主要在接近零壁面壓力時啟動，並在與近壁湍流結構的壽命相當的時間尺度上運作。

##### **Interaction-Centered Intelligence: Toward Interaction as the Primary Unit of Analysis in Co-Creative AI and Human-AI Systems**
2606.00807v1 by Nicholas Davis

Traditional artificial intelligence has largely conceptualized intelligence as isolated computation occurring within bounded agents. Across classical AI, machine learning, and many generative systems, the dominant unit of analysis remains the individual model or autonomous system evaluated through outputs, benchmarks, prediction accuracy, or optimization performance. While these approaches have produced major advances, they often under-theorize the role of interaction in the emergence of intelligence, creativity, meaning, and adaptive behavior. This paper proposes interaction as the primary unit of analysis for co-creative AI and interaction-centered intelligence more broadly. Drawing from distributed cognition, embodied cognition, enaction, participatory sense-making, human-computer interaction, and computational creativity, the paper traces a historical progression toward increasingly relational accounts of intelligence. Building upon prior work in Creative Sense-Making, quantified co-creation, and co-creative systems such as the Drawing Apprentice and AI Drawing Partner, it argues that intelligence emerges through evolving interaction dynamics among agents, environments, and socio-technical systems rather than solely through internal computation. The paper introduces Interaction-Centered Intelligence as a framework for understanding human-AI co-creation, collaborative emergence, adaptive participation, and interactional dynamics. Rather than evaluating intelligence solely through generated outputs, the framework emphasizes interaction trajectories, coordination patterns, participatory engagement, adaptive regulation, and interactional drift unfolding through time. Implications for explainable co-creative AI, hybrid intelligence, enactive AI, and future human-AI systems are discussed.

摘要：傳統人工智慧在很大程度上將智慧概念化為在有限代理內部發生的孤立計算。在經典人工智慧、機器學習以及許多生成系統中，主導的分析單位仍然是個別模型或通過輸出、基準、預測準確性或優化性能進行評估的自主系統。雖然這些方法已經帶來了重大的進展，但它們往往對互動在智慧、創造力、意義和適應性行為的出現中的角色理論不足。本文提出將互動作為共創人工智慧和更廣泛的以互動為中心的智慧的主要分析單位。本文借鑒了分布式認知、具身認知、行動、參與式意義建構、人機互動和計算創造力，追溯了向日益關係化的智慧解釋的歷史進程。基於在創意意義建構、量化共創以及如繪圖學徒和人工智慧繪圖夥伴等共創系統的先前研究，本文主張智慧是通過代理、環境和社會技術系統之間不斷演變的互動動態而非僅僅通過內部計算而出現的。本文引入以互動為中心的智慧作為理解人類與人工智慧共創、協作出現、適應性參與和互動動態的框架。該框架強調互動軌跡、協調模式、參與性參與、適應性調節和隨時間展開的互動漂移，而不是僅僅通過生成的輸出來評估智慧。本文討論了對可解釋的共創人工智慧、混合智慧、行動人工智慧和未來人類與人工智慧系統的影響。

##### **Wavelet as Tokenizer: Preliminary Results on a Shared Wavelet Token Schema for Natural Signals**
2606.02631v1 by Shenghao Ding

This paper studies whether audio, images, and video can share a common wavelet token schema rather than relying on separate modality-specific latent grids. It introduces a preliminary continuous-token model built around a one-level Haar DWT/IDWT frontend, a shared coefficient-token layout, optional structural metadata, lightweight modality value adapters, and a shared token-wise encoder-decoder trunk. On Speech Commands, EuroSAT RGB, and DAVIS 2017 data, a dense shared model reaches 39.92 dB audio, 29.37 dB image, and 23.93 dB video PSNR. A matched-rate sweep under continuous latent scalar budgets indicates that the visual gains are not explained solely by latent capacity, while also showing that additive metadata embeddings are not a universal source of improvement. Finally, fixed-rate energy selection provides a strong non-parametric baseline: energy_global improves average PSNR over uniform selection by 16.73 dB for audio, 16.90 dB for images, and 15.86 dB for video under compressed keep ratios. Masked sparse training reaches 34.45 dB video PSNR with 50% of dense tokens. The results support a unified wavelet token schema and sparse token interface, while stopping short of establishing a universal discrete vocabulary.

摘要：這篇論文研究音頻、圖像和視頻是否可以共享一個共同的小波令牌架構，而不是依賴於單獨的特定於模態的潛在網格。<lb/>它介紹了一個初步的連續令牌模型，該模型圍繞一級Haar DWT/IDWT前端、共享的係數令牌佈局、可選的結構元數據、輕量級的模態值適配器以及共享的令牌編碼-解碼主幹構建。<lb/>在Speech Commands、EuroSAT RGB和DAVIS 2017數據上，一個密集共享模型達到了39.92 dB音頻、29.37 dB圖像和23.93 dB視頻PSNR。<lb/>在連續潛在標量預算下的匹配速率掃描表明，視覺增益並不僅僅是由潛在容量解釋的，同時也顯示附加的元數據嵌入並不是一個普遍的改進來源。<lb/>最後，固定速率能量選擇提供了一個強大的非參數基準：在壓縮保持比下，energy_global使音頻的平均PSNR比均勻選擇提高了16.73 dB，圖像提高了16.90 dB，視頻提高了15.86 dB。<lb/>掩碼稀疏訓練在50%的密集令牌下達到了34.45 dB視頻PSNR。<lb/>這些結果支持一個統一的小波令牌架構和稀疏令牌接口，同時未能建立一個普遍的離散詞彙。

##### **The Paradox of Outcome Optimization: A Causal Information-Theoretic Bound on Reasoning Shortcuts in LLMs**
2606.00674v1 by Zihan Chen, Yiming Zhang, Wenxiang Geng, Zenghui Ding, Yining Sun

Large Language Models (LLMs) aligned via outcome-based Reinforcement Learning (RL) frequently exhibit a critical failure mode: they achieve high performance on in-distribution benchmarks while demonstrating brittle reasoning capabilities on out-of-distribution (OOD) tasks. We term this phenomenon Reward-Induced Manifold Collapse. We establish a theoretical framework bridging Structural Causal Models (SCM) and the Information Bottleneck (IB) principle to explain this paradox. We define reasoning as a high-complexity causal process and shortcut learning as the exploitation of low-complexity spurious correlations. Under the implicit inductive bias of Stochastic Gradient Descent (SGD), models optimized for outcome rewards are biased toward shortcut solutions whenever the training distribution allows for a ``Markovian Screening'' of the true causal mechanism. We derive a new generalization bound based on Semantic Coverage Measure ($η$) rather than sample size, showing why data scaling on homogeneous distributions may fail to correct reasoning flaws. We also show that Process Reward Models (PRMs) function as Topological Filters, enforcing step-wise mutual information constraints that render the low-complexity shortcut manifold inadmissible. These results provide a mathematical grounding for the role of process supervision beyond simple credit assignment.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）透過基於結果的強化學習（RL）進行對齊時，經常顯示出一種關鍵的失效模式：它們在內部分佈基準上表現出高效能，但在外部分佈（OOD）任務上卻展現出脆弱的推理能力。我們將這一現象稱為獎勵誘導的流形崩潰。我們建立了一個理論框架，將結構因果模型（SCM）與信息瓶頸（IB）原則聯繫起來，以解釋這一悖論。我們將推理定義為一個高複雜度的因果過程，而捷徑學習則被定義為利用低複雜度的虛假相關性。在隨機梯度下降（SGD）的隱性歸納偏見下，為結果獎勵而優化的模型在訓練分佈允許對真實因果機制進行“馬爾可夫篩選”的情況下，會偏向捷徑解決方案。我們基於語義覆蓋度量（$η$）而非樣本大小推導出一個新的泛化界限，顯示為何在同質分佈上的數據擴展可能無法修正推理缺陷。我們還展示了過程獎勵模型（PRMs）作為拓撲過濾器的功能，強制執行逐步的互信息約束，使低複雜度的捷徑流形不可接受。這些結果為過程監督在簡單的信用分配之外的角色提供了數學基礎。

##### **MultiTurnPSB: Evaluating Multi-Turn Jailbreak Attacks an dClassifier-Based Defenses for Medical AI Safety**
2606.02630v1 by Anushka Sheoran, Yiduo Hao

Patient-facing medical chatbots are commonly evaluated on single-turn prompts, yet real users push back after refusals, add urgency, and invoke authority. We introduce MultiTurnPSB, a four-turn adversarial extension of PatientSafetyBench, and evaluate GPT-4.1-mini under fixed template, template-adaptive, and live adversarial attacks. Unsafe responses rise from 35% to nearly 80% by Turn 4 under live attack. Under the same adversary, GPT-4.1-mini and Claude Sonnet 4.5 are statistically indistinguishable at baseline but diverge to a 19x gap by Turn 4, a difference invisible to single-turn evaluation. We characterize four degradation trajectory signatures and identify a two-element attack formula responsible for most catastrophic failures. A lightweight input-side classifier reduces Turn 4 unsafe responses by 52 percentage points despite severe accuracy degradation, but the 45% false alarm rate on benign queries is the primary deployment constraint. A methodological finding also emerges: Claude Sonnet refused to generate adversarial messages in over half of late-turn conversations despite explicit red team framing, suggesting safety training may generalize to the attacker role.

摘要：病人面對的醫療聊天機器人通常在單輪提示下進行評估，然而實際用戶在拒絕後會反擊、增加緊迫感並引用權威。我們介紹了 MultiTurnPSB，這是一個四輪對抗擴展的 PatientSafetyBench，並在固定模板、模板自適應和實時對抗攻擊下評估 GPT-4.1-mini。在實時攻擊下，不安全的回應從第 4 輪的 35% 上升到接近 80%。在相同的對手下，GPT-4.1-mini 和 Claude Sonnet 4.5 在基線上統計上無法區分，但在第 4 輪時卻擴大到 19 倍的差距，這一差異在單輪評估中是不可見的。我們特徵化了四種降級軌跡特徵，並確定了一個負責大多數災難性失敗的兩元素攻擊公式。一個輕量級的輸入端分類器儘管準確性嚴重下降，仍能將第 4 輪不安全回應減少 52 個百分點，但在良性查詢上的 45% 假警報率是主要的部署限制。一個方法論的發現也浮現出來：儘管有明確的紅隊框架，Claude Sonnet 在超過一半的晚輪對話中拒絕生成對抗消息，這表明安全訓練可能會泛化到攻擊者角色。

##### **Revisiting Parameter-Based Knowledge Editing in Large Language Models: Theoretical Limits and Empirical Evidence**
2606.00570v1 by Wanying Ren, Xin Song, Futing Wang, Guoxiu He, Aixin Sun

Parameter-based knowledge editing updates the internal knowledge of large language models (LLMs) via localized weight modifications and has attracted significant attention. However, most existing methods overlook fundamental theoretical limitations and are rarely evaluated under realistic, practice-oriented settings. In this paper, we first present a theoretical analysis based on the dimensional Collapse Hypothesis, explaining how localized parameter edits can propagate along fragile directions in the representation space, inducing global interference and ultimately causing reasoning collapse. Building on this insight, we conduct a comprehensive empirical evaluation by systematically varying knowledge complexity, number of edits, evaluation dimensions, and baseline methods. Our results show that parameter-based editing methods consistently damage core LLM capabilities. In contrast, a simple retrieval-based baseline achieves consistently stronger performance than all parameter-editing methods across all evaluated conditions. These findings highlight that preserving the fundamental capabilities of LLMs after knowledge editing should be a central concern for future research.

摘要：參數基礎的知識編輯透過局部權重修改更新大型語言模型（LLMs）的內部知識，並引起了相當大的關注。<lb/>然而，大多數現有方法忽略了基本的理論限制，並且很少在現實的、實踐導向的環境下進行評估。<lb/>在本文中，我們首先基於維度崩潰假說進行理論分析，解釋了局部參數編輯如何在表示空間中沿著脆弱的方向傳播，導致全球干擾並最終造成推理崩潰。<lb/>基於這一見解，我們通過系統地變化知識複雜性、編輯數量、評估維度和基準方法，進行了全面的實證評估。<lb/>我們的結果顯示，基於參數的編輯方法持續損害核心 LLM 能力。<lb/>相對而言，一個簡單的基於檢索的基準在所有評估條件下的表現始終優於所有參數編輯方法。<lb/>這些發現突顯了在知識編輯後保持 LLM 的基本能力應該是未來研究的核心關注點。

##### **CAFOSat: A Strongly Annotated Dataset for Infrastructure-Aware CAFO Mapping Using High-Resolution Imagery**
2606.00548v1 by Oishee Bintey Hoque, Nibir Chandra Mandal, Mandy L Wilson, Samarth Swarup, Madhav Marathe, Abhijin Adiga

Concentrated Animal Feeding Operations (CAFOs) play an important role in agricultural production but are also associated with environmental, public health, and disease surveillance concerns. Large-scale mapping of CAFOs from remote sensing imagery remains challenging due to heterogeneous infrastructure layouts, noisy location records, inconsistent annotations, and incomplete inventories. We introduce CAFOSat, a strongly annotated, infrastructure-aware dataset for CAFO mapping across the United States. CAFOSat integrates high-resolution National Agriculture Imagery Program (NAIP) imagery with multi-source CAFO inventories collected across multiple states and transforms weak geolocation records into refined annotations through a human-in-the-loop pipeline combining AI-assisted annotation, GradCAM-based localization, and geometric clustering. To improve dataset quality, we curate challenging negative samples using land-cover-guided sampling with spatial exclusion constraints and provide infrastructure-level annotations, including barns, manure ponds, and grazing-related features, through manual verification. The resulting dataset contains more than 45,000 image patches spanning 20 states and four major CAFO categories. We benchmark a diverse set of convolutional, transformer-based, and vision-language models, demonstrating the value of refined annotations and curated negative samples for CAFO classification and generalization. In addition, we introduce a synthetic augmentation pipeline that generates infrastructure-aware variations to increase training diversity and improve robustness under distribution shifts. CAFOSat provides a large-scale benchmark for advancing infrastructure-aware agricultural monitoring and CAFO mapping from high-resolution remote sensing imagery.

摘要：集中動物飼養作業（CAFOs）在農業生產中扮演著重要角色，但也與環境、公共健康和疾病監測問題相關聯。由於基礎設施佈局異質、位置記錄噪音、註釋不一致以及清單不完整，從遙感影像進行CAFO的大規模映射仍然具有挑戰性。我們介紹了CAFOSat，一個強標註的、關注基礎設施的CAFO映射數據集，涵蓋美國各地。CAFOSat整合了高解析度的國家農業影像計畫（NAIP）影像與來自多個州的多源CAFO清單，並通過一個人機協作的流程將弱地理位置記錄轉換為精細的註釋，該流程結合了AI輔助註釋、基於GradCAM的定位和幾何聚類。為了提高數據集質量，我們使用土地覆蓋引導的取樣方法，結合空間排除約束，策劃了具有挑戰性的負樣本，並通過人工驗證提供包括穀倉、糞便池和與放牧相關特徵的基礎設施級註釋。最終生成的數據集包含超過45,000個影像片段，涵蓋20個州和四個主要CAFO類別。我們基準測試了一組多樣的卷積、基於Transformer的和視覺-語言模型，展示了精細註釋和策劃負樣本在CAFO分類和泛化中的價值。此外，我們介紹了一個合成增強流程，生成關注基礎設施的變體，以增加訓練多樣性並提高在分佈變化下的穩健性。CAFOSat為推進基礎設施關注的農業監測和基於高解析度遙感影像的CAFO映射提供了一個大規模基準。

##### **Evaluating Bivariate Causal Statements Based on Mutual Compatibility**
2606.00278v1 by Erik Jahn, Dominik Janzing

For many real-world systems, causal ground truth is difficult to obtain, making claims about causal effects hard to assess. We develop methods for evaluating collections of $\binom{n}{2}$ bivariate causal statements over a set of $n$ variables. In the setting of acyclic linear statements, any such collection can be extended to a unique multivariate causal model, but we argue that this induced model is implausible if it imposes substantial additional confounding to explain observed correlations. We introduce a compatibility score that quantifies this notion of plausibility, notably without relying on the faithfulness assumption. Additionally, we define an incompatibility score for purely graphical bivariate causal statements, based on global consistency constraints that are derived from acyclicity and faithfulness assumptions. We give theoretical and empirical evidence that both scores can successfully distinguish correct from incorrect causal statements in generic settings. Moreover, we demonstrate the practical applicability of our methods by analyzing causal claims made by large language models. Our work aims to provide a foundation for assessing the reliability of causal information derived from human experts or artificial intelligence in settings where alternative forms of validation are unavailable.

摘要：對於許多現實世界的系統，因果真相難以獲得，使得對因果效應的主張難以評估。<lb/>我們開發了評估 $\binom{n}{2}$ 個雙變量因果陳述的方法，這些陳述涉及一組 $n$ 個變量。<lb/>在無循環線性陳述的背景下，任何這樣的集合都可以擴展為一個唯一的多變量因果模型，但我們認為，如果這個誘導模型施加了實質性的額外混淆來解釋觀察到的相關性，那麼這是不可行的。<lb/>我們引入了一個兼容性分數，量化這種可行性的概念，特別是無需依賴忠實性假設。<lb/>此外，我們為純圖形的雙變量因果陳述定義了一個不兼容性分數，該分數基於從無循環性和忠實性假設中推導出的全局一致性約束。<lb/>我們提供了理論和實證證據，表明這兩個分數能夠在通用環境中成功區分正確和不正確的因果陳述。<lb/>此外，我們通過分析大型語言模型所做的因果主張，展示了我們方法的實際應用性。<lb/>我們的工作旨在為評估從人類專家或人工智能中獲得的因果信息的可靠性提供基礎，特別是在無法使用其他驗證形式的情況下。

##### **Fine-grained Verification via Diagnostic Reasoning Supervision for Aspect Sentiment Triplet Extraction**
2605.31446v1 by Wenna Lai, Haoran Xie, Guandong Xu, Qing Li, S. Joe Qin

Aspect Sentiment Triplet Extraction (ASTE) aims to identify aspect terms, opinion terms, and sentiment polarities as structured triplets, providing essential inputs for downstream information system applications such as opinion mining, explainable recommendations, and review summarization. Prior work mainly focuses on end-to-end extraction, while post hoc verification of extracted triplets remains comparatively underexplored. This gap limits the reliability of ASTE systems, since predicted triplets may be locally plausible while being globally invalid. Moreover, candidate invalidity is multi-faceted and candidate usability is inherently graded, motivating a fine-grained verification mechanism that can filter or re-rank outputs from diverse extractors. In this paper, we propose FiVeD, a framework for Fine-grained Verification with Diagnostic reasoning supervision. Specifically, the verifier is trained with multiple complementary objectives, including validity classification and quality score estimation as primary tasks, with error type classification and rationale generation as auxiliary tasks. We define hierarchical error categories and construct plausible incorrect triplets under semantic and syntactic constraints, and leverage an off-the-shelf LLM with task-specific rubrics to produce quality scores and diagnostic rationales. During inference, the resulting quality scores are used to filter candidate outputs, supporting adjustable precision-recall tradeoffs. Experiments across multiple ASTE baselines demonstrate that FiVeD consistently improves extraction performance by up to 3.53 F1 points as a plug-and-play verification module.

摘要：方面情感三元組提取（ASTE）旨在識別方面術語、意見術語和情感極性作為結構化的三元組，為下游信息系統應用提供必要的輸入，如意見挖掘、可解釋的推薦和評論摘要。之前的工作主要集中在端到端提取，而對提取三元組的事後驗證則相對未被充分探索。這一差距限制了ASTE系統的可靠性，因為預測的三元組可能在局部上是合理的，但在全局上卻無效。此外，候選無效性是多方面的，候選可用性本質上是分級的，這促使我們需要一種細粒度的驗證機制，能夠過濾或重新排序來自不同提取器的輸出。在本文中，我們提出了FiVeD，一個細粒度驗證框架，具有診斷推理監督。具體而言，驗證器是通過多個互補目標進行訓練的，包括有效性分類和質量評分估計作為主要任務，錯誤類型分類和推理生成作為輔助任務。我們定義了分層錯誤類別，並在語義和語法約束下構建合理的錯誤三元組，並利用現成的LLM和特定任務的評分標準來產生質量評分和診斷推理。在推理過程中，生成的質量評分用於過濾候選輸出，支持可調的精確度-召回權衡。在多個ASTE基準上的實驗表明，FiVeD作為即插即用的驗證模塊，始終能將提取性能提高最多3.53個F1點。

##### **FAM-Bench: A Multimodal Benchmark for Condition-Aware Food-as-Medicine Reasoning**
2605.31410v1 by Mingyang Mao, Bhargav Rishi Medisetti, Utkarsh Grover, Tanvir Ibrahim, Wenyan Li, Tingting Zhang, Xiaomin Lin

Food-as-Medicine requires models to reason beyond what a dish is or what nutrition it contains: they must decide whether a concrete food choice is appropriate for a specific health condition. Existing food AI benchmarks primarily evaluate dish recognition, recipe understanding, nutrient estimation, or general nutrition question answering, leaving this health-aware decision layer largely untested. We introduce FAM-Bench, a multi-modal Food-as-Medicine benchmark with 2500 nutrition-expert-verified instances across 13 diet-related health conditions. The benchmark contains two complementary tasks: dish-level suitability assessment, where models judge whether a dish is suitable for a condition from its image and ingredient list, and comparative dish analysis, where models rank four candidate dishes by condition-specific suitability. Both tasks require integrating ingredient evidence, visual preparation cues, and clinical nutrition constraints, providing a standardized testbed for grounded health-aware reasoning in language and vision-language models.

##### **HypoAgent: An Agentic Framework for Interactive Abductive Hypothesis Generation over Knowledge Graphs**
2605.31370v1 by Yisen Gao, Yixi Cai, Tianshi Zheng, Jiaxin Bai, Yangqiu Song

Abductive reasoning over knowledge graphs aims to generate logical hypotheses that explain observed entities or facts. Existing controllable hypothesis generation methods allow users to guide this process with explicit conditions, but they remain limited in interactive settings: they struggle to ground evolving natural-language intents across multi-turn dialogues and provide little fine-grained diagnosis when generated hypotheses fail. To address these limitations, we propose HypoAgent, an Agentic framework for interactive abductive Hypothesis Generation over knowledge graphs. HypoAgent integrates three agents: an Intent Recognition Agent that grounds user utterances and dialogue history into executable KG conditions, a Hypothesis Generation Agent that performs controllable hypothesis generation according to the extracted user intention, and a Root Cause Analysis Agent that diagnoses unreliable hypothesis fragments and leverages KG neighborhood probing to identify supported refinements. Experiments on commonsense and biomedical domain-specific knowledge graphs demonstrate that HypoAgent achieves state-of-the-art semantic similarity under single-turn, multi-turn, and unconditional settings. Our code is available at https://github.com/HKUST-KnowComp/HypoAgent.

摘要：推理知識圖譜的歸納推理旨在生成解釋觀察到的實體或事實的邏輯假設。現有的可控假設生成方法允許用戶用明確的條件來指導這一過程，但在互動環境中仍然有限：它們難以在多輪對話中將不斷演變的自然語言意圖具體化，並且在生成的假設失敗時提供的細緻診斷也很少。為了解決這些限制，我們提出了HypoAgent，一個針對知識圖譜的互動歸納假設生成的代理框架。HypoAgent整合了三個代理：一個意圖識別代理，將用戶的話語和對話歷史轉化為可執行的KG條件；一個假設生成代理，根據提取的用戶意圖執行可控的假設生成；以及一個根本原因分析代理，診斷不可靠的假設片段，並利用KG鄰域探測來識別支持的細化。對常識和生物醫學領域特定知識圖譜的實驗表明，HypoAgent在單輪、多輪和無條件設置下達到了最先進的語義相似度。我們的代碼可在https://github.com/HKUST-KnowComp/HypoAgent獲得。

##### **dashi: A Python library for Dataset Shift Characterization to Support Trustworthy AI Development and Deployment**
2605.31360v1 by David Fernández-Narro, Pablo Ferri, Ángel Sánchez-García, Juan M. García-Gómez, Carlos Sáez

The Artificial Intelligence (AI) life cycle requires a thorough understanding of the underlying data dynamics for robust, safe and cost-effective AI development and use. Dataset shifts are defined as changes between train and test data distributions. Whether occurring over time (temporal) or across different sites (multi-source), they can severely degrade model performance and compromise data quality. This is particularly important in health AI, where the safety and fundamental rights of patients can be severely affected by uncontrolled shifts both at training and operational stages. While the theoretical foundations of covariate, prior, and concept shifts are well established, there is a lack of accessible and comprehensive software tools to perform their analysis. We introduce dashi, an open-source Python library designed for the exploration, quantification, and characterization of dataset shifts. dashi provides a dual approach: an unsupervised approach that leverages information geometry and non-parametric statistical manifolds to data variability characterization and analysis (e.g., Information Geometric Temporal plots and Multi-Source Variability metrics like Global Probabilistic Deviation and Source Probabilistic Outlyingness), and a supervised approach that quantifies and characterizes model performance degradation. Both unsupervised and supervised approaches work across user-defined temporal and domain/source batches. We demonstrate the utility of dashi on three simulated and real-world health AI case studies on gestational diabetes mellitus, COVID-19 and emergency medical dispatch. By providing interactive visual analytics and variability metrics, dashi supports trustworthiness of AI life cycle stages enabling robust and safe machine learning pipelines through the assessment of data coherence and AI performance.

摘要：人工智慧（AI）生命週期需要對基礎數據動態有透徹的理解，以實現穩健、安全和具成本效益的AI開發和使用。數據集轉變被定義為訓練和測試數據分佈之間的變化。無論是隨時間發生（時間性）還是跨不同地點（多來源），它們都可能嚴重降低模型性能並影響數據質量。這在健康AI中尤為重要，因為患者的安全和基本權利可能會受到訓練和運行階段的無法控制的轉變的嚴重影響。儘管協變數、先驗和概念轉變的理論基礎已經建立，但缺乏可訪問和全面的軟體工具來進行其分析。我們介紹了dashi，一個開源的Python庫，旨在探索、量化和特徵化數據集轉變。dashi提供了雙重方法：一種無監督的方法，利用信息幾何和非參數統計流形來進行數據變異性的特徵化和分析（例如，信息幾何時間圖和多來源變異性指標，如全局概率偏差和來源概率異常性），以及一種監督的方法，量化和特徵化模型性能下降。無論是無監督還是監督的方法，都可以在用戶定義的時間和領域/來源批次中運作。我們在三個模擬和真實世界的健康AI案例研究中展示了dashi的實用性，這些案例涉及妊娠糖尿病、COVID-19和緊急醫療調度。通過提供互動式視覺分析和變異性指標，dashi支持AI生命週期階段的可信度，通過評估數據一致性和AI性能來實現穩健和安全的機器學習管道。

##### **Gradient Descent with Large Step Size Restores Symmetry in Deep Linear Networks with Multi-Pathway**
2606.05219v1 by Hee-Sung Kim, Sungyoon Lee

Recent analyses of multi-pathway Deep Linear Networks use Gradient Flow to predict a "winner-takes-all" specialization in which path symmetry breaks and each feature concentrates in a single pathway. In this work, we show that discrete Gradient Descent (GD) with a large step size tells a different story. We prove that single-path solutions are sharp minima, whereas distributing signals across pathways reduces sharpness by a factor that decreases with both the number of pathways and depth. Consequently, while early training reproduces the depth-driven symmetry breaking predicted by GF, oscillations at the Edge of Stability subsequently override this tendency and drive the network into a re-balancing phase, where signals redistribute across pathways. Together, these results clarify how depth shapes pathway competition and explain why large-step GD favors shared representations rather than persistent single-pathway dominance.

摘要：最近對多路徑深度線性網絡的分析使用梯度流來預測一種「贏者通吃」的專業化，其中路徑對稱性破裂，每個特徵集中在單一路徑上。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們展示了具有大步長的離散梯度下降（GD）則講述了另一個故事。<lb/>我們證明了單路徑解是尖銳的最小值，而在路徑之間分配信號則會降低尖銳度，這一降低的因素隨著路徑數量和深度的增加而減少。<lb/>因此，雖然早期訓練再現了GF預測的深度驅動對稱破裂，但穩定邊緣的振盪隨後超越了這一趨勢，並將網絡推入重新平衡的階段，在這一階段中，信號在路徑之間重新分配。<lb/>綜合這些結果，澄清了深度如何塑造路徑競爭，並解釋了為什麼大步長的GD更傾向於共享表示，而不是持續的單一路徑主導。

##### **Entropic Projection Alignment: Estimating, Explaining, and Improving Model Performance Under Distribution Shift**
2605.31250v1 by Salim I. Amoukou, Emanuele Albini, Tom Bewley, Saumitra Mishra, Manuela Veloso

We propose a unified framework for addressing three key challenges of distribution shift: (1) estimating a model's performance on an unlabeled target domain, (2) explaining the shift by identifying the features responsible, and (3) improving the target domain performance. Our method, Entropic Projection Alignment (EPA), aligns the source distribution to the target by matching carefully selected moments while simultaneously minimising the KL divergence from the source. This formulation yields a unique closed-form solution for importance weights, achieving robustness through implicit variance control. Drawing on domain adaptation theory, we establish that moment matching is sufficient for reliable estimation and adaptation, avoiding the need for full density ratio recovery. Extensive experiments, together with strong theoretical guarantees, demonstrate that EPA consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines while offering substantial computational efficiency.

摘要：我們提出了一個統一框架，以解決分佈轉移的三個關鍵挑戰：<lb/>（1）估計模型在未標記目標領域上的性能，<lb/>（2）通過識別負責的特徵來解釋轉移，<lb/>（3）改善目標領域的性能。<lb/>我們的方法，熵投影對齊（EPA），通過匹配精心選擇的矩來將源分佈對齊到目標，同時最小化來自源的KL散度。<lb/>這一公式為重要性權重提供了一個獨特的封閉形式解，通過隱式方差控制實現了穩健性。<lb/>基於領域適應理論，我們建立了矩匹配對於可靠估計和適應是足夠的，避免了對全密度比恢復的需求。<lb/>大量實驗以及強有力的理論保證表明，EPA在計算效率上提供了顯著的優勢，並且始終超越了最先進的基準。

##### **Developing a Culturally Grounded, AI-Augmented UX Research Point of View (POV): An Exemplar Case Study from Telemedicine Dementia Care**
2605.31147v1 by Abiodun Adedeji, Huseyin Dogan, Festus Adedoyin, Michelle Heward, Melike Akca, Emmanuel Oluwatosin Oluokun, Fatima Ahmad Muhazu, Olumuyiwa Ayorinde

User Experience Research (UXR) Points of View (POVs) distil complex and often fragmented research evidence into actionable perspectives that guide how teams interpret user needs, frame design decisions, and align stakeholders. Although POVs are widely used in industry practice, there are few published examples that explicitly document how POVs are constructed, particularly in culturally sensitive and low-resource contexts. This paper presents an exemplar case study demonstrating how a culturally grounded, AI-augmented UXR POV was developed to inform TeleDeCa, a telemedicine dementia care framework for family caregivers in Nigeria. Building on the UXR POV Playbook and pyramid framework, we illustrate how mixed-methods research, hypothesis generation, and ontology-based modelling can be combined to form a defensible POV without requiring a fully finalised system or validated outcomes. 摘要：使用者體驗研究 (UXR) 的觀點 (POVs) 將複雜且經常支離破碎的研究證據提煉成可行的視角，指導團隊如何解釋使用者需求、框定設計決策以及對齊利益相關者。雖然POVs在行業實踐中被廣泛使用，但公開的範例很少，特別是在文化敏感和資源匱乏的情境中，明確記錄POVs的構建過程。本文呈現了一個範例案例研究，展示如何開發一個文化根植的、人工智慧增強的UXR POV，以指導TeleDeCa，這是一個為尼日利亞家庭照顧者提供的遠程醫療癡呆症護理框架。在UXR POV手冊和金字塔框架的基礎上，我們說明了如何將混合方法研究、假設生成和基於本體的建模結合起來，形成一個可辯護的POV，而不需要完全最終化的系統或驗證的結果。生成性人工智慧 (GenAI) 被整合到UXR POV框架中，作為一個有限的研究合作者，支持綜合、假設探索和敘事構建，同時保留人類判斷、倫理責任和文化敏感性。本文的貢獻在於提取可重用的遊戲卡片和一個遊戲，擴展了UXR POV手冊，並作為CHI 2026研討會上開發AI驅動的UXR POV的範例材料。

##### **The Shape of Addition: Geometric Structures of Arithmetic in Large Language Models**
2606.03645v1 by Liuyuan Wen, Xun Zhu, Lihao Huang, Wenbin Li, Yang Gao

Large Language Models exhibit paradoxical fragility in fundamental arithmetic, implying a disconnect between internal computation and discrete output. By analyzing the residual stream geometry during multi-operand addition, we identify the Iso-Raw-Sum Trajectory (IRST), a geometric structure where representations are anchored by semantic digits and modulated by continuous carry fibers. We propose the Noisy Quantization Model to explain this geometry, framing arithmetic errors as Geometric Slippages caused by internal neural noise pushing a continuous, latent Carry Potential across quantization thresholds. This geometric framework further elucidates Probe Versatility, explaining how lightweight probes can disentangle coexisting latent signals (such as ground truth versus hallucination) from a single activation vector. Finally, we validate these insights through a geometric consistency check method that effectively detects and corrects these quantization failures during inference. Our code is available at https://github.com/RL-MIND/Shape-of-Addition.

摘要：大型語言模型在基本算術上表現出矛盾的脆弱性，這暗示了內部計算與離散輸出之間的脫節。<lb/>通過分析多操作數加法過程中的殘差流幾何，我們識別出同位原始和總軌跡（IRST），這是一種幾何結構，其中表示由語義數字錨定，並由連續進位纖維調制。<lb/>我們提出了噪聲量化模型來解釋這種幾何，將算術錯誤框定為由內部神經噪聲推動的幾何滑移，這種噪聲使得連續的潛在進位潛力跨越量化閾值。<lb/>這一幾何框架進一步闡明了探測器的多功能性，解釋了輕量級探測器如何能夠從單一激活向量中解開共存的潛在信號（例如真實值與幻覺）。<lb/>最後，我們通過幾何一致性檢查方法驗證了這些見解，該方法有效地檢測和修正了推理過程中的量化失敗。<lb/>我們的代碼可在 https://github.com/RL-MIND/Shape-of-Addition 獲得。

##### **Developing an AI-Powered UX Research Point of View for Digital Health in A Regulatory Context: An Exemplar Case from MSM and Transgender HIV Care in Nigeria**
