##### **Learning to Solve and Optimize by Evolving Code**
2605.31049v1 by Veronika Semmelrock, Benedetta Strizzolo, Francesco Zuccato, Gerhard Friedrich, Patrick Rodler, Konstantin Schekotihin

Combinatorial and optimization problems are fundamental to many industrial AI applications. Solving large-scale real-world instances of such problems typically requires careful problem formalization, specialized solvers, and expert-designed heuristics. Thus, experts need to specify not only what solutions are, but also how they are derived. By introducing the tool CHECKMATE, we show that algorithm generation via code evolution represents a paradigm shift by eliminating the need to formulate the how. CHECKMATE solely relies on the what. Specifically, a formal specification ensures solutions' correctness and enables systematic performance evaluation of the generated programs, while a natural language description guides the evolutionary process. The effectiveness of our method is demonstrated on selected problems from two industrial domains: configuration and scheduling. In all cases, the evolved algorithms consistently outperform state-of-the-art solvers. This underscores the potential of formal methods in guiding code evolution for automatically solving complex real-world problems.

摘要：組合和優化問題對於許多工業 AI 應用來說是基礎性的。解決這類問題的大規模現實案例通常需要仔細的問題形式化、專門的求解器和專家設計的啟發式方法。因此，專家需要不僅指定解決方案是什麼，還要說明它們是如何得出的。通過引入工具 CHECKMATE，我們展示了通過代碼演化生成算法代表了一種範式轉變，因為它消除了對於如何形式化的需求。CHECKMATE 完全依賴於什麼。具體而言，正式規範確保了解決方案的正確性，並使生成程序的系統性能評估成為可能，而自然語言描述則指導演化過程。我們的方法在來自兩個工業領域的選定問題上得到了有效性證明：配置和排程。在所有情況下，演化的算法始終超越了最先進的求解器。這強調了正式方法在指導代碼演化以自動解決複雜現實問題方面的潛力。

##### **TUX: Measuring Human--AI Tacit Understanding**
2605.30930v1 by Yueshen Li, Hanyi Min, Vedant Das Swain, Koustuv Saha

As large language models (LLMs) increasingly act as collaborative partners, human--AI alignment is often evaluated through explicit task success, accuracy, or reward optimization. Yet many collaborative settings depend on tacit understanding: whether an agent can align with a human's evaluative stance or representational priors without clear objectives, communication, or feedback. To study this capacity, we develop a spectrum-placement task inspired by the social party game Wavelength, in which humans and agents independently place concepts along subjective spectra. We operationalize the Tacit Understanding Index (TUX) as a pairwise measure of similarity between human and agent judgments, and evaluate it with 241 human participants and 200 profile-conditioned LLM agents across four models. We find that nearest human--agent pairs in trait space achieve significantly higher TUX, suggesting that tacit alignment is structured by person-level characteristics rather than random similarity. Regression analyses show that TUX becomes more explainable as predictor sets become richer, with individual traits, decision-making styles, and confidence improving over aggregate trait-distance baselines. These findings suggest that tacit understanding between humans and LLMs is measurable, while revealing the limits of profile-based conditioning for capturing deeper representational alignment.

摘要：隨著大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地作為合作夥伴，人類與人工智慧的對齊通常通過明確的任務成功、準確性或獎勵優化來評估。<lb/>然而，許多合作環境依賴於默契理解：一個代理是否能夠在沒有明確目標、溝通或反饋的情況下，與人類的評價立場或表徵先驗對齊。<lb/>為了研究這一能力，我們開發了一個受社交派對遊戲Wavelength啟發的光譜放置任務，在這個任務中，人類和代理獨立地將概念放置在主觀光譜上。<lb/>我們將默契理解指數（TUX）操作化為人類和代理判斷之間的成對相似性度量，並在四個模型中對241名人類參與者和200名基於個人資料的LLM代理進行評估。<lb/>我們發現，在特徵空間中，最近的人類與代理配對達到了顯著更高的TUX，這表明默契對齊是由個人層面的特徵結構化的，而不是隨機相似性。<lb/>回歸分析顯示，隨著預測變量集變得更加豐富，TUX變得更具可解釋性，個體特徵、決策風格和信心在整體特徵距離基準之上有所改善。<lb/>這些發現表明，人類與LLMs之間的默契理解是可測量的，同時揭示了基於個人資料的條件化在捕捉更深層表徵對齊方面的局限性。

##### **Design and Evaluation of Multi-Agent AI Oracle Systems for Prediction Market Resolution**
2605.30802v1 by Tarun Kota

Prediction markets aggregate collective intelligence to forecast uncertain events, but their utility depends on reliable outcome resolution. Existing oracle systems tradeoff fast but brittle automation against accurate but costly human arbitration. Single-LLM oracles achieve meaningful accuracy but inherit all failure modes of their underlying model with no self-correction mechanism. We evaluate whether multi-agent LLM architectures can improve oracle resolution accuracy over single-model baselines. We compare independent aggregation and deliberative consensus against single-LLM baselines (GPT-5 Nano, DeepSeek V3, and Llama-3.3-70B) on 1,189 resolved prediction market questions from KalshiBench. All agents share a common evidence layer through Exa, with retrieval filtered by publication date to isolate reasoning from retrieval quality. Independent aggregation with confidence-weighted voting achieves the highest accuracy at 83.43 percent, outperforming the best individual model by 1.01 percentage points. Deliberative consensus degrades accuracy to approximately 76 percent, below every single-model baseline, attributed to error propagation during debate where confidently wrong models flip correct ones. Error correlations across models (0.529-0.689) explain why aggregation gains fall short of the theoretical Condorcet ceiling, placing a fundamental limit on ensemble approaches. Many questions resist correction by any multi-agent architecture, motivating escalation to human arbitration. We propose routing criteria for hybrid AI-human oracle systems: auto-resolving only unanimous, high-confidence questions yields 97.87 percent accuracy on 47 percent of the dataset, with inter-agent disagreement flagging the remainder for human review.

摘要：預測市場聚合集體智慧以預測不確定事件，但其效用取決於可靠的結果解決。現有的預言機系統在快速但脆弱的自動化與準確但昂貴的人為仲裁之間進行權衡。單一LLM預言機實現了有意義的準確性，但繼承了其底層模型的所有失敗模式，且沒有自我修正機制。我們評估多代理LLM架構是否能改善預言機解決的準確性，超越單模型基準。我們在來自KalshiBench的1,189個已解決的預測市場問題上，將獨立聚合和深思熟慮的共識與單一LLM基準（GPT-5 Nano、DeepSeek V3和Llama-3.3-70B）進行比較。所有代理通過Exa共享一個共同的證據層，檢索根據出版日期過濾，以隔離推理與檢索質量。使用信心加權投票的獨立聚合在83.43%的準確率上達到了最高的準確性，超過了最佳單一模型1.01個百分點。深思熟慮的共識將準確性降至約76%，低於每個單模型基準，這歸因於辯論期間錯誤傳播，當自信錯誤的模型翻轉正確的模型。模型之間的錯誤相關性（0.529-0.689）解釋了為什麼聚合增益未能達到理論上的康多塞上限，對集成方法施加了基本限制。許多問題無法被任何多代理架構修正，促使升級至人為仲裁。我們提出了混合AI-人類預言機系統的路由標準：僅自動解決一致的高信心問題，在47%的數據集中實現了97.87%的準確率，其餘部分則因代理間的分歧而標記為人類審查。

##### **On the impact of retrieved content representations in RAG Pipelines**
2605.30790v1 by Jonathan J Ross, Bevan Koopman, Anton van der Vegt, Guido Zuccon

Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) supplements a language model's input with retrieved documents, yet most RAG pipelines inherit retrieval components designed for human readers. How retrieved content should be represented when the consumer is a large language model (LLM) rather than a human is less well understood. Recent work has proposed transformations of retrieved content and identified properties that affect generation, but each examines a single transformation or property in isolation, leaving open which features of a document's representation matter most. We address this with a controlled comparison: holding retrieval fixed, we vary only the representation of retrieved documents, comparing an original baseline against thirteen transformations spanning selection, summarisation, and reformulation, in query-dependent and query-independent variants. Across these fourteen representations we measure question-answering accuracy for four generators, and for each representation we also measure answer retention: whether a known answer-bearing document still supports its answer after transformation. We find that answer retention is the primary determinant of generator accuracy; notably, when retention is high, a representation's wording, structure, length, and query-dependence have limited effect. This suggests that accuracy gains attributed to specific mechanisms in prior work may be partly explained by how well those mechanisms preserve answer-bearing content, an attribution that cannot be settled without controlling for retention.

摘要：檢索增強生成（RAG）通過檢索的文檔來補充語言模型的輸入，但大多數 RAG 管道繼承了為人類讀者設計的檢索組件。當消費者是一個大型語言模型（LLM）而非人類時，檢索內容應如何表示則不太清楚。最近的研究提出了檢索內容的轉換，並識別了影響生成的屬性，但每個研究都孤立地檢查了單一的轉換或屬性，未能確定文檔表示的哪些特徵最為重要。我們通過控制比較來解決這個問題：固定檢索，我們僅改變檢索文檔的表示，將原始基準與涵蓋選擇、摘要和重述的十三種轉換進行比較，包括查詢依賴和查詢獨立的變體。在這十四種表示中，我們測量了四個生成器的問答準確性，並且對於每種表示，我們還測量了答案保留：即在轉換後，已知的答案承載文檔是否仍然支持其答案。我們發現答案保留是生成器準確性的主要決定因素；值得注意的是，當保留率高時，表示的措辭、結構、長度和查詢依賴性對準確性的影響有限。這表明，先前工作中歸因於特定機制的準確性增益可能部分是由於這些機制在保留答案承載內容方面的有效性，這一歸因無法在不控制保留的情況下確定。

##### **Kalimati Vegetable Price Index Forecasting with a Momentum Corrected Online Stacking Ensemble**
2605.30720v1 by Sahaj Raj Malla

Forecasting agricultural commodity prices in emerging economies is difficult due to high volatility, frequent supply disruptions, and strong cultural influences on demand. This study introduces the Kalimati Vegetable Price Index (KVPI), a new inverse-volatility weighted composite index that aggregates 135 daily wholesale commodities from Kathmandu over ten years (2013-2023). By creating a stable macro-level signal, the KVPI reduces the noise inherent in modelling individual crops. A rich set of 64 causally valid features was developed, including festival lead-lag effects, rolling statistics, and calendar variables. Fourteen forecasting models spanning statistical, tree-based, deep learning, hybrid, and transformer architectures were rigorously evaluated across short (7-day), medium (14- and 30-day), and long-term (90-day) horizons. Tree-based ensembles proved notably robust, while classical statistical models and complex transformers struggled with the noisy dataset. The proposed Momentum-Corrected Online Stacking Ensemble achieved the strongest performance, yielding a Root Mean Square Error (RMSE) of 1.771, an exceptionally low Mean Absolute Percentage Error (MAPE) of 0.68%, and explaining 84.5% of the variance (R-squared = 0.845) at the 90-day horizon. This open-source pipeline provides policymakers and supply chain actors in Nepal and similar markets with a practical, reliable tool for anticipating price movements and strengthening food security.

摘要：預測新興經濟體的農產品價格是困難的，因為這些市場具有高度波動性、頻繁的供應中斷，以及對需求的強烈文化影響。這項研究介紹了卡利馬提蔬菜價格指數（KVPI），這是一個新的逆波動加權綜合指數，匯總了2013年至2023年間加德滿都的135種每日批發商品。通過創建一個穩定的宏觀信號，KVPI減少了建模單一作物時固有的噪音。開發了一組豐富的64個因果有效特徵，包括節慶的滯後效應、滾動統計和日曆變數。對於短期（7天）、中期（14天和30天）和長期（90天）的預測模型，對十四種模型進行了嚴格評估，這些模型涵蓋了統計、基於樹的、深度學習、混合和Transformer架構。基於樹的集成模型顯示出特別的穩健性，而傳統的統計模型和複雜的Transformer在噪音數據集上表現不佳。所提出的動量修正在線堆疊集成模型達到了最佳性能，根均方誤差（RMSE）為1.771，平均絕對百分比誤差（MAPE）極低，僅為0.68%，並在90天的預測中解釋了84.5%的變異（R平方 = 0.845）。這個開源管道為尼泊爾及類似市場的政策制定者和供應鏈參與者提供了一個實用、可靠的工具，以預測價格變動並加強食品安全。

##### **Simple Token-Efficient Vision-Language Model for Case-level Pathology Synoptic Report Generation**
2605.30716v1 by Zhiyuan Yang, Jiahao Cheng, Vincent Quoc-Huy Trinh, Mahdi S. Hosseini

Generating clinically useful pathology reports for pathology cases from whole-slide images (WSIs) is challenging due to gigapixel resolution, long visual-token sequences, and the complexity of case-level reasoning, where a single case may contain multiple WSIs with heterogeneous tissues and ambiguous findings. We present a simple token-efficient vision--language model for case-level synoptic report generation that remains practical under constrained GPU memory. Our architecture follows a minimal three-component design: a frozen pathology patch encoder, a lightweight two-layer MLP vision-language aligner, and a large language model decoder, with an explicit WSI marker token to separate slides within a case. Training proceeds in two supervised stages: (1) aligner-only WSI captioning using heterogeneous WSI-text pairs, and (2) case-level supervised fine-tuning on case-report pairs for structured report generation. To reduce sequence length, we represent each slide using $512 \times 512$ patches at $5\times$ magnification, which reduces the average sequence length by up to $64\times$ times compared to the commonly used $20\times$ patches. Combined with efficient training techniques, we enable practical training with only half a NVIDIA H100 GPU. Across both training stages, our approach achieves high ROUGE-L/METEOR/BLEU-4 scores while being substantially more efficient in memory and runtime. In AI-based evaluations, our model is consistently preferred over strong baselines. Extensive ablations characterize performance-efficiency trade-offs and identify simple choices that improve robustness in multi-WSI settings. Overall, this work provides a strong, reproducible baseline for efficient pathology report generation, lowering the barrier to multi-WSI VLM research under limited compute.

摘要：生成臨床有用的病理報告，針對來自全片影像（WSIs）的病理案例，由於其千億像素的解析度、長視覺標記序列以及案例層級推理的複雜性，面臨挑戰，其中單一案例可能包含多個具有異質組織和模糊發現的WSIs。我們提出了一種簡單的令牌高效視覺-語言模型，用於案例層級的綜合報告生成，並在受限的GPU記憶體下保持實用。我們的架構遵循最小的三組件設計：一個凍結的病理補丁編碼器、一個輕量級的兩層MLP視覺-語言對齊器，以及一個大型語言模型解碼器，並使用明確的WSI標記令牌來區分案例內的幻燈片。訓練分為兩個監督階段進行：（1）僅對齊器的WSI標題生成，使用異質的WSI-文本對，和（2）針對案例報告對的案例層級監督微調，以進行結構化報告生成。為了減少序列長度，我們使用$512 \times 512$的補丁，並在$5\times$放大倍率下表示每個幻燈片，這使得平均序列長度比常用的$20\times$補丁減少了最多$64\times$倍。結合高效的訓練技術，我們僅用半個NVIDIA H100 GPU實現了實用的訓練。在兩個訓練階段中，我們的方法在ROUGE-L/METEOR/BLEU-4分數上都取得了高分，同時在記憶體和運行時間上顯著更高效。在基於AI的評估中，我們的模型始終比強基線更受青睞。廣泛的消融實驗描述了性能-效率的權衡，並確定了簡單的選擇，以提高多WSI設置中的穩健性。總體而言，這項工作為高效的病理報告生成提供了一個強大且可重複的基線，降低了在有限計算資源下進行多WSI VLM研究的門檻。

##### **Healthcare Mechanisms from Policy-as-Code Search under Strategic Provider Response**
2605.30680v1 by Zihan Wang, Xiang Xu, Hongyuan Zha, Wenhao Li

Healthcare mechanisms are inseparable from the strategic provider response they induce: existing healthcare AI benchmarks hold this response fixed and so cannot evaluate mechanisms by the equilibrium they produce. We recast hospital mechanism design as program synthesis for language models: typed, inspectable rule programs are executed and scored by Medi-Sim, a multi-agent simulator with five strategic provider channels (coding, selection, delay, effort, triage). An incentive sweep recovers classical health-economics findings as adjacent regimes -- up-coding and low-complexity-patient selection under profit pressure, and Goodhart-style drift where measured performance becomes anti-correlated with true outcomes -- and a single audit lever exposes pressure migration: closing the coding channel more than doubles low-complexity selection. LLM-guided evolutionary code search over the same rule-program space then synthesizes an inspectable mixed-objective program that eliminates up-coding, halves rejection, and retains most of the profit-oriented baseline's funds.

摘要：醫療保健機制與其引發的戰略提供者反應密不可分：現有的醫療保健 AI 基準將這一反應固定，因此無法通過其產生的均衡來評估機制。我們將醫院機制設計重新構想為語言模型的程序合成：類型化、可檢查的規則程序由 Medi-Sim 執行並評分，這是一個具有五個戰略提供者通道（編碼、選擇、延遲、努力、分診）的多代理模擬器。一個激勵掃描恢復了經典健康經濟學的發現，作為相鄰的體系——在利潤壓力下的上編碼和低複雜性病人選擇，以及 Goodhart 風格的漂移，其中測量的表現與真實結果反向相關——而單一的審計槓桿揭示了壓力遷移：關閉編碼通道使低複雜性選擇增加超過兩倍。然後，基於 LLM 指導的演化代碼搜索在相同的規則程序空間中合成了一個可檢查的混合目標程序，消除了上編碼，將拒絕率減半，並保留了大部分以利潤為導向的基線資金。

##### **Counterfactual Evaluation Reveals Hidden Capability Profiles in Clinical LLMs and Agents**
2605.30590v1 by Matt Turk

Two clinical AI systems can score nearly identically on coverage-based rubrics yet behave radically differently when their patient inputs change: one updates its recommendations to match the new clinical signal, while the other produces the same output regardless. We introduce the Causal Sensitivity Score (CSS), a pre-registered interventional metric that mutates oncology tumor-board cases along five clinically meaningful dimensions - biomarker flips, prior-treatment failures, biomarker removals, surgery-status changes, and stage perturbations - and scores whether each model updates its recommendations in the pre-registered correct direction using a {0, 0.5, 1.0} scale. Benchmarked against the Consensus Match Score (CMS), a coverage-based weighted recall metric, six frontier models from three labs evaluated in single-shot inference across 224 cases rank in nearly opposite orders: all six models change rank, the CMS-worst model becomes CSS-best, and one upper-mid CMS model ranks last on CSS. We further surface a universal safety blind spot: every frontier model fails on surgery-status interventions (at most 17.2% CSS on Family D), a finding CMS does not expose. The metric also transfers to tool-using agents: in a ReAct-style experiment, tool use improves CSS for five of six models (+2.5 to +20.3 percentage points), yet the lowest-CSS model retrieves the same chart sections and still fails to update its recommendations - revealing a structural responsiveness deficit visible only under counterfactual evaluation. Cross-judge replication and three-rater medical-professional validation confirm the aggregate findings. Interventional pre-registered metrics like CSS complement coverage-based evaluation for clinical AI agents: they capture responsiveness that coverage metrics miss and offer a candidate dense reward signal for future agentic RL systems.

摘要：兩個臨床 AI 系統在基於覆蓋率的評分標準上幾乎得分相同，但當患者輸入變化時，它們的行為卻截然不同：一個系統根據新的臨床信號更新其建議，而另一個系統則無論如何都產生相同的輸出。我們介紹了因果敏感度分數 (CSS)，這是一個預註冊的干預指標，沿著五個臨床意義重大的維度變更腫瘤委員會案例——生物標記翻轉、先前治療失敗、生物標記移除、手術狀態變更和階段擾動——並評分每個模型是否在預註冊的正確方向上更新其建議，使用 {0, 0.5, 1.0} 的標準。與共識匹配分數 (CMS) 進行基準比較，來自三個實驗室的六個前沿模型在 224 個案例中的單次推理評估中幾乎排名相反：所有六個模型的排名都發生變化，CMS 最差的模型成為 CSS 最佳，而一個中上等的 CMS 模型在 CSS 中排名最後。我們進一步揭示了一個普遍的安全盲點：每個前沿模型在手術狀態干預上都失敗（在 D 類家庭中最多 17.2% CSS），這一發現是 CMS 所未揭示的。該指標還可轉移到使用工具的代理：在 ReAct 風格的實驗中，工具使用提高了六個模型中五個的 CSS（+2.5 到 +20.3 個百分點），然而最低 CSS 的模型檢索相同的圖表部分，仍然未能更新其建議——揭示了只有在反事實評估下才能顯現的結構性反應不足。交叉評審重複和三評審醫療專業驗證確認了總體發現。像 CSS 這樣的干預預註冊指標補充了基於覆蓋率的臨床 AI 代理評估：它們捕捉到覆蓋率指標所忽略的反應性，並為未來的代理強化學習系統提供了一個候選的密集獎勵信號。

##### **XAI-SOH-FL: Enhancing SOH-FL with Adaptive Aggregation and Explainable AI for Intrusion Detection in Heterogeneous IoT**
2606.00134v1 by Ambreen Aslam, Maaz Hassan, Bibi Zahra, Muhammad Khuram Shahzad

Intrusion Detection Systems (IDS) in Internet of Things (IoT) environments face significant challenges due to data heterogeneity, lack of labeled data, and limited model interpretability. Federated Learning (FL) offers a privacy-preserving solution; however, existing approaches such as SOH-FL suffer from two key limitations: reliance on a manually tuned aggregation parameter γ and lack of explainability in model predictions. In this paper, we propose XAI-SOH-FL, an enhanced framework that integrates adaptive aggregation and explainable artificial intelligence into the SOH-FL paradigm. First, we introduce a dynamic γ selection mechanism based on similarity thresholding, enabling the aggregation process to adapt to evolving data distributions. Second, Bayesian Optimization is employed to automatically determine optimal γ values, eliminating the need for manual tuning. Third, SHAP (SHapley Additive exPlanations) is incorporated to provide feature-level interpretability for intrusion detection decisions. Experimental evaluation on the CICIDS2017 dataset demonstrates that the proposed approach achieves an accuracy of 94.12% and an F1-score of 0.92, outperforming the baseline SOH-FL model while converging in fewer communication rounds. Furthermore, SHAP-based analysis reveals that flow-level features such as Flow Duration and Packet Length significantly influence model predictions. These results indicate that XAI-SOH-FL provides an effective balance between accuracy, adaptability, and interpretability in heterogeneous IoT environments.

摘要：入侵檢測系統（IDS）在物聯網（IoT）環境中面臨重大挑戰，這是由於數據異質性、缺乏標記數據和模型可解釋性有限所致。聯邦學習（FL）提供了一種保護隱私的解決方案；然而，現有的方法如SOH-FL存在兩個主要限制：依賴手動調整的聚合參數γ和模型預測缺乏可解釋性。在本文中，我們提出了XAI-SOH-FL，一個增強框架，將自適應聚合和可解釋人工智慧整合到SOH-FL範式中。首先，我們介紹了一種基於相似性閾值的動態γ選擇機制，使聚合過程能夠適應不斷變化的數據分佈。其次，採用貝葉斯優化自動確定最佳γ值，消除了手動調整的需要。第三，納入SHAP（SHapley Additive exPlanations）以提供入侵檢測決策的特徵層級可解釋性。對CICIDS2017數據集的實驗評估表明，所提出的方法達到了94.12%的準確率和0.92的F1分數，超越了基線SOH-FL模型，同時在更少的通信輪次中收斂。此外，基於SHAP的分析顯示，流級特徵如流持續時間和數據包長度對模型預測有顯著影響。這些結果表明，XAI-SOH-FL在異質IoT環境中提供了準確性、適應性和可解釋性之間的有效平衡。

##### **Gram: Assessing sabotage propensities via automated alignment auditing**
2605.30322v1 by David Lindner, Victoria Krakovna, Sebastian Farquhar

We introduce Gram, an automated alignment auditing framework to assess the propensity of AI agents to engage in sabotage. We evaluate Gemini models across 17 simulated agentic deployment scenarios that incentivize sabotage. We find Gemini models misbehave in about 2-3% of our simulated trajectories. Many of these cases are explained by "overeagerness" in Gemini models resulting in both excessive role-playing and goal-seeking behavior. In contrast to other alignment auditing approaches, Gram is designed to specifically evaluate misalignment and intentional sabotage in agentic coding and research agents. We additionally introduce an experimental investigator agent pipeline which enables fine-grained targeted experiments to identify the drivers of misbehavior. We find that increasing realism of environments and removing nudges to misbehave tends to reduce sabotage rates close to zero.

##### **A Mechanistic Analysis of Adversarial Fine-tuning of Vision Transformers**
2606.07593v1 by Hannah Gao, Isha Agarwal, Dylan Hadfield-Menell, Rachel Ma

The widespread use of image classification models in high-risk, real-world situations necessitates making these models robust to slight disturbances or perturbations, such as blurring or sharpening, in the input images. While vision transformers (ViTs) play an integral role in many modern-day multi-modal models like Vision-Language-Models (VLMs) and Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models, they have received a lack of attention in the setting of robustness. In this work, we analyze the effects of adversarial fine-tuning, a popular method for improving model robustness to image perturbations, on a ViT's performance on perturbed and regular images through a mechanistic lens. We adversarially train a ViT on low-frequency and high-frequency image corruptions, and attempt to explain changes in downstream model performance through an examination of the model's attention mechanisms, internal representations, and knowledge evolution. Overall, our results suggest that, while fine-tuning on inputs with common corruptions improves model performance and certainty on new instances of corrupted data, these improvements do not transfer to other classes of corruptions not seen in the training. Additionally, despite observing changes in visual attention and knowledge evolution across layers, we found that adversarial training did not lead to fundamental changes in the sparse representations learned by ViTs.

摘要：廣泛使用影像分類模型於高風險的現實情境中，必須使這些模型對輸入影像中的輕微擾動或干擾（如模糊或銳化）具有穩健性。雖然視覺Transformer（ViTs）在許多現代多模態模型中扮演著不可或缺的角色，例如視覺-語言模型（VLMs）和視覺-語言-行動（VLA）模型，但在穩健性方面卻受到忽視。在本研究中，我們從機制的角度分析了對抗性微調這一流行方法對ViT在擾動和正常影像上的性能影響，該方法旨在提高模型對影像擾動的穩健性。我們對ViT進行了低頻和高頻影像損壞的對抗性訓練，並試圖通過檢查模型的注意力機制、內部表示和知識演變來解釋下游模型性能的變化。總體而言，我們的結果表明，儘管在具有常見損壞的輸入上進行微調能改善模型在新損壞數據實例上的性能和確定性，但這些改進並不會轉移到訓練中未見過的其他類別的損壞。此外，儘管我們觀察到不同層次間的視覺注意力和知識演變的變化，但我們發現對抗性訓練並未導致ViTs學習到的稀疏表示發生根本性的變化。

##### **Genetically Aligned Patient Representations Improve Hematological Diagnosis**
2605.29980v1 by Muhammed Furkan Dasdelen, Fatih Ozlugedik, Ilaria Looser, Rao Muhammad Umer, Christian Pohlkamp, Carsten Marr

Multimodal alignment of histopathology encoders with transcriptomic and genomic data has been shown to significantly improve performance in downstream diagnostic tasks. Hematological cytology is unique in that visual single-cell evaluation is often paired with cytogenetics and molecular genetics for blood cancer diagnosis. In this study, we present a framework to align single white blood cell images with chromosomal aberrations (karyotype) and somatic mutations from targeted gene panels. Our training strategy follows a two-stage approach: (i) self-supervised, vision-only pretraining of a transformer aggregator using an iBOT head on a cohort of over 1500 patients, and (ii) genetic alignment via supervised contrastive loss on acute myeloid leukemia patients. Our genetically aligned patient encoder improves hematological diagnostic tasks, outperforming slide-level histopathology foundation models. Additionally, the model provides off-the-shelf retrieval capabilities for diseases and genetic alterations. Incorporating genetic data into patient encoders increases the quality of patient representations, providing a framework that aligns with clinical diagnostic workflows and paves the way for future multimodal hematology-specific AI. The code and model weights are available at https://github.com/marrlab/GenBloom.

##### **Why Specialist Models Still Matter: A Heterogeneous Multi-Agent Paradigm for Medical Artificial Intelligence**
2605.29744v1 by Yanan Wang, Shuaicong Hu, Jian Liu, Guohui Zhou, Aiguo Wang, Cuiwei Yang

The impressive performance of generalist large language models (LLMs) such as GPT and Claude in healthcare raises a critical question: will domain-specific medical specialist models become obsolete? We argue that the future of medical artificial intelligence (AI) lies not in building monolithic medical foundation models, nor in replacing human expertise, but in orchestrating collaboration among generalist LLMs, domain-specific specialist models, and clinicians. We propose HetMedAgent, a heterogeneous medical multi-agent framework that enables conflict-aware evidence fusion, uncertainty-based clinician intervention triggering, and adaptive threshold calibration. Experiments on three real-world clinical decision-making tasks demonstrate that the synergy between generalist LLMs and domain-specific specialist models significantly outperforms using either type of model alone, validating the irreplaceable value of specialist models in modality-specific analysis. HetMedAgent represents a shift from building medical LLMs or foundation models to multi-agent collaboration, achieving a balance between general reasoning capabilities and domain-specific precision.

##### **FHRFormer: A Self-Supervised Masked Transformer Framework for Fetal Heart Rate Time-Series Inpainting and Forecasting**
2605.29695v1 by Kjersti Engan, Neel Kanwal, Anita Yeconia, Ladislaus Blacy, Yuda Munyaw, Estomih Mduma, Hege Ersdal

Approximately 10% of newborns require assistance to initiate breathing at birth, and around 5% need ventilation support. Fetal heart rate (FHR) monitoring plays a crucial role in assessing fetal well-being during prenatal care, enabling the detection of abnormal patterns and supporting timely obstetric interventions to mitigate fetal risks during labor. Applying artificial intelligence (AI) methods to analyze large datasets of continuous FHR monitoring episodes with diverse outcomes may offer novel insights into predicting the risk of needing breathing assistance or interventions. Recent advances in wearable FHR monitors have enabled continuous fetal monitoring without compromising maternal mobility. However, sensor displacement during maternal movement, as well as changes in fetal or maternal position, often lead to signal dropout, resulting in gaps in recorded FHR data. Such missing data limits the extraction of meaningful insights and complicates automated (AI-based) analysis. Traditional approaches to handling missing data, such as simple interpolation techniques, often fail to preserve the spectral characteristics of the signals. In this paper, we propose a masked transformer-based autoencoder approach to reconstruct missing FHR signals by capturing both local temporal and frequency components of the data. The proposed method demonstrates robustness across varying durations of missing data and can be used for signal inpainting and forecasting. The proposed approach can be applied retrospectively to research datasets to support the development of AI-based risk algorithms. In the future, the proposed method could be integrated into wearable FHR monitoring devices to achieve earlier and more robust risk detection.

摘要：大約 10% 的新生兒在出生時需要協助啟動呼吸，約有 5% 需要通氣支持。胎心率 (FHR) 監測在產前護理中扮演著關鍵角色，能夠評估胎兒健康狀況，檢測異常模式，並支持及時的產科干預，以減少分娩期間的胎兒風險。應用人工智慧 (AI) 方法分析具有多樣結果的大型連續 FHR 監測數據集，可能提供預測需要呼吸協助或干預風險的新見解。最近可穿戴 FHR 監測器的進步使得連續胎兒監測得以實現，而不會妨礙母體的活動。然而，在母體運動期間，傳感器位移以及胎兒或母體位置的變化，往往導致信號丟失，造成記錄的 FHR 數據出現間隙。這種缺失數據限制了有意義見解的提取，並使自動化 (基於 AI) 分析變得複雜。傳統處理缺失數據的方法，如簡單插值技術，往往無法保留信號的頻譜特徵。在本文中，我們提出了一種基於掩碼Transformer的自編碼器方法，以通過捕捉數據的局部時間和頻率組件來重建缺失的 FHR 信號。所提出的方法在不同缺失數據持續時間下顯示出穩健性，並可用於信號修復和預測。該方法可回顧性地應用於研究數據集，以支持基於 AI 的風險算法的開發。在未來，所提出的方法可以整合到可穿戴 FHR 監測設備中，以實現更早和更穩健的風險檢測。

##### **Battery-Sim-Agent: Leveraging LLM-Agent for Inverse Battery Parameter Estimation**
2605.29560v1 by Jiawei Chen, Xiaofan Gui, Shikai Fang, Shengyu Tao, Shun Zheng, Weiqing Liu, Jiang Bian

Parameterizing high-fidelity "digital twins" of batteries is a critical yet challenging inverse problem that hinders the pace of battery innovation. Prevailing methods formulate this as a black-box optimization (BBO) task, employing algorithms that are sample-inefficient and blind to the underlying physics. In this work, we introduce a new paradigm that reframes the inverse problem as a reasoning task, and present Battery-Sim-Agent, the first framework to deploy a Large Language Model (LLM) agent in a closed loop with a high-fidelity battery simulator. The agent mimics a human scientist's workflow: it interprets rich, multi-modal feedback from the simulator, forms physically-grounded hypotheses to explain discrepancies, and proposes structured parameter updates. On a systematically constructed benchmark suite spanning diverse battery chemistries, operating conditions, and difficulty levels, our agent significantly outperforms strong BBO baselines like Bayesian optimization in identifying accurate parameters. We further demonstrate the framework's capability in complex long-horizon degradation fitting tasks and validate its practical applicability on real-world battery datasets. Our results highlight the promise of LLM-agents as reasoning-based optimizers for scientific discovery and battery parameter estimation.

摘要：參數化高保真度的「數位雙胞胎」電池是一個關鍵但具挑戰性的反向問題，這妨礙了電池創新的進程。現行方法將其表述為黑箱優化（BBO）任務，採用的算法在樣本效率上表現不佳，且對潛在物理原理視而不見。在本研究中，我們引入了一種新的範式，將反向問題重新框架為推理任務，並提出了Battery-Sim-Agent，這是第一個在高保真電池模擬器中以閉環方式部署大型語言模型（LLM）代理的框架。該代理模擬了人類科學家的工作流程：它解釋來自模擬器的豐富多模態反饋，形成基於物理的假設來解釋差異，並提出結構化的參數更新。在一個系統性構建的基準套件中，涵蓋了多樣的電池化學、操作條件和難度級別，我們的代理在識別準確參數方面顯著超越了像貝葉斯優化這樣的強BBO基準。我們進一步展示了該框架在複雜長期退化擬合任務中的能力，並驗證了其在現實世界電池數據集上的實用性。我們的結果突顯了LLM代理作為基於推理的優化器在科學發現和電池參數估計中的潛力。

##### **LLMs Without Deep Neural Networks: New Architecture, Benefits and Case Study**
2605.30385v1 by Vincent Granville

The purpose of this article is to provide validation to my deep neural network alternative in the context of LLMs. Very recently, there has been a significant interest by Chinese researchers in a model called RBF network, as a substitute to standard DNNs, with increased explainability and higher accuracy. It turns out that my new model, discovered independently, is based on the exact same machinery. But with a major twist: it does not need DNN as it finds the global optimum of the loss function in closed form, in one iteration, thus eliminating the tedious training step. Here I provide a high-level overview of my technology, with case study and comparison to similar methods.

摘要：這篇文章的目的是在LLMs的背景下對我的深度神經網絡替代方案提供驗證。最近，中國研究人員對一種稱為RBF網絡的模型產生了重大興趣，作為標準DNN的替代方案，具有更高的可解釋性和更高的準確性。事實上，我的新模型是獨立發現的，基於完全相同的機制。但有一個重大轉折：它不需要DNN，因為它以封閉形式在一次迭代中找到損失函數的全局最優解，從而消除了繁瑣的訓練步驟。在這裡，我提供了我的技術的高層次概述，並附上案例研究和與類似方法的比較。
