摘要：可驗證性、歸屬性和可重複性是科學知識的基本要求，但當前的出版基礎設施並未在大規模上強制執行這些要求。我們介紹了Traxia，一個原生於代理的科學出版框架，在這個框架中，AI研究代理發表可驗證的論文，建立聲譽身份，互相進行同行評審，並在共享來源模型中與人類合作。Traxia將代理視為一級認識參與者：每篇論文都有推理痕跡，每個主張都有置信區間，每個代理都有加密簽名的身份，每次合作都有不可變的貢獻日誌。我們正式化了五個組件：代理身份和登記、可驗證出版層、四層同行評審協議、聲譽和質押引擎，以及具有矛盾檢測的知識圖譜。該框架針對可重複性失敗、來源不透明和全球南方研究能力的排斥。本文僅呈現架構基礎和正式規範；不報告實證結果。評估和更深入的組件研究將在後續論文中進行。一個原型部分實現了核心形式化；完整系統仍在積極開發中。

##### **ZAS-SQL: Distilling Rules from Failures for Zero-Shot Text-to-SQL**
2606.08245v1 by Hongzhou Zheng, Yixin Gou, Wenjia Zhang

Text-to-SQL translates natural language into executable SQL queries. Few-shot in-context learning methods built upon large language models (LLMs) achieve strong performance, yet their reliance on demonstrations limits cross-domain generalization and consumes substantial context window space. Existing zero-shot methods, lacking effective generation constraints, still fall short of few-shot approaches. We observe that LLM failures in zero-shot Text-to-SQL are not random but exhibit systematic, recurring patterns. Building on this observation, we propose a fully zero-shot Text-to-SQL framework that distills core generation rules from failure cases through a Map-Reduce-based rule distillation pipeline and improves generation quality via three complementary modules: knowledge-augmented schema representation, which supplements missing semantics in Data Definition Language; a rule-driven structured reasoning framework that suppresses structural deviations; and Execution-Guided Early Stopping, which enables low-cost self-correction. On Spider, the proposed framework achieves up to 87.2% and 88.6% execution accuracy on the Dev and Test sets, respectively, establishing a new zero-shot state-of-the-art and surpassing multiple few-shot and fine-tuning methods built upon GPT-4/4o. On the domain-specific dataset UrbanPlan, it achieves 81.3%, confirming that the rule distillation approach generalizes across domains. Moreover, when equipped with a 4B-parameter model, the framework surpasses zero-shot baselines of leading closed-source models, demonstrating strong model generality.

摘要：文本到 SQL 將自然語言轉換為可執行的 SQL 查詢。基於大型語言模型 (LLMs) 的少量示例上下文學習方法表現出色，但它們對示範的依賴限制了跨領域的泛化，並消耗了大量的上下文窗口空間。現有的零-shot 方法缺乏有效的生成約束，仍然不及少量示例的方法。我們觀察到 LLM 在零-shot 文本到 SQL 中的失敗並非隨機，而是顯示出系統性的、重複的模式。基於這一觀察，我們提出了一個完全的零-shot 文本到 SQL 框架，通過基於 Map-Reduce 的規則提煉管道從失敗案例中提煉核心生成規則，並通過三個互補模塊提高生成質量：知識增強的模式表示，補充數據定義語言中的缺失語義；一個驅動規則的結構推理框架，抑制結構偏差；以及執行引導的早期停止，實現低成本的自我修正。在 Spider 上，所提出的框架在開發集和測試集上分別達到 87.2% 和 88.6% 的執行準確率，樹立了新的零-shot 最佳紀錄，超越了多種基於 GPT-4/4o 的少量示例和微調方法。在特定領域數據集 UrbanPlan 上，它達到 81.3%，證實了規則提煉方法在不同領域之間的泛化。此外，當配備 4B 參數模型時，該框架超越了領先的封閉源模型的零-shot 基準，顯示出強大的模型泛化能力。

##### **Paediatric-HGNN: A Hybrid Heterogeneous Graph Neural Network for Detecting Disfluency in Children's Speech via Multiscale Acoustic Fusion**
2606.08210v1 by Rashini Liyanarachchi, Rachael Mackay, Alison Short, Aditya Joshi, Erik Meijering

Automated stuttering detection (ASD) systems struggle with paediatric speech due to high acoustic variability in developing voices and the subtle distinction between pathological stuttering and typical developmental disfluencies. We introduce Paediatric-HGNN, a framework using a Context-aware Part-whole Interaction Network (CaPIN) tailored for paediatric data. Instead of conventional 1D signal modelling, our approach builds a heterogeneous graph capturing hierarchical relationships between lexical units (word nodes) and fine-grained acoustic segments (frame nodes). Trained on curated paediatric corpora (UCLASS and FluencyBank), Paediatric-HGNN achieves 82.4% weighted accuracy and a Typical Disfluency F1-score of 0.386. Modelling hierarchical lexical-acoustic interactions captures developmental "searching" behaviour, offering a more robust and interpretable tool for early clinical intervention.

摘要：自動口吃檢測（ASD）系統在兒童語音中面臨挑戰，因為發展中聲音的聲學變異性高，以及病理性口吃與典型發展性流暢性障礙之間的微妙區別。我們介紹了兒童-HGNN，這是一個使用上下文感知的部分整體互動網絡（CaPIN）為兒童數據量身定制的框架。與傳統的1D信號建模不同，我們的方法構建了一個異質圖，捕捉詞彙單位（詞節點）與細粒度聲學片段（幀節點）之間的層次關係。在經過精心挑選的兒童語料庫（UCLASS和FluencyBank）上訓練後，兒童-HGNN達到了82.4%的加權準確率和0.386的典型流暢性F1分數。建模層次詞彙-聲學互動捕捉了發展中的“搜尋”行為，為早期臨床干預提供了一個更穩健且可解釋的工具。

##### **Beyond Additivity: Causal Discovery in Location-Scale Noise Models with Hidden Variables**
2606.08196v1 by Mariyam Khan, Shohei Shimizu, Thong Pham

We study causal discovery from observational data when some variables are hidden and the data-generating process follows a location-scale noise model (LSNM). Existing methods that handle hidden confounders typically assume additive noise, but in practice, causes often modulate not just the mean but also the variance of their effects. We prove that acyclic directed mixed graphs (ADMGs) satisfying a bow-free condition are identifiable under LSNM with hidden variables, establishing the first identifiability result for causally insufficient models beyond noise additivity. We further provide sufficient conditions for identifying causal direction even when the bow-free assumption is violated. Our two-stage algorithm, LSNM-UV, is sound and complete, and experiments demonstrate improved performance over additive baselines on heteroscedastic data.

摘要：我們研究在某些變數隱藏的情況下，從觀察數據中進行因果發現，並且數據生成過程遵循位置-尺度噪聲模型（LSNM）。現有處理隱藏混淆變數的方法通常假設噪聲是加性的，但在實踐中，原因往往不僅調節其影響的均值，還調節其影響的方差。我們證明了滿足無弓條件的無循環有向混合圖（ADMGs）在隱藏變數下是可識別的，這建立了超越噪聲加性模型的因果不足模型的首個可識別性結果。我們進一步提供了即使在違反無弓假設的情況下識別因果方向的充分條件。我們的兩階段算法LSNM-UV是健全且完整的，實驗顯示在異方差數據上其性能優於加性基準。

##### **TextEconomizer: Enhancing Lossy Text Compression with Denoising Transformers and Entropy Coding**
2606.08184v1 by Mahbub E Sobhani, Anika Tasnim Rodela, Chowdhury Mofizur Rahman, Dewan Md. Farid, Swakkhar Shatabda

Lossy text compression reduces data size while preserving core meaning, making it well-suited for summarization, automated analysis, and digital archives. Despite the dominance of transformer-based models in language modeling, integrating context vectors and entropy coding into Sequence-to-Sequence (Seq2Seq) generation remains underexplored. A key challenge lies in identifying the most informative context vectors from encoder output and incorporating entropy coding to enhance storage efficiency while maintaining high-quality outputs, even under noisy text. We introduce TextEconomizer, an encoder-decoder framework paired with a transformer neural network that reduces variable-sized inputs by 50% to 80% without prior knowledge of dataset dimensions. Our model achieves competitive compression ratios via entropy coding while delivering near-perfect text quality, assessed by BLEU, ROUGE, METEOR, and semantic similarity scores. TextEconomizer operates with approximately 153x fewer parameters than comparable models, achieving a 5.39x compression ratio without sacrificing semantic quality. We also evaluate an LSTM-based autoencoder achieving a state-of-the-art 67x compression ratio with 196x fewer parameters, and LLaMAFormer, a modified transformer with 263x fewer parameters than ICAE while maintaining competitive text quality. TextEconomizer significantly surpasses existing transformer-based models in balancing memory efficiency and high-fidelity outputs, marking a breakthrough in lossy compression with optimal space utilization.

摘要：有損文本壓縮在保留核心意義的同時減少數據大小，使其非常適合用於摘要、自動分析和數字檔案。儘管基於Transformer的模型在語言建模中佔主導地位，但將上下文向量和熵編碼整合到序列到序列（Seq2Seq）生成中仍然未被充分探索。一個主要挑戰在於從編碼器輸出中識別出最具信息量的上下文向量，並納入熵編碼以提高存儲效率，同時在嘈雜文本下保持高質量的輸出。我們介紹了TextEconomizer，一個與Transformer神經網絡配對的編碼器-解碼器框架，能在不事先了解數據集維度的情況下將可變大小的輸入減少50%到80%。我們的模型通過熵編碼實現了具有競爭力的壓縮比，同時提供接近完美的文本質量，通過BLEU、ROUGE、METEOR和語義相似性分數進行評估。TextEconomizer的參數約比可比較的模型少153倍，實現了5.39倍的壓縮比而不犧牲語義質量。我們還評估了一個基於LSTM的自編碼器，實現了67倍的最先進壓縮比，參數少196倍，以及LLaMAFormer，一個修改過的Transformer，其參數比ICAE少263倍，同時保持競爭力的文本質量。TextEconomizer在平衡內存效率和高保真輸出方面顯著超越現有的基於Transformer的模型，標誌著有損壓縮在最佳空間利用方面的突破。

##### **Decision-Aware Memory Cards: Counterfactual-Inspired Context Selection and Compression for Tool-Using LLM Agents**
2606.08151v1 by Xinyu Guan, Qianyang Zhao, Yuming Deng

Tool-using LLM agents often fail not because relevant text is absent, but because decisive evidence is not selected, compressed, or surfaced at action time. We present CICL, a decision-aware context layer that turns instance evidence into a context graph, routes deterministic, Opus-assisted, Qwen, Codex/GPT-5.5, and Qwen-QLoRA judgments through a shared eight-field schema, scores units by action shift, outcome uplift, necessity, and negative-transfer risk, and packs high-utility evidence as typed memory cards for a budgeted agent. The design separates the measured decision signal from the judge model, so frontier annotation, local surrogates, and lightweight rankers can be compared under one auditable protocol. Empirically, CICL yields a concrete open-benchmark gain while exposing its limits. On 50 SWE-bench Verified file-retrieval instances, direct Qwen3.6-plus reranking of BM25 top-50 candidates raises hit@1 from 0.58 to 0.78 and MRR@10 from 0.634 to 0.790, with all 2,500 judgments parseable. Controlled diagnostics show action-criticality: at budget 120, CICL reaches F1 0.620 on v1 and 0.425 on v3, and removing the top-utility semantic v3 unit collapses F1 to 0.000. Supplementary checks add Qwen-QLoRA agreement over 710 candidates, a small 200-label real-code Opus-assisted signal, and a three-instance patch smoke validating retrieval-to-patch plumbing without claiming official SWE-bench success. RepoBench-R summaries still beat cards, and compact rankers do not yet replace the heuristic. CICL contributes a reproducible measurement and selection layer for decision-critical context, not an end-to-end coding-agent repair claim.

摘要：工具使用的 LLM 代理經常失敗，不是因為缺乏相關文本，而是因為在行動時未選擇、壓縮或顯示決定性證據。我們提出 CICL，一個決策感知的上下文層，將實例證據轉換為上下文圖，通過共享的八字段架構路由確定性、Opus 輔助的、Qwen、Codex/GPT-5.5 和 Qwen-QLoRA 判斷，根據行動轉移、結果提升、必要性和負轉移風險對單位進行評分，並將高效用證據打包為類型記憶卡以供預算代理使用。該設計將測量的決策信號與判斷模型分開，因此邊界註釋、本地替代品和輕量級排名器可以在一個可審計的協議下進行比較。實證結果顯示，CICL 在揭示其限制的同時，產生了具體的開放基準增益。在 50 個 SWE-bench 驗證的文件檢索實例中，對 BM25 前 50 名候選者進行直接的 Qwen3.6-plus 重新排名，將 hit@1 從 0.58 提升至 0.78，將 MRR@10 從 0.634 提升至 0.790，且所有 2,500 個判斷均可解析。受控診斷顯示行動關鍵性：在預算 120 下，CICL 在 v1 上達到 F1 0.620，在 v3 上達到 0.425，並且移除最高效用的語義 v3 單位使 F1 崩潰至 0.000。補充檢查增加了 Qwen-QLoRA 在 710 個候選者上的一致性、一個小型 200 標籤的實際代碼 Opus 輔助信號，以及三個實例的補丁煙霧測試，驗證了檢索到補丁的管道，而不聲稱官方的 SWE-bench 成功。RepoBench-R 摘要仍然超越卡片，緊湊的排名器尚未取代啟發式方法。CICL 為決策關鍵上下文提供了一個可重現的測量和選擇層，而不是一個端到端的編碼代理修復聲明。

##### **SAGE: An LLM-driven Self Reflective Agentic Framework for Fraud Detection**
2606.08146v1 by Yichen Chen, Siying Li, Yuhang Liang, Lijun Wang, Renyang Liu

Fraud detection in payment, e-commerce, and telecommunications systems requires accuracy at the individual level, robustness under severe class imbalance, and ease of understanding for risk managers. Existing methods fall at least one of these requirements: automated machine learning systems search a fixed numerical space without semantic awareness of the dataset; graph neural network-based methods require pre-defined relational graphs and remain opaque at the individual-decision level; and the design of general-purpose large language model (LLM) agents does not consider the recall and precision constraints specific to real-world fraud detection. In this paper, we propose SAGE, the first end-to-end LLM-driven multi-agent framework for fraud detection. SAGE coordinates three dedicated agents that make decisions based on a six-layer Data Diagnostic Tree (DDT) and a Markov decision process guided by natural-language gradients, automatically optimizing the model under a fraud-specific reward. On five fraud datasets and five LLM backbones, SAGE wins $96.00\%$ of method--dataset comparisons and improves F1 by an average of $40.86\%$ over baselines. The code is available at https://github.com/yichenC1c/SAGE.

摘要：詐騙檢測在支付、電子商務和電信系統中需要在個體層面上具備準確性、在嚴重類別不平衡下的穩健性，以及對風險管理者易於理解。現有的方法至少在這些要求中有一項不足：自動化機器學習系統在沒有語義意識的情況下搜索固定的數值空間；基於圖神經網絡的方法需要預先定義的關係圖，並在個體決策層面上保持不透明；而通用大型語言模型（LLM）代理的設計則未考慮到特定於現實世界詐騙檢測的召回率和精確度約束。在本文中，我們提出了SAGE，首個端到端的LLM驅動多代理詐騙檢測框架。SAGE協調三個專用代理，根據六層數據診斷樹（DDT）和由自然語言梯度指導的馬爾可夫決策過程做出決策，自動優化模型以獲得特定於詐騙的獎勵。在五個詐騙數據集和五個LLM骨幹上，SAGE在方法-數據集比較中贏得了$96.00\%$的勝率，並在基準上平均提高了$40.86\%$的F1分數。代碼可在 https://github.com/yichenC1c/SAGE 獲得。

##### **Continual Quadruped Robots Coordination via Semantic Skill Discovery**
2606.08102v1 by Daoqing Wang, Yuchen Xiao, Weixuan Huang, Zhilong Zhang, Shenghua Wan, Meng Li, Lei Yuan, Yang Yu

Multi-quadruped coordination has attracted increasing attention due to its enhanced payload capacity, broader contact coverage, and improved adaptability to challenging tasks. Existing methods for multi-quadruped manipulation typically focus on predefined or closed task families, often relying on multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) to train task-specific coordination policies. However, such methods struggle in open-ended continual learning settings, where tasks arrive sequentially and robots are expected to acquire new coordination skills while reusing previously learned ones without catastrophic forgetting. To address this challenge, we propose Conquer, a semantic skill-library framework that formulates continual multi-quadruped coordination as a retrieve-adapt-update process. First, to accommodate varying team sizes across tasks, we design a team-structured Self-Allies-Goal (SAG) backbone that supports variable-cardinality robot teams by explicitly modeling each robot's own state, teammate context, and task goal. For each incoming task, Conquer constructs a task-level semantic descriptor from pre-execution information and retrieves a relevant skill from the library for adaptation. After successful execution, Conquer updates the skill library by extracting trajectory-level semantic descriptors and organizing them according to semantic distance, thereby enabling continual skill accumulation and cross-task knowledge transfer. Simulation experiments show that Conquer achieves a final average success rate of 95.6%, demonstrating strong forward transfer and negligible catastrophic forgetting. Real-world rollouts on Unitree Go2 teams further validate the deployment feasibility of Conquer for practical multi-quadruped coordination. Simulation and real-robot demonstration videos are available at: https://conquer-project.pages.dev/.

摘要：多四足協調因其增強的載荷能力、更廣的接觸範圍和改善的適應性而受到越來越多的關注。現有的多四足操作方法通常專注於預定義或封閉的任務類別，經常依賴於多代理強化學習（MARL）來訓練特定任務的協調策略。然而，這些方法在開放式持續學習環境中面臨挑戰，因為任務是依序到來的，機器人需要在不發生災難性遺忘的情況下，獲取新的協調技能，同時重用先前學習的技能。為了解決這一挑戰，我們提出了Conquer，一個語義技能庫框架，將持續的多四足協調公式化為檢索-適應-更新過程。首先，為了適應不同任務中的隊伍大小，我們設計了一個團隊結構的自我盟友目標（SAG）骨幹，通過明確建模每個機器人的自身狀態、隊友上下文和任務目標，支持可變基數的機器人隊伍。對於每個進來的任務，Conquer從執行前信息中構建任務級語義描述符，並從庫中檢索相關技能進行適應。在成功執行後，Conquer通過提取軌跡級語義描述符並根據語義距離進行組織來更新技能庫，從而實現持續的技能積累和跨任務知識轉移。模擬實驗顯示，Conquer達到了95.6%的最終平均成功率，展現出強大的前向轉移和微不足道的災難性遺忘。在Unitree Go2團隊上的實際應用進一步驗證了Conquer在實際多四足協調中的部署可行性。模擬和真實機器人演示視頻可在以下網址查看：https://conquer-project.pages.dev/。

##### **vla.cpp: A Unified Inference Runtime for Vision-Language-Action Models**
2606.08094v1 by Khanh D. Nguyen, Hung T. Ho, Chinh T. Nguyen, Thanh Q. Duong, Linh D. Le, Duy M. H. Nguyen, Vien A. Ngo, An T. Le

Vision-Language-Action (VLA) policies are typically shipped as Python/PyTorch stacks that assume a workstation-class GPU, a mismatch for the hardware on which robots actually run. We present vla.cpp, a portable C++ inference runtime built on llama.cpp. To our knowledge, it is the first ggml-class engine to natively serve the flow-matching and diffusion VLA inference pattern, in which a cached vision-language prefix is consumed by a cross-attending action expert integrated over several solver steps. A single runtime serves seven architectures spanning five backbone and four action-head families behind one request/response protocol, with each model packaged as a self-contained bundle. On LIBERO-Object, the engine matches a state-of-the-art checkpoint to within one episode out of 200, and runs BitVLA at 100% success in 1.3 GiB of memory. The same bundle runs unchanged across three hardware tiers, from a consumer GPU down to an 8 GB embedded module. A cross-hardware roofline analysis shows that batch-1 VLA inference is compute-bound, so utilization rather than bandwidth is the deployment lever; an IMMA ladder GEMM derived from this analysis cuts BitVLA per-step latency by 4.5x. We then frame an on-robot stress test on an ALOHA arm that isolates the latency constraint under which a learned VLA must replan against a moving target on the hardware it was trained for. Code, demo videos, and the reproducible benchmark scaffold are available at https://fai-modelopt-tech.github.io/vla-cpp.github.io/.

摘要：視覺-語言-行動 (VLA) 策略通常作為 Python/PyTorch 堆疊發佈，假設使用工作站級別的 GPU，這與機器人實際運行的硬體不符。我們提出了 vla.cpp，一個基於 llama.cpp 的可攜式 C++ 推理運行時。據我們所知，它是第一個 ggml 類引擎，能夠原生支持流匹配和擴散 VLA 推理模式，其中一個緩存的視覺-語言前綴被跨注意的行動專家在幾個求解步驟中整合使用。單一運行時支持七種架構，涵蓋五個主幹和四個行動頭系列，並且在一個請求/響應協議下運行，每個模型被打包為一個獨立的捆綁包。在 LIBERO-Object 上，該引擎在 200 次回合中匹配了一個最先進的檢查點，並在 1.3 GiB 的內存中以 100% 的成功率運行 BitVLA。相同的捆綁包在三個硬體層級上運行不變，從消費者 GPU 到 8 GB 嵌入式模組。跨硬體的 roofline 分析顯示，批次 1 的 VLA 推理是計算受限的，因此利用率而非帶寬是部署的槓桿；基於此分析的 IMMA 梯形 GEMM 將 BitVLA 每步延遲減少了 4.5 倍。然後，我們在 ALOHA 手臂上框定了一個機器人壓力測試，該測試隔離了學習的 VLA 必須在其訓練的硬體上對移動目標重新規劃的延遲約束。代碼、演示視頻和可重現的基準架構可在 https://fai-modelopt-tech.github.io/vla-cpp.github.io/ 獲得。

##### **A Multi-modal Agentic Co-pilot for Evidence Grounded Computational Pathology**
2606.08093v1 by Zhe Xu, Zhengyu Zhang, Zhiyuan Cai, Jiahao Xu, Yijie Lin, Ziyi Liu, Junlin Hou, Hongyi Wang, Yuxiang Nie, Ling Liang, Yihui Wang, Yingxue Xu, Ronald Cheong Kin Chan, Li Liang, Hao Chen

Pathology is the cornerstone of modern medicine, where accurate decision-making relies heavily on evidence-based practices. While artificial intelligence (AI) has the potential to transform clinical workflows, the intersection of AI and evidence-based medicine remains under-explored, with primitive attempts restricted to text-only general medicine. In this work, we present PathPocket, a multimodal AI agentic co-pilot designed specifically for evidence grounded pathology. We construct the most comprehensive pathology evidence corpus to date, encompassing approximately 110,472 public and authorized documents structured across a rigorous hierarchy of evidence from clinical guideline to expert opinion. From this meticulously graded foundation, we build a large-scale multimodal pathology hypergraph containing over 4.55 million entities and 7.10 million relations. Serving as a robust knowledge engine, this hypergraph provides traceable evidence for a collaborative multi-agent reasoning framework integrating input understanding, evidence retrieval, filtering, and diagnosis generation. This enables PathPocket to seamlessly resolve a wide spectrum of clinical tasks, ranging from text-only queries to complex multimodal diagnostics involving region-of-interest (ROI) and gigapixel whole-slide images (WSIs). We rigorously evaluate the system on a multidimensional benchmark of over 200,000 real-world cases, where it significantly outperforms existing state-of-the-arts. Crucially, extensive user studies demonstrate that PathPocket substantially improves the diagnostic accuracy and confidence of pathologists. By directly grounding pathology interpretations in verifiable literature, PathPocket offers a practical and scalable solution for the future of evidence grounded computational pathology.

摘要：病理學是現代醫學的基石，準確的決策高度依賴於基於證據的實踐。雖然人工智慧（AI）有潛力改變臨床工作流程，但AI與基於證據的醫學的交集仍然未被充分探討，早期的嘗試僅限於文字型的一般醫學。在這項工作中，我們介紹了PathPocket，一個專為基於證據的病理學設計的多模態AI代理助手。我們構建了迄今為止最全面的病理證據語料庫，涵蓋約110,472份公共和授權文件，這些文件按照從臨床指導到專家意見的嚴格證據層級進行結構化。基於這一經過仔細評估的基礎，我們建立了一個大型多模態病理超圖，包含超過455萬個實體和710萬個關係。作為一個強大的知識引擎，這個超圖為一個協作的多代理推理框架提供可追溯的證據，該框架整合了輸入理解、證據檢索、過濾和診斷生成。這使得PathPocket能夠無縫解決廣泛的臨床任務，從僅限於文字的查詢到涉及感興趣區域（ROI）和千兆像素全切片圖像（WSIs）的複雜多模態診斷。我們在超過200,000個真實案例的多維基準上對系統進行了嚴格評估，結果顯著超越了現有的最先進技術。至關重要的是，廣泛的用戶研究表明，PathPocket顯著提高了病理學家的診斷準確性和信心。通過將病理解釋直接基於可驗證的文獻，PathPocket為基於證據的計算病理學的未來提供了一個實用且可擴展的解決方案。

##### **"I understand your perspective": LLM Persuasion and Sycophancy through the Lens of Communicative Action Theory**
2606.08076v1 by Esra Dönmez, Agnieszka Falenska

Large Language Models (LLMs) can generate high-quality arguments, yet their ability to engage in nuanced and persuasive communicative actions remains largely unexplored. This work explores the persuasive potential of LLMs through the framework of Jürgen Habermas' Theory of Communicative Action. It examines whether LLMs express illocutionary intent (i.e., pragmatic functions of language such as conveying knowledge, building trust, or signaling similarity) in ways that are comparable to human communication. We simulate online discussions between opinion holders and LLMs using conversations from the persuasive subreddit ChangeMyView. We then compare the likelihood of illocutionary intents in human-written and LLM-generated counter-arguments, specifically those that successfully changed the original poster's view. We find that all three LLMs effectively convey illocutionary intent -- often more so than humans -- potentially increasing their anthropomorphism. Further, LLMs craft sycophantic responses that closely align with the opinion holder's intent, a strategy strongly associated with opinion change. Finally, crowd-sourced workers find LLM-generated counter-arguments more agreeable and consistently prefer them over human-written ones. These findings suggest that LLMs' persuasive power extends beyond merely generating high-quality arguments. On the contrary, training LLMs with human preferences effectively tunes them to mirror human communication patterns, particularly nuanced communicative actions, potentially increasing individuals' susceptibility to their influence.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）能夠生成高品質的論點，但它們在進行細緻且具說服力的溝通行為方面的能力仍然大多未被探索。這項工作透過尤爾根·哈貝馬斯的交往行動理論框架探討LLMs的說服潛力。它檢視LLMs是否以可與人類溝通相提並論的方式表達語言的意圖行為（即傳遞知識、建立信任或傳達相似性等語言的實用功能）。我們使用來自說服性子版面ChangeMyView的對話模擬意見持有者與LLMs之間的在線討論。然後，我們比較人類撰寫的反駁論點與LLM生成的反駁論點中意圖行為的可能性，特別是那些成功改變原始發帖者觀點的論點。我們發現所有三個LLMs有效地傳達意圖行為——通常比人類更為有效——這可能增加它們的人性化。此外，LLMs製作的奉承性回應與意見持有者的意圖緊密對齊，這是一種與觀點改變強烈相關的策略。最後，眾包工作者發現LLM生成的反駁論點更具可接受性，並且始終偏好這些論點而非人類撰寫的論點。這些發現表明，LLMs的說服力超越了僅僅生成高品質論點。相反，使用人類偏好訓練LLMs有效地調整它們以模仿人類的溝通模式，特別是細緻的溝通行為，這可能增加個體對其影響的敏感性。

##### **SurgiQ: A Large-Scale Multi-Domain Benchmark for Evaluating Surgical Understanding in Large Language Models**
2606.08071v1 by Ayah Al-Naji, Edoardo Fazzari, Saif Alkindi, Hamdan Alhadhrami, Preslav Nakov, Cesare Stefanini

Reliable evaluation of large language models in surgery remains underdeveloped. Broad medical benchmarks test clinical knowledge, while surgery requires procedural reasoning, management trade-offs, negation handling, and selection among plausible operative decisions. We present SurgiQ, a text-only, source-grounded benchmark of 13,055 four-option multiple-choice questions spanning six surgical domains and four question formats: case-based, reasoning, best-option, and negative. SurgiQ is constructed from surgical textbooks, open-access papers, and examination material using a multi-stage generation, verification, and expert-audit pipeline. We evaluate 35 open-weight LLMs under a unified log-likelihood protocol. Our results show substantial remaining headroom: smaller models often remain near the 25\% random baseline, while the best model reaches 68.1\% accuracy. General-purpose models, especially Qwen2.5, outperform most biomedical models, suggesting that current medical specialization does not yet provide sufficiently broad surgical coverage. Calibration and error analysis further show that even strong models make confident mistakes on clinically plausible distractors, motivating more reliable and broader surgical LLM evaluation.

摘要：可靠的手術大型語言模型評估仍然不夠成熟。廣泛的醫學基準測試臨床知識，而手術則需要程序推理、管理權衡、否定處理和在合理的手術決策之間進行選擇。我們提出了SurgiQ，一個僅限文本的、基於來源的基準，包含13,055道四選一的多選題，涵蓋六個手術領域和四種問題格式：案例基礎、推理、最佳選擇和否定。SurgiQ是從手術教科書、開放獲取的論文和考試材料中構建的，使用多階段生成、驗證和專家審核流程。我們在統一的對數似然協議下評估了35個開放權重的LLM。我們的結果顯示出相當大的提升空間：較小的模型通常接近25\%的隨機基線，而最佳模型達到了68.1\%的準確率。通用模型，特別是Qwen2.5，超越了大多數生物醫學模型，這表明當前的醫學專業化尚未提供足夠廣泛的手術覆蓋。校準和錯誤分析進一步顯示，即使是強大的模型在臨床上合理的干擾項上也會自信地犯錯，這促使我們進行更可靠和更廣泛的手術LLM評估。

##### **OSMGraphCLIP: Learning Global Location Representations from OpenStreetMap Graphs**
2606.08046v1 by Dimitrios Michail, Eleni Saka, Ioannis Giannopoulos, Ioannis Papoutsis

We present OSMGraphCLIP, a CLIP-style geospatial representation model that learns global location embeddings from freely available OpenStreetMap (OSM) data. OSMGraphCLIP represents geographic environments as heterogeneous graphs of typed OSM features, preserving the topological and semantic relationships among roads, buildings, land-use regions, and points of interest. A multi-scale graph encoder captures both fine-grained local structure and broader landscape composition, and supervises a spherical-harmonics location encoder through a contrastive alignment objective. We evaluate OSMGraphCLIP across a diverse suite of downstream geospatial regression and classification tasks spanning climate, ecology, socioeconomic indicators, public health, land cover, biodiversity, and wildfire forecasting, and show that structured OSM data alone supports strong global location representations across domains. OSMGraphCLIP matches or exceeds satellite-based baselines on the majority of benchmarks, with the most pronounced advantage on socioeconomic and public-health tasks, where OSM's explicit semantic annotation of the built environment encodes patterns of human activity that satellite pixels can only capture indirectly. On ecological and environmental tasks, the model remains closely competitive with imagery-based methods despite using no Earth observation data. Qualitative analysis confirms that the learned embeddings organize geographic space coherently, recovering biome boundaries, urban gradients, and tropical--temperate distinctions from map topology alone.

摘要：我們提出了OSMGraphCLIP，一種CLIP風格的地理空間表示模型，從自由可用的OpenStreetMap (OSM) 數據中學習全球位置嵌入。OSMGraphCLIP將地理環境表示為異質圖，包含類型化的OSM特徵，保留了道路、建築、土地使用區域和興趣點之間的拓撲和語義關係。多尺度圖編碼器捕捉細緻的局部結構和更廣泛的景觀組成，並通過對比對齊目標來監督球面調和位置編碼器。我們在多樣的下游地理空間回歸和分類任務上評估OSMGraphCLIP，這些任務涵蓋氣候、生態、社會經濟指標、公共健康、土地覆蓋、生物多樣性和野火預測，並顯示僅使用結構化的OSM數據就能在各個領域支持強大的全球位置表示。OSMGraphCLIP在大多數基準測試中與衛星基準相匹配或超越，尤其在社會經濟和公共健康任務上表現最為明顯，因為OSM對建成環境的明確語義註釋編碼了人類活動的模式，而衛星像素只能間接捕捉這些模式。在生態和環境任務上，該模型儘管不使用任何地球觀測數據，仍然與基於影像的方法保持密切競爭。定性分析證實，學習到的嵌入能夠一致地組織地理空間，僅通過地圖拓撲恢復生物群落邊界、城市梯度和熱帶—溫帶的區分。

##### **SafeECGMatch: Calibration-Aware Joint Frequency and Time Space Semi-Supervised Learning for Open-Set ECG Classification**
2606.08037v1 by Hongkyu Koh, Ikbeom Jang

Electrocardiogram (ECG) classification models often suffer from severe label scarcity, making semi-supervised learning (SSL) an attractive strategy for reducing annotation costs. In clinical settings, however, unlabeled pools frequently contain out-of-distribution (OOD) anomalies or diagnostic groups absent from the labeled set. Standard SSL forces incorrect pseudo-labels onto these unseen classes, producing overconfident predictions. To address this, we propose SafeECGMatch, a calibration-aware safe SSL framework for single-label ECG classification under label distribution mismatch. Methodologically, SafeECGMatch employs a dual-branch architecture extracting time-frequency latent representations via ECG-specific augmentations. Crucially, it dynamically aligns confidence with empirical accuracy through adaptive label smoothing and temperature scaling, calibrating both the multiclass classifier and the OOD detector across temporal and spectral domains. This joint optimization allows trustworthy OOD rejection and reliable pseudo-labeling. Evaluated on the PTB-XL and PhysioNet/CinC Challenge benchmarks, SafeECGMatch achieves state-of-the-art accuracy and calibration, advancing reliable knowledge discovery in physiological time-series. Code is available at https://github.com/labhai/SafeECGMatch.

摘要：心電圖（ECG）分類模型常常面臨標籤稀缺的問題，使得半監督學習（SSL）成為降低標註成本的吸引策略。<lb/>然而，在臨床環境中，未標註的數據池經常包含分佈外（OOD）異常或缺失於標註集的診斷組。<lb/>標準的SSL強制將不正確的偽標籤強加於這些未見的類別，導致過度自信的預測。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們提出了SafeECGMatch，這是一個考慮校準的安全SSL框架，適用於標籤分佈不匹配的單標籤ECG分類。<lb/>在方法論上，SafeECGMatch採用雙分支架構，通過ECG特定的增強技術提取時間-頻率潛在表示。<lb/>關鍵在於，它通過自適應標籤平滑和溫度縮放，動態地將信心與經驗準確性對齊，對多類別分類器和OOD檢測器進行校準，涵蓋時間和頻譜領域。<lb/>這種聯合優化允許可靠的OOD拒絕和可信的偽標註。<lb/>在PTB-XL和PhysioNet/CinC挑戰基準上評估，SafeECGMatch實現了最先進的準確性和校準，推進了生理時間序列中的可靠知識發現。<lb/>代碼可在 https://github.com/labhai/SafeECGMatch 獲得。

##### **GIScholarBench: Benchmarking LLM Overconfidence in GIS Research**
2606.08036v1 by Zongrng Li, Mingzheng Yang, Lei Zou, Hongxu Ma, Hao Tian, Siqi Zhou, Wenjing Gong, Kaili Zhang, Bingqian Chen, Mitch Zhang, Yifan Yang

Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used in academic research workflows, but scholarly tasks require high factual precision and therefore expose a key weakness: overconfidence. Here, overconfidence is defined behaviorally as the tendency to produce confident, assertive, and well-formatted outputs even when the underlying knowledge is incomplete or unverifiable, rather than as a calibration gap between stated confidence and accuracy. To examine this issue, we introduce GIScholarBench, a benchmark built from 10,865 papers published in 25 core GIScience journals between 2020 and 2025. The benchmark covers three tasks with increasing cognitive complexity: metadata retrieval, literature linking, and research direction generation. We evaluate Claude Sonnet 4.5, Gemini 3, and ChatGPT 5.3 through their native web interfaces under real-world user-facing conditions. Results show consistent overconfidence across all tasks. In metadata retrieval, ChatGPT 5.3 achieves the highest accuracy, but all models still generate definitive titles and DOIs when predictions are wrong. In literature linking, Claude Sonnet 4.5 recovers the most references, but all models show a clear gap between top-ranked retrieval and longer citation lists, suggesting that references are extended beyond reliable retrieval capacity. In research direction generation, AI-generated directions show lower topic coverage, higher novel miss rates, and lower semantic diversity than real future-citing papers. These findings suggest that LLM overconfidence is task-invariant but takes different forms: factual overgeneration in retrieval, unreliable citation expansion in literature linking, and overconfidence in output completeness during research ideation.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在學術研究工作流程中越來越常被使用，但學術任務需要高事實精確度，因此暴露出一個關鍵弱點：過度自信。在這裡，過度自信被行為上定義為即使基礎知識不完整或無法驗證，仍然產生自信、果斷且格式良好的輸出，而不是陳述的自信與準確性之間的校準差距。為了檢驗這個問題，我們介紹了GIScholarBench，這是一個基於2020年至2025年間在25本核心地理資訊科學期刊上發表的10,865篇論文建立的基準。該基準涵蓋了三個具有逐步增加的認知複雜性的任務：元數據檢索、文獻鏈接和研究方向生成。我們通過其原生網頁介面在真實的用戶面對條件下評估Claude Sonnet 4.5、Gemini 3和ChatGPT 5.3。結果顯示所有任務中均存在一致的過度自信。在元數據檢索中，ChatGPT 5.3達到了最高的準確率，但所有模型在預測錯誤時仍然生成確定的標題和DOI。在文獻鏈接中，Claude Sonnet 4.5恢復了最多的參考文獻，但所有模型在排名最高的檢索和較長的引用列表之間顯示出明顯的差距，這表明參考文獻的擴展超出了可靠檢索的能力。在研究方向生成中，AI生成的方向顯示出較低的主題覆蓋率、更高的新穎遺漏率以及較低的語義多樣性，與真正的未來引用論文相比。這些發現表明，LLM的過度自信是任務不變的，但表現出不同的形式：在檢索中事實過度生成，在文獻鏈接中不可靠的引用擴展，以及在研究構思過程中對輸出完整性的過度自信。

##### **Summarization is Not Dead Yet**
2606.08000v1 by Dongqi Liu, Chenxi Whitehouse, Zheng Zhao, Zhuchen Cao, Jian Li, Yabiao Wang

The progress of large language models (LLMs) has fueled claims that model-generated summaries rival or even surpass human-written references, raising questions about whether summarization remains an open research problem. We re-examine this narrative through a multi-track evaluation covering five diverse datasets and five state-of-the-art LLMs, combining controlled human assessment, bias-mitigated LLM-as-Judge protocols, factuality verification against external knowledge, and corpus-level linguistic analysis. Our findings reveal a more nuanced landscape in which human reference summaries continue to demonstrate advantages in informativeness and faithfulness, whereas LLM outputs are preferred mainly for surface-level coherence and fluency. Factuality verification indicates that human references remain more reliable, particularly for claims involving reasoning or synthesis, and linguistic analysis uncovers a pattern of stylistic homogeneity across different models. These observations suggest that current LLMs have raised the floor of summarization quality, but the ceiling of their performance remains below human capabilities.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）的進展引發了模型生成的摘要與人類撰寫的參考資料相媲美甚至超越的說法，這引發了關於摘要是否仍然是一個開放研究問題的疑問。<lb/>我們通過一項多軌評估重新檢視這一敘事，涵蓋五個多樣化的數據集和五個最先進的LLMs，結合了受控的人類評估、減少偏見的LLM作為評判者的協議、對外部知識的事實驗證，以及語料庫層面的語言分析。<lb/>我們的研究結果揭示了一個更為細緻的格局，在這個格局中，人類參考摘要在信息量和忠實度方面仍然顯示出優勢，而LLM的輸出主要在表面的一致性和流暢性上受到青睞。<lb/>事實驗證顯示，人類參考資料在可靠性方面仍然更高，特別是對於涉及推理或綜合的主張，而語言分析則揭示了不同模型之間的風格同質性模式。<lb/>這些觀察表明，當前的LLMs提高了摘要質量的底線，但它們的性能上限仍低於人類的能力。

##### **MechLens: Late Crystallization of Factual Knowledge Explains Intervention Effectiveness in Language Models**
2606.07978v1 by Xueping Gao

Understanding where LLMs store factual knowledge is critical for hallucination mitigation. We systematically quantify Late Crystallization: factual knowledge does not gradually emerge across layers but "crystallizes" abruptly at the final layers. Across five model families (Pythia, Gemma, Qwen2.5, Llama-3.1, Mistral; 0.5--14B), 26.8%--93.4% of correct answers never enter top-10 predictions at any intermediate layer, with late emergence (>80% depth) consistent across architectures. Cross-scale (Qwen2.5-14B) and cross-benchmark (MMLU: 98.2%) results confirm generality; tuned lens rules out probe artifacts. A sentiment-classification control (0.5% for Qwen vs. 85.9% factual; 2.0% for Mistral vs. 26.8%) confirms the phenomenon is specific to factual recall.
  Late Crystallization yields a crystallization-guided intervention principle: CAA outperforms DoLa on moderate-crystallization models (Llama, Mistral; p<0.001), with a directionally consistent reversal on high-crystallization Qwen (+25.4% vs. +15.5% MC1, p=0.069). LayerNorm ablation shows crystallization is intrinsic to the residual stream; LN scaling (x1.2) yields +11.8% MC1 with zero inference overhead. We further reveal a Computability-Memorization Spectrum: computable knowledge crystallizes earlier (layer 22.1/28) than memorized facts (28.0/28). We release MechLens supporting five model families.

摘要：理解大型語言模型（LLMs）儲存事實知識的位置對於減少幻覺是至關重要的。<lb/>我們系統性地量化了晚期結晶：事實知識並不是在各層之間逐漸出現，而是在最後幾層中突然“結晶”。<lb/>在五個模型家族（Pythia、Gemma、Qwen2.5、Llama-3.1、Mistral；0.5--14B）中，26.8%--93.4%的正確答案在任何中間層中都從未進入前10名預測，晚期出現（&gt;80%深度）在各架構中是一致的。<lb/>跨尺度（Qwen2.5-14B）和跨基準（MMLU：98.2%）的結果確認了普遍性；調整的鏡頭排除了探測伪影。<lb/>情感分類控制（Qwen的0.5%對比事實的85.9%；Mistral的2.0%對比26.8%）確認了這一現象是特定於事實回憶的。<lb/>晚期結晶產生了一個以結晶為指導的干預原則：CAA在中度結晶模型（Llama、Mistral；p&lt;0.001）上優於DoLa，在高結晶的Qwen上有一個方向一致的逆轉（+25.4%對比+15.5% MC1，p=0.069）。<lb/>LayerNorm消融顯示結晶是殘差流的內在特性；LN縮放（x1.2）在沒有推理開銷的情況下產生了+11.8% MC1。<lb/>我們進一步揭示了一個可計算性-記憶光譜：可計算知識比記憶事實更早結晶（層22.1/28對比28.0/28）。<lb/>我們發布了MechLens，支持五個模型家族。

##### **Unification of Closed-Open Industrial Detection Scenarios: New Large-Scale Benchmarks,Challenges and Baselines**
2606.07953v1 by Zekai Zhang, Jinglin Zhang, Qinghui Chen, Gang Li, Da Chen, Shuainan Jing, He Wang, Dagang Li, Cong Liu, Cong Bai, Shengyong Chen

Large-scale Visual-Language Models (LVLMs) have achieved remarkable success in natural visual tasks, yet their application to industrial defect detection remains challenging due to two fundamental limitations: (i) the scarcity of large-scale industrial datasets that cover diverse defect categories across multiple domains, and (ii) the reliance on manual prompts (points, boxes, masks) that introduce subjective noise and lack text-visual interaction for fine-grained understanding. To address these challenges, we introduce a Large-Scale Multi-Modal Industrial Open-Closed benchmark (MMIOC-1M) containing over one million samples across $14$ super-categories, $29$ industrial scenes, and $351$ defect subcategories. To our knowledge, MMIOC-1M is the first unified largest benchmark supporting both open-vocabulary and closed-set industrial detection, providing valuable pre-training data for LVLMs in industrial scenarios. Furthermore, we propose a Refined Text-Visual Prompt Network (RTVPNet) that incorporates three key innovations: (1) an expert-assisted domain projection mechanism that enables rapid adaptation of general vision models to industrial domains, (2) an energy-based sparse sampling strategy that automatically generates refined visual prompts without manual intervention, and (3) a bidirectional text-visual interaction module that enhances cross-modal semantic alignment and understanding. Extensive experiments demonstrate that RTVPNet achieves state-of-the-art performance on MMIOC-1M, LVIS, and COCO benchmarks while maintaining computational efficiency. The dataset and code are available at https://github.com/hellozzk/MMIO.

摘要：大型視覺語言模型（LVLMs）在自然視覺任務中取得了顯著的成功，但其在工業缺陷檢測中的應用仍然面臨挑戰，主要有兩個根本限制：（i）缺乏涵蓋多個領域中各種缺陷類別的大型工業數據集，以及（ii）依賴手動提示（點、框、面具），這引入了主觀噪音，並且缺乏文本與視覺的互動以進行細緻理解。為了解決這些挑戰，我們介紹了一個大型多模態工業開放-封閉基準（MMIOC-1M），其中包含超過一百萬個樣本，涵蓋$14$個超類別、$29$個工業場景和$351$個缺陷子類別。據我們所知，MMIOC-1M是第一個支持開放詞彙和封閉集工業檢測的統一最大基準，為LVLMs在工業場景中提供了有價值的預訓練數據。此外，我們提出了一個精煉文本-視覺提示網絡（RTVPNet），該網絡包含三個關鍵創新：（1）一個專家輔助的領域投影機制，使得通用視覺模型能夠快速適應工業領域，（2）一種基於能量的稀疏採樣策略，自動生成精煉的視覺提示而無需手動干預，以及（3）一個雙向文本-視覺互動模塊，增強跨模態的語義對齊和理解。大量實驗表明，RTVPNet在MMIOC-1M、LVIS和COCO基準上達到了最先進的性能，同時保持了計算效率。數據集和代碼可在 https://github.com/hellozzk/MMIO 獲得。

##### **Larch: Learned Query Optimization for Semantic Predicates**
2606.07923v1 by Fuheng Zhao, Pawel Liskowski, Zihan Li, Benjamin Han, Puxuan Yu, Varich Boonsanong, Dimitris Tsirogiannis, Anupam Datta

With the advent of Large Language Models (LLMs), many database systems introduced semantic operators that enabled analytical queries over unstructured data (e.g. text, images, videos). Semantic operators typically incur high inference costs and latencies making semantic (AI) SQL queries challenging to apply on large scale datasets. At the same time, their semantic nature leads database engines to treat them as black boxes, making AISQL queries difficult to optimize. In this paper, we introduce Larch, a framework for optimizing the execution of semantic filters in AI SQL queries. Larch was inspired by two key observations: i) the high latency of semantic operators leaves significant room for computationally-heavy runtime optimization techniques, ii) unstructured data are typically accompanied by semantic information in the form of embeddings allowing for efficient semantic comparisons between AI_FILTER prompts and data values. Based on these two key observations, we present two Larch variants: Larch-A2C and Larch-Sel. Larch-A2C encodes arbitrary semantic filters expression tree using an embedding-augmented Gated Graph Neural Network and formulates the filter evaluation order as a Markov decision process. In contrast, Larch-Sel leverages a supervised learning model to predict filter selectivities, subsequently applying dynamic programming to find a near-optimal evaluation order for each input row. Evaluated across diverse real-world datasets and comprehensive synthetic workloads, both Larch variants always outperform existing semantic filter optimization techniques in terms of token usage. Our results demonstrate that Larch is robust across diverse workloads, reducing total token cost overhead by 3x-19x compared to Palimpzest and Quest.

摘要：隨著大型語言模型（LLMs）的出現，許多資料庫系統引入了語義運算子，使得對非結構化數據（例如文本、圖像、視頻）的分析查詢成為可能。語義運算子通常會產生高推理成本和延遲，這使得在大規模數據集上應用語義（AI）SQL 查詢變得具有挑戰性。與此同時，它們的語義特性使得資料庫引擎將其視為黑箱，這使得優化 AISQL 查詢變得困難。在本文中，我們介紹了 Larch，一個用於優化 AI SQL 查詢中語義過濾器執行的框架。Larch 的靈感來自兩個關鍵觀察：i) 語義運算子的高延遲留下了大量的計算密集型運行時優化技術的空間，ii) 非結構化數據通常伴隨著以嵌入形式存在的語義信息，這使得 AI_FILTER 提示與數據值之間的語義比較變得高效。基於這兩個關鍵觀察，我們提出了兩個 Larch 變體：Larch-A2C 和 Larch-Sel。Larch-A2C 使用嵌入增強的門控圖神經網絡編碼任意語義過濾器表達樹，並將過濾器評估順序公式化為馬爾可夫決策過程。相對而言，Larch-Sel 利用監督學習模型來預測過濾器的選擇性，隨後應用動態規劃為每個輸入行找到近似最優的評估順序。在多樣的現實世界數據集和全面的合成工作負載中評估，兩個 Larch 變體在令牌使用方面始終優於現有的語義過濾器優化技術。我們的結果顯示，Larch 在各種工作負載中都表現穩健，與 Palimpzest 和 Quest 相比，總令牌成本開銷減少了 3 倍至 19 倍。

##### **Beyond Pass/Fail: Using Process Mining to Understand How LLMs Resist (and Fail) Red Team Attacks**
2606.07833v1 by Zvi Topol

Standard AI red teaming evaluations reduce adversarial campaigns to a single binary outcome, attack success rate (ASR), not taking into account the sequential structure of how models resist or yield to attacks. We propose applying process mining, a discipline for discovering and analyzing process models from event logs, to red teaming traces. We conduct a controlled experiment pitting 60 HarmBench prompts against two LLMs, GPT-OSS 120B and Llama 3.3 70B, using 10 prompt mutation strategies over up to 110 attempts per prompt. From the resulting 8,575 scored events we extract Directly-Follows Graphs (DFGs) and state transition matrices that reveal structurally distinct defense profiles invisible to ASR alone: GPT-OSS exhibits a near-absorbing refusal state, while Llama presents multiple porous escape routes from refusal to getting successfully jailbroken. We further show that mutator effectiveness is asymmetric across models and that time-to-jailbreak distributions differ by an order of magnitude.

摘要：標準的人工智慧紅隊評估將對抗性攻擊活動簡化為單一的二元結果，即攻擊成功率（ASR），而未考慮模型抵抗或屈從於攻擊的序列結構。我們建議將過程挖掘應用於紅隊追蹤，這是一門從事件日誌中發現和分析過程模型的學科。我們進行了一項受控實驗，將60個HarmBench提示與兩個大型語言模型（LLMs）對抗，分別是GPT-OSS 120B和Llama 3.3 70B，使用10種提示變異策略，對每個提示進行最多110次嘗試。從結果中獲得的8,575個評分事件中，我們提取了直接後續圖（DFGs）和狀態轉換矩陣，揭示了僅通過ASR無法察覺的結構性防禦特徵：GPT-OSS顯示出近乎吸收的拒絕狀態，而Llama則呈現多條從拒絕到成功越獄的多孔逃逸路徑。我們進一步顯示，變異器的有效性在不同模型之間是不對稱的，且越獄所需的時間分佈相差一個數量級。

##### **Scaling Participation in Modular AI Systems**
2606.07812v1 by Shangbin Feng, Yike Wang, Weijia Shi, Luke Zettlemoyer, Yejin Choi, Yulia Tsvetkov

Humanity is a mosaic of multifaceted talents and needs, and any truly intelligent AI must reflect that richness. Yet the LLMs used by all are built by the few -- a centralized market of monolithic AI models structurally ill-suited to capture the diversity of human knowledge, reasoning, and values. Here we introduce scaling participation, a new paradigm in which modular AI systems are built from the bottom up through the contributions of diverse stakeholders. Participants contribute small models trained on their own interests and priorities; these models then collaborate in modular frameworks as compositional AI systems. Participatory AI systems outperform monolithic LLMs by up to 15.4% across 15 tasks, such as reasoning and factuality, surpassing models larger than all contributed components combined. Further experiments show that participatory AI systems benefit from contributor diversity, substantially improve on each contributor's original priorities, and exhibit emergent capabilities that allow them to solve over 15% of problems where all individual models fail. Scaling participation provides a technical foundation for transitioning from the monolithic status quo toward an open, bottom-up, and collaborative AI future.

##### **Evaluating RAG Reliability under Clean, Misleading, and Mixed Retrieval**
2606.07783v1 by Sevgi Yigit-Sert

Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) is widely used to improve the factual reliability of large language models (LLMs) by grounding answers in retrieved evidence. In misinformation-rich environments, however, retrieved content may include plausible but incorrect information, raising concerns about the reliability of RAG-based information access systems.
  In this work, we propose an evaluation protocol to systematically test how the RAG system handles conflicts between parametric knowledge and evidence retrieved from context with varying amounts of misleading information. We target correct answers to factoid questions that the model responds to correctly, even when there is no retrieval, and use this to test the system with clean, poisoned, and mixed evidence.
  The proposed analytical framework combines parametric override and confidence metrics to assess when and how misleading information affects the generation process of LLMs. This study aims to provide insights into the robustness of RAG systems in information disorder scenarios.

摘要：檢索增強生成（RAG）被廣泛用於提高大型語言模型（LLMs）的事實可靠性，通過將答案基於檢索到的證據。然而，在充滿錯誤資訊的環境中，檢索的內容可能包括看似合理但不正確的信息，這引發了對基於RAG的信息訪問系統可靠性的擔憂。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們提出了一個評估協議，以系統地測試RAG系統如何處理參數知識與從上下文中檢索到的證據之間的衝突，並且這些證據包含不同程度的誤導性信息。我們針對模型正確回答的事實性問題，即使在沒有檢索的情況下也能正確回答，並利用這一點來測試系統在乾淨、被污染和混合證據下的表現。<lb/>所提出的分析框架結合了參數覆蓋和信心指標，以評估誤導性信息何時以及如何影響LLMs的生成過程。本研究旨在提供對RAG系統在信息混亂場景中穩健性的見解。

##### **Unlocking Latent Value: Taxonomy-Guided Recovery of High-Performing Data from Low-Tier Web Corpora**
2606.07778v1 by Neeraj Varshney, Sanket Lokegaonkar, Nasser Zalmout, Qingyu Yin, Priyanka Nigam, Bing Yin

Dominant web data curation pipelines for pretraining collapse document quality into a single composite score, systematically missing high-value content along dimensions the scorer underweights. We present a taxonomy-driven framework that recovers this value by filtering along semantically meaningful dimensions that composite scores fail to capture. First, building on the ESSENTIAL-WEB taxonomy, we introduce two novel dimensions: timeliness and cultural specificity, both of which show low pairwise NMI with existing ones. We annotate 14M documents using Qwen2.5 32B and distill into a lightweight 0.5B model. To enable rapid corpus-wide annotation, we additionally train a 73M multi-task MLP on E5 embeddings, achieving 50x inference throughput. Second, to navigate the combinatorial explosion of filter configurations, we introduce a compute-efficient two-pass framework: Pass 1 identifies the strongest dimension signals at small scale; Pass 2 constructs and evaluates conjunctive and disjunctive compound filters from the top performers - identifying high-performing configurations at a fraction of full scaling-law cost. Applying the selected filters to deprioritized web data, taxonomy-filtered subsets outperform their unfiltered baselines and even surpass the highest-quality tier. On mid-tier data, our best filter improves over its unfiltered baseline by 12.1% on reasoning, 9.5% on coding, and 2.0% on knowledge benchmarks, exceeding unfiltered top-tier data by 6.7% on reasoning and 13.7% on coding. Furthermore, filtered data from two tiers below the typical production threshold improves by 22.3% on reasoning and 19.5% on coding over its unfiltered baseline, surpassing top-tier data on coding benchmarks. These results establish that vast latent value remains locked in deprioritized web data, and that multi-dimensional taxonomy filtering is a principled, compute-efficient key to unlocking it.

摘要：主導的網路數據策展管道在預訓練中將文件質量壓縮為單一的綜合分數，系統性地忽略了評分者低估的高價值內容。我們提出了一個基於分類法的框架，通過沿著綜合分數未能捕捉的語義意義維度進行篩選來恢復這一價值。首先，基於ESSENTIAL-WEB分類法，我們引入了兩個新維度：時效性和文化特異性，這兩者與現有維度的成對NMI均顯示出較低的相關性。我們使用Qwen2.5 32B對1400萬份文件進行註釋，並提煉成一個輕量級的0.5B模型。為了實現快速的全語料庫註釋，我們還在E5嵌入上訓練了一個73M的多任務MLP，實現了50倍的推理吞吐量。其次，為了應對過濾配置的組合爆炸，我們引入了一個計算高效的兩次通過框架：第一次通過在小規模下識別最強的維度信號；第二次通過從最優表現者中構建和評估聯合和非聯合的複合過濾器 - 以較低的全規模成本識別高效配置。將所選過濾器應用於被降權的網路數據，經過分類法過濾的子集在表現上超越了未過濾的基準，甚至超過了最高質量層級。在中等層級數據上，我們的最佳過濾器在推理上比其未過濾的基準提高了12.1%，在編碼上提高了9.5%，在知識基準上提高了2.0%，在推理上超過了未過濾的最高層級數據6.7%，在編碼上超過了13.7%。此外，來自典型生產閾值下兩個層級的過濾數據在推理上比其未過濾的基準提高了22.3%，在編碼上提高了19.5%，超過了編碼基準的最高層級數據。這些結果證明，巨大的潛在價值仍然鎖定在被降權的網路數據中，而多維分類法過濾是一種原則性、計算高效的鑰匙，可以解鎖這一價值。

##### **MemDreamer: Decoupling Perception and Reasoning for Long Video Understanding via Hierarchical Graph Memory and Agentic Retrieval Mechanism**
2606.07512v1 by Cong Chen, Guo Gan, Kaixiang Ji, ChaoYang Zhang, Zhen Yang, Guangming Yao, Hao Chen, Jingdong Chen, Yi Yuan, Chunhua Shen

Current Vision-Language Models struggle with hours-long videos because processing full-length visual sequences induces prohibitive token explosion and attention dilution. To overcome this, we introduce MemDreamer to decouple perception and reasoning, shifting long-video understanding into an agentic exploration process. As a plug-and-play framework, it incrementally streams videos to construct a Hierarchical Graph Memory, a top-down three-tier architecture for semantic abstraction, anchored by a foundational graph capturing spatiotemporal and causal relations. During inference, the reasoning model employs agentic tool-augmented retrieval, navigating hierarchies, searching nodes, and traversing logical edges via an Observation-Reason-Action loop. Experiments show MemDreamer achieves SOTA results across four mainstream benchmarks, narrowing the gap with human experts to only 3.7 points. It constrains the reasoning context window to merely 2% of full-context ingestion while delivering a 12.5 point absolute accuracy gain. Furthermore, statistical analysis uncovers a strong positive linear correlation between an VLM's performance on logic reasoning and long-video understanding benchmarks, establishing agentic capability scaling as a new paradigm for multimodal comprehension.

摘要：目前的視覺-語言模型在處理長達數小時的視頻時面臨困難，因為處理完整的視覺序列會導致過多的標記爆炸和注意力稀釋。為了解決這個問題，我們引入了MemDreamer來解耦感知和推理，將長視頻理解轉變為一個主動探索的過程。作為一個即插即用的框架，它逐步流式傳輸視頻以構建層次圖記憶，這是一種自上而下的三層架構，用於語義抽象，並以捕捉時空和因果關係的基礎圖為基礎。在推理過程中，推理模型利用主動工具增強檢索，導航層次結構，搜索節點，並通過觀察-推理-行動循環穿越邏輯邊緣。實驗表明，MemDreamer在四個主流基準上達到了SOTA結果，將與人類專家的差距縮小至僅3.7分。它將推理上下文窗口限制為僅2%的完整上下文攝取，同時實現了12.5分的絕對準確性增益。此外，統計分析揭示了VLM在邏輯推理和長視頻理解基準上的表現之間存在強正線性相關，確立了主動能力擴展作為多模態理解的新範式。

##### **Sparse Subspace-to-Expert Sharing for Task-Agnostic Continual Learning**
2606.07500v1 by Fatema Siddika, Md Anwar Hossen, Tanwi Mallick, Ali Jannesari

Continual learning in Large Language Models (LLMs) is hindered by the plasticity-stability dilemma, where acquiring new capabilities often leads to catastrophic forgetting of previous knowledge. Existing methods typically treat parameters uniformly, failing to distinguish between specific task knowledge and shared capabilities. We introduce Mixture of Sparse Experts for Task Agnostic Continual Learning (SETA), a framework that resolves the plasticity-stability conflict through adaptive sparse subspace decomposition into task-specific expert modules. Unlike standard updates, where tasks compete for the same parameters, SETA separates knowledge into unique experts, designed to isolate task-specific patterns, and shared experts, responsible for capturing common features. This structure is maintained through adaptive elastic anchoring and a routing-aware regularization that jointly protect shared knowledge at both the weight and routing levels and enable a unified gating network to automatically retrieve the correct expert combination during inference. Extensive experiments across diverse domain-specific benchmarks demonstrate that SETA achieves competitive or superior overall performance relative to state-of-the-art continual learning baselines, with particularly strong retention of early-task knowledge and improved backward transfer on LLaMA-2 7B and Qwen3-4B.

摘要：持續學習在大型語言模型（LLMs）中受到可塑性-穩定性困境的阻礙，獲得新能力往往導致對先前知識的災難性遺忘。現有的方法通常將參數視為均勻，未能區分特定任務知識和共享能力。我們介紹了適用於任務無關持續學習的稀疏專家混合模型（SETA），這是一個通過自適應稀疏子空間分解為特定任務專家模塊來解決可塑性-穩定性衝突的框架。與標準更新不同，任務在SET中不再競爭相同的參數，而是將知識分離為獨特的專家，旨在隔離特定任務的模式，和共享專家，負責捕捉共同特徵。這一結構通過自適應彈性錨定和路由感知正則化得以維持，這兩者共同保護權重和路由層面的共享知識，並使統一的門控網絡能夠在推理過程中自動檢索正確的專家組合。在多個特定領域基準上進行的廣泛實驗表明，SETA在整體性能上達到了與最先進的持續學習基準相當或更優的表現，特別是在早期任務知識的保留和在LLaMA-2 7B及Qwen3-4B上的改進回傳轉移方面表現強勁。

##### **How AI Agents Reshape Knowledge Work: Autonomy, Efficiency, and Scope**
2606.07489v1 by Jeremy Yang, Kate Zyskowski, Noah Yonack, Jerry Ma

Frontier AI systems are bridging the gap between intelligence and utility by shifting from conversational assistants to autonomous agents that execute tasks end to end. Using production data from Perplexity's Search and Computer products, we study this transition by examining how AI agents accelerate and reshape knowledge work. Three key empirical findings emerge. First, using sessions with near-identical initial query pairs as natural experiments for the same underlying task attempted with both products, Computer performs 26 minutes of autonomous work per user session, versus 33 seconds for Search. Computer automates task decomposition and execution that Search users might otherwise manually orchestrate and implement. As a result, Computer shifts follow-up query distribution toward higher-order work such as verification and extension. Autonomy also increases execution quality, with per-query dissatisfaction rates 55% lower on Computer than on Search. Second, due to its autonomy advantage, Computer reduces completion time from 269 to 36 minutes on matched tasks, lowering estimated time and cost by 87% and 94%, respectively, compared to humans equipped with Search alone. Third, Computer changes the scope of work that users attempt: Computer queries more often cross occupational boundaries, require higher-order cognition, draw on broader expertise, take the form of composite tasks that bundle interdependent subtasks into a single query, and unlock work activities that are essentially absent from Search usage among the same users. Together, the evidence indicates that AI agents accelerate workflows, enhance output quality, reduce costs, and expand the breadth and depth of automated work.

##### **The Masked Advantage: Uncovering Local-Language Access to Cultural Knowledge in LLMs**
2606.07422v1 by Yang Zhang, Xiao Fei, Amr Mohamed, Sarah Almeida Carneiro, Mersin Konomi, Mingmeng Geng, Ahmed Asaad, Guokan Shang, Michalis Vazirgiannis

Large language models are increasingly used to answer culturally grounded questions across languages, yet it remains unclear whether local cultural knowledge is better accessed through English or the local language. Existing evaluations face two key limitations: many rely on parallel template-based questions that may not reflect how cultural knowledge naturally appears, and raw accuracy conflates general language proficiency with language-conditioned knowledge access. We address these issues with a controlled framework built on real-world cultural questions collected from regional benchmarks and local sources. By crossing question type (culture-agnostic vs. culture-specific) with query language (English vs. local language), and estimating ability with a shared 1PL item response theory model, we separate proficiency from localized knowledge access. Across 13 locales and roughly 80 models, we find a consistent English advantage on culture-agnostic questions, indicating stronger English proficiency. However, after accounting for this proficiency gap, local languages show a positive knowledge-access advantage in nearly all locale-model settings. This advantage is often masked in raw accuracy but becomes more visible for frontier, regionally aligned, or language-adapted models. Our results suggest that weaker local-language performance does not necessarily imply weaker cultural knowledge; rather, local cultural knowledge may be more accessible through the local language but hidden by limited language proficiency.

##### **Off-Policy Evaluation with Strategic Agents via Local Disclosure**
2606.07308v1 by Kiet Q. H. Vo, Abbavaram Gowtham Reddy, Julian Rodemann, Siu Lun Chau, Krikamol Muandet

We study off-policy evaluation (OPE) under strategic behavior where decision subjects (or agents) respond to a decision maker's policy by strategically modifying their covariates. Such behavior induces a policy-dependent covariate shift, breaking the standard assumption in existing methods that covariates are exogenous to the policy. Related work addresses this challenge by imposing strong assumptions such as repeated interactions or full knowledge of agents' response behavior, substantially limiting its applicability to OPE. In contrast, we consider a one-shot OPE setting where the decision maker has only partial knowledge of the agents' response behavior. Our key insight is that disclosing local information through post-hoc explanations reveals agents' pre-strategic covariates prior to adaptation, mitigating the information loss induced by strategic behavior. Leveraging this structure, we estimate a statistical model for the agents' responses and construct a doubly robust estimator for policy value. By assuming that the agents' cost sensitivity follows a conditional log-normal distribution, we establish consistency of the proposed estimator and validate our approach empirically. More broadly, our results highlight how interaction design can mitigate information asymmetry by revealing otherwise hidden structure in agents' strategic responses.

摘要：我們研究在策略行為下的離線政策評估（OPE），其中決策主體（或代理人）通過策略性地修改其協變量來回應決策者的政策。這種行為引發了依賴政策的協變量變化，打破了現有方法中協變量與政策無關的標準假設。相關工作通過施加強假設，如重複互動或對代理人反應行為的完全了解，來應對這一挑戰，這大大限制了其在OPE中的適用性。相反，我們考慮一個一次性OPE設定，其中決策者對代理人的反應行為只有部分了解。我們的關鍵見解是，通過事後解釋披露局部信息，可以揭示代理人在適應之前的前策略協變量，從而減輕策略行為引起的信息損失。利用這一結構，我們為代理人的反應估計了一個統計模型，並構建了一個雙重穩健的政策價值估計器。通過假設代理人的成本敏感性遵循條件對數正態分佈，我們確立了所提估計器的一致性並在實證上驗證了我們的方法。更廣泛地說，我們的結果突顯了互動設計如何通過揭示代理人策略反應中隱藏的結構來減輕信息不對稱。

##### **Phun-Bench: Evaluating LLMs on Phonological Understanding in Chinese**
2606.07300v1 by Xing Yue, Yongliang Shen, Weiming Lu

Language is a vehicle for thought, intricately tied to sounds, symbols, and meaning. However, most large language model (LLM) research focuses on meaning (semantics) and symbols (spelling) while largely overlooking sounds. Existing benchmarks on LLMs' phonological abilities are either solvable through rote memorization or intertwined with other abilities, making them inadequate to measure LLMs' genuine ability in phonological understanding. Here, we present Phun-Bench, a purpose-built Chinese benchmark with diverse tasks and settings across three dimensions (Homophony, Rhyme, and Phonetic Similarity), designed to systematically evaluate LLMs' phonological understanding. Our results show that while LLMs excel at recalling correct pronunciations, they generally struggle to leverage phonological knowledge in the flexible and intuitive way that human speakers do.
