##### **MatMind: A Structure-Activity Knowledge-Driven Generative Foundation Model for Materials Science**
2606.07712v1 by Zhan'ao Yao, Boxuan Zhang, Jingyuan Shu, Xiaoyu Wu, Rongyan Wang, Linjing Li, Dajun Zeng, Yudong Yao, Tingwei Chen, Youwei Wang, Xiaolin Zhao, Jiahui Shi, Jianjun Liu

Progress in AI-driven crystal materials science has so far been carried by narrow architectures purpose-built for individual tasks -- graph neural networks for property prediction, diffusion and flow-matching models for crystal generation -- each excelling within its niche yet unable to act as a shared backbone across the full spectrum of materials problems. Generative large language models offer a fundamentally different paradigm, in which structural representation, quantitative prediction, and structure-activity reasoning can be unified within one model, but the materials community has yet to see this paradigm realized at a level competitive with established narrow specialists. Here we present MatMind, a generative foundation model purpose-built for crystal materials science under this paradigm, developed through the coordinated activation of structure-activity knowledge and physics-informed feedback within a progressive training framework -- combining structure-activity knowledge injection, a dual-head architecture that jointly trains language reasoning and numerical regression in a shared representation space, and multi-objective physics-informed reinforcement learning over stability, novelty, and structural diversity. Across three task families, MatMind attains the lowest mean absolute error on energy above hull, bulk modulus, and band gap -- surpassing graph neural network predictors purpose-built for these tasks -- reaches an S.U.N. rate of 65.3% on unconditional crystal generation, and achieves a comparable multiplicative improvement on magnetization-density-conditioned generation, where only 21 positive samples exist within over 600000 training entries. By matching or surpassing narrow specialists on their own ground while operating within a single unified model, MatMind shows that the LLM-based paradigm can serve as a viable backbone for crystal materials science going forward.

摘要：在人工智慧驅動的晶體材料科學方面，迄今為止的進展主要依賴於為特定任務而建造的狹窄架構——圖神經網絡用於性質預測，擴散和流匹配模型用於晶體生成——每個模型在其專業領域中表現出色，但無法作為一個共享的基礎來解決全範圍的材料問題。生成性大型語言模型提供了一種根本不同的範式，在這種範式中，結構表示、定量預測和結構-活性推理可以在一個模型中統一，但材料社群尚未看到這一範式在與既有狹窄專家競爭的水平上實現。這裡我們介紹 MatMind，一個專為晶體材料科學而設計的生成性基礎模型，基於這一範式開發，通過結構-活性知識和物理知識反饋的協調激活，在一個漸進的訓練框架內進行——結合結構-活性知識注入、共同訓練語言推理和數值回歸的雙頭架構，以及針對穩定性、新穎性和結構多樣性的多目標物理知識強化學習。在三個任務類別中，MatMind 在能量高於殼、體模量和能隙的平均絕對誤差上達到了最低值——超越了為這些任務專門設計的圖神經網絡預測器——在無條件晶體生成上達到了 65.3% 的 S.U.N. 率，並在磁化密度條件生成上實現了可比的乘法改進，儘管在超過 600000 條訓練條目中僅存在 21 個正樣本。通過在一個統一的模型內匹配或超越狹窄專家，MatMind 顯示出基於大型語言模型的範式可以作為未來晶體材料科學的可行基礎。

##### **Geometry of Semantic Space: Comparative Study of Discrete and Continuous Models**
2606.07183v1 by Gabriel Bounias, Sabine Ploux

This work examines the semantic geometry underlying NLP models. We compare supervised vector embeddings, such as CamemBERT, with lexical co-occurrence graphs that encode semantic relations more directly. While transformer-based embeddings achieve strong performance, their induced geometries often display unsatisfactory distributions. In contrast, graph-based models reveal a clearer and more human-readable organization of meaning. We have implemented a methodology that allows us to perform a comparative analysis either based on the structure of the graphs or based on the topology of the embeddings induced by these two approaches. The results of the comparison -- applied to the French "Great National Debate" corpus a collection of citizen contributions to the public debate -- show a similar local topology but a very different overall structure and topology. Theses findings suggest complementary perspectives between deep supervised models and graph-based models, considering a new pathway to guide neural architectures toward more stable and interpretable convergence with graphs structures.

摘要：這項工作考察了 NLP 模型背後的語義幾何。<lb/>我們比較了監督式向量嵌入，如 CamemBERT，與更直接編碼語義關係的詞彙共現圖。<lb/>儘管基於Transformer的嵌入達到了強大的性能，但它們所產生的幾何形狀往往顯示出不令人滿意的分佈。<lb/>相反，基於圖的模型顯示出更清晰且更易於人類理解的意義組織。<lb/>我們實施了一種方法論，允許我們根據圖的結構或這兩種方法所產生的嵌入的拓撲進行比較分析。<lb/>比較的結果——應用於法語的「大國民辯論」語料庫，這是一個公民對公共辯論的貢獻集合——顯示出相似的局部拓撲，但整體結構和拓撲卻截然不同。<lb/>這些發現暗示了深度監督模型和基於圖的模型之間的互補視角，考慮到一條新的途徑，以引導神經架構朝向與圖結構更穩定和可解釋的收斂。

##### **UrduMMLU: A Massive Multitask Benchmark for Urdu Language Understanding**
2606.07167v1 by Ahmer Tabassum, Sarfraz Ahmad, Hasan Iqbal, Owais Aijaz, Momina Ahsan, Preslav Nakov

Meaningful multilingual evaluation must test models in the target language and educational context. Urdu, spoken by more than 230 million people, lacks a broad MMLU-style benchmark built from native educational sources. We introduce UrduMMLU, a benchmark of 26,431 Urdu MCQs across 26 subjects and five domains, collected from native Urdu MCQ banks and public examination PDFs. Unlike translation-based resources, UrduMMLU covers both standard academic subjects and Urdu- and region-specific content. We label the exam-derived portion through dual human annotation with strict consensus filtering. We evaluate 30 LLMs under English and Urdu prompts, yielding 60 zero-shot evaluations, and further evaluate four open-source LLMs under multiple few-shot settings across both prompt languages. Gemini-3.5-Flash performs best, reaching 90.20% and 90.34% accuracy, while no other model exceeds 85%. The strongest open-source model trails by 7.79 and 8.92 points, and many models lose 25 to 40 points on Urdu-centered Humanities subjects compared with STEM. Few-shot prompting yields only modest gains. UrduMMLU shows that Urdu knowledge remains uneven in current LLMs, especially for regionally grounded content.

摘要：有意義的多語言評估必須在目標語言和教育環境中測試模型。烏爾都語由超過2.3億人使用，但缺乏基於本地教育資源建立的廣泛MMLU風格基準。我們介紹了UrduMMLU，這是一個涵蓋26個科目和五個領域的26,431個烏爾都語選擇題的基準，這些題目來自本地烏爾都語選擇題庫和公共考試PDF。與基於翻譯的資源不同，UrduMMLU涵蓋了標準學術科目以及烏爾都語和區域特定內容。我們通過雙重人工標註並嚴格共識篩選來標記考試衍生部分。我們在英語和烏爾都語提示下評估了30個LLM，產生了60個零樣本評估，並進一步在兩種提示語言下對四個開源LLM進行了多個少樣本設置的評估。Gemini-3.5-Flash表現最佳，達到90.20%和90.34%的準確率，而其他模型均未超過85%。最強的開源模型落後7.79和8.92點，許多模型在與STEM相比的烏爾都語人文科目上損失了25到40點。少樣本提示僅帶來適度的增益。UrduMMLU顯示目前的LLM在烏爾都語知識上仍然不均衡，特別是在區域性內容方面。

##### **From Privacy to Workflow Integrity: Communication-Graph Metadata in Autonomous Agent Interoperability**
2606.07150v1 by Bijaya Dangol

Agent-interoperability protocols such as A2A and MCP standardize what agents say to one another, but assume address-based transport over HTTP(S). Such transports protect message content, increasingly with end-to-end encryption. What they leave in the clear is the communication graph: which agent contacts which, when, and how often. In agent systems this graph is more consequential than a privacy framing suggests. Endpoints are often capability-labeled, workflows are structured and chained, and interactions are coupled to real actions, so an observer recovers more than past relationships. It can infer the pending workflow, the task being assembled and the action likely to follow. At machine speed, it can act on that inference before the workflow completes. The threat is therefore one of workflow integrity, not privacy alone: predictive leverage over autonomous action. We give a threat model for the agent communication graph; identify what makes agent metadata distinctively revealing (semanticity, prospectivity, actuation); define transport- and bootstrap-layer privacy properties and weigh candidate transports (SimpleX/SMP, Tor, mixnets) against them; and present an A2A case study in which a metadata-protecting binding is expressible but surfaces the protocol's identity assumptions. We test these on a generative model anchored to a real A2A capture. From passive metadata alone, with no payloads, a classifier recovers a task's class well above chance, from only the workflow's opening; applied together, the properties drive that recovery sharply back toward chance. Beyond what an observer can recover, we measure the leverage of acting on the leak: from a workflow's opening and under a fixed budget, an adversary choosing which workflows to act on realizes in this model most of a clairvoyant attacker's advantage over a metadata-blind one, and the same properties suppress it.

摘要：代理互操作性協議如 A2A 和 MCP 標準化了代理之間的交流內容，但假設基於地址的 HTTP(S) 傳輸。這些傳輸保護消息內容，越來越多地使用端到端加密。它們留下的明文是通信圖：哪個代理在何時、以何種方式聯繫哪個代理，以及聯繫的頻率。在代理系統中，這個圖比隱私框架所暗示的更具影響力。端點通常被標記為能力，工作流程是結構化和鏈接的，互動與實際行動相耦合，因此觀察者能夠恢復的不僅僅是過去的關係。它可以推斷出待處理的工作流程、正在組裝的任務以及可能隨之而來的行動。在機器速度下，它可以在工作流程完成之前根據該推斷進行行動。因此，威脅不僅僅是隱私，而是工作流程的完整性：對自主行動的預測性杠杆。我們提供了一個代理通信圖的威脅模型；確定使代理元數據具有獨特揭示性的因素（語義性、前瞻性、啟動性）；定義傳輸層和引導層的隱私屬性，並根據這些屬性權衡候選傳輸（SimpleX/SMP、Tor、混合網絡）；並呈現一個 A2A 案例研究，其中可表達的元數據保護綁定顯示了協議的身份假設。我們在一個基於真實 A2A 捕獲的生成模型上測試這些。僅從被動的元數據，沒有有效載荷，分類器能夠從工作流程的開頭準確恢復任務的類別，遠高於隨機概率；當這些屬性一起應用時，則驅動該恢復急劇回到隨機概率。超出觀察者能夠恢復的內容，我們測量了利用洩漏進行行動的杠杆：從工作流程的開頭，在固定預算下，選擇行動的對手在這個模型中實現了大部分預知攻擊者相對於盲元數據攻擊者的優勢，而相同的屬性則抑制了這種優勢。

##### **Beyond Post-hoc Explanation: Toward Glassbox AI via Probabilistic Mediation**
2606.07113v1 by Manuele Leonelli

Large language models are rapidly becoming infrastructural components in high-stakes institutional settings, including public administration, legal reasoning, and healthcare, where opacity is not merely inconvenient but institutionally and legally untenable. Existing approaches to explainability are predominantly post-hoc, offering unstable, non-contestable accounts that have no formal relationship to the reasoning process that produced the output. We argue that the problem is not the absence of explanation but the absence of structured reasoning in the first place. This paper makes the case for a fundamentally different architecture, which we call the Glassbox Framework, in which Bayesian networks serve as transparent, ante-hoc mediation layers for generative models. Bayesian networks encode domain knowledge, causal assumptions, and probabilistic dependencies before inference occurs, enabling auditable reasoning traces, uncertainty quantification, and contestable outputs. We characterise the architecture of this framework and ground it in a benefit eligibility scenario, identifying the foundational challenges spanning semantic alignment, dynamic model construction, probabilistic grounding, and human governance that must be solved to realise it at scale. By shifting from post-hoc explanation to ante-hoc probabilistic mediation, this work outlines a principled path toward AI systems that are not only powerful but fundamentally accountable.

摘要：大型語言模型正迅速成為高風險機構環境中的基礎設施組件，包括公共行政、法律推理和醫療保健，在這些領域中，不透明性不僅是個不便，而是機構上和法律上無法接受的。現有的可解釋性方法主要是事後解釋，提供不穩定、不可爭辯的說明，與產生輸出的推理過程沒有正式的關係。我們認為問題不在於缺乏解釋，而在於根本缺乏結構化的推理。本文主張一種根本不同的架構，我們稱之為玻璃盒框架，其中貝葉斯網絡作為生成模型的透明、事前中介層。貝葉斯網絡在推理發生之前編碼領域知識、因果假設和概率依賴性，從而實現可審計的推理痕跡、不確定性量化和可爭辯的輸出。我們描述了這一框架的架構，並將其根植於一個福利資格場景中，識別出必須解決的基礎挑戰，包括語義對齊、動態模型構建、概率基礎和人類治理，以便在大規模上實現它。通過從事後解釋轉向事前概率中介，這項工作勾勒出一條原則性的道路，朝著不僅強大而且根本負責的人工智慧系統邁進。

##### **MetaConfigurator: AI-Assisted RDF Authoring from JSON Data**
2606.07094v1 by Felix Neubauer, Mahdi Jafarkhani, Kenichi Endo, Jürgen Pleiss, Benjamin Uekermann

Scientific workflows increasingly generate structured JSON data that is easy to exchange but difficult to interpret consistently across systems due to lacking semantic interoperability. While JSON Schema ensures structural validation, it provides no native support for Linked Data semantics.
  This paper presents an RDF Authoring View extending the open-source JSON Schema editor MetaConfigurator, enabling researchers to transform existing JSON, YAML, or CSV data into RDF using AI-assisted RML mappings, refine triples, execute SPARQL queries, visualize knowledge graphs, and export RDF serializations within a single integrated web interface. This workflow is supported by ontology-aware IRI auto-completion, bidirectional synchronization between JSON-LD text views and RDF triple tables, and AI-assisted SPARQL query generation from natural language hints.
  We demonstrate the workflow using laboratory data from metal-organic framework (MOF) synthesis experiments. Protocol data describing reagents, procedure steps, and quantities is converted from JSON to ontology-based JSON-LD via RML mappings. We then refine the semantic representation, query relationships between experimental conditions and outcomes, and explore the resulting knowledge graph interactively. This integrated environment bridges conventional structured data management with Semantic Web technologies while preserving experimental context and lowering technical barriers through AI assistance.

摘要：科學工作流程越來越多地生成結構化的 JSON 數據，這些數據易於交換，但由於缺乏語義互操作性，跨系統的一致解釋卻變得困難。雖然 JSON Schema 確保了結構驗證，但它並不提供對 Linked Data 語義的原生支持。<lb/>  
本文提出了一種 RDF 編輯視圖，擴展了開源的 JSON Schema 編輯器 MetaConfigurator，使研究人員能夠使用 AI 輔助的 RML 映射將現有的 JSON、YAML 或 CSV 數據轉換為 RDF，精煉三元組，執行 SPARQL 查詢，視覺化知識圖譜，並在單一集成的網頁介面中導出 RDF 序列化。<lb/>  
這一工作流程得到了本體感知的 IRI 自動補全、JSON-LD 文本視圖與 RDF 三元組表之間的雙向同步，以及基於自然語言提示的 AI 輔助 SPARQL 查詢生成的支持。<lb/>  
我們使用金屬有機框架 (MOF) 合成實驗的實驗室數據來演示這一工作流程。描述試劑、程序步驟和數量的協議數據通過 RML 映射從 JSON 轉換為基於本體的 JSON-LD。然後，我們精煉語義表示，查詢實驗條件與結果之間的關係，並互動式地探索生成的知識圖譜。這一集成環境將傳統的結構化數據管理與語義網技術相結合，同時保留實驗上下文並通過 AI 輔助降低技術障礙。

##### **EssentialGIN: a new approach for gene essentiality prediction based on graph isomorphism neural networks**
2606.07700v1 by Sahar Mansouri-Rad, Zahra Narimani, Parvin Razzaghi, Nazanin Hosseinkhan

Background: Prediction of essential genes (proteins), is a basic and challenging problem but at the same time very costly and time-consuming in wet-lab experiments. Predicting essential genes, only based on computational methods (to introduce wet-lab candidates) using centrality measures are not accurate and result in large number of false positives; therefore, more complex models such as deep learning and also integration of biological information are used in recent research to identify essential genes.
  Methods: In this work we focus on graph isomorphism networks, in order to embed proteins as a node in PPI network to conserve topological features of PPI network, and also integrate biological data such as gene expression data, gene orthology information and gene subcellular localization information, and introduced a deep architecture for predicting essential genes. Graph isomorphism network architecture is modified in this work for embedding node information.
  Results: Our experiments proved that the proposed method outperforms baseline centrality-based methods and also machine learning based methods such as Node2Vec, MLP, and also graph attention networks (GAT).
  Conclusion: In this paper we observed that using graph isomorphism networks that integrate biological data (as node attributes) and preserve network topology can significantly improve the essential gene prediction accuracy. In simpler organisms such as E. coli and D. melanogaster, methods such as multi-layer perceptron using Node2Vec embedding also performs very good, but in H. sapiens the introduced architecture significantly outperforms deep learning and other graph neural network solutions.
  Keywords: Essential gene prediction, graph neural network, graph isomorphism network, PPI network, node embedding

摘要：背景：預測基本基因（蛋白質）是一個基本且具有挑戰性的問題，但同時在濕實驗室實驗中非常耗費成本和時間。僅基於計算方法（以引入濕實驗室候選者）使用中心性度量來預測基本基因並不準確，並導致大量假陽性；因此，最近的研究中使用了更複雜的模型，如深度學習，並整合生物信息來識別基本基因。<lb/>  
方法：在這項工作中，我們專注於圖同構網絡，以便將蛋白質嵌入為PPI網絡中的一個節點，以保留PPI網絡的拓撲特徵，並整合生物數據，如基因表達數據、基因同源性信息和基因亞細胞定位信息，並引入了一種深度架構來預測基本基因。這項工作中對圖同構網絡架構進行了修改，以嵌入節點信息。<lb/>  
結果：我們的實驗證明，所提出的方法在性能上超越了基於中心性的基線方法以及基於機器學習的方法，如Node2Vec、MLP，以及圖注意力網絡（GAT）。<lb/>  
結論：在本文中，我們觀察到使用整合生物數據（作為節點屬性）並保留網絡拓撲的圖同構網絡可以顯著提高基本基因預測的準確性。在簡單的生物體中，如大腸桿菌和果蠅，使用Node2Vec嵌入的多層感知器等方法表現也非常好，但在智人中，所引入的架構顯著超越了深度學習和其他圖神經網絡解決方案。<lb/>  
關鍵詞：基本基因預測、圖神經網絡、圖同構網絡、PPI網絡、節點嵌入

##### **Hierarchical Semantic-Constrained Heterogeneous Graph for Audio-Visual Event Localization**
2606.07033v1 by Zhe Yang, Ruyi Zhang, Hongtao Chen, Wenrui Li, Hengyu Man, Wangmeng Zuo, Xiaopeng Fan

Open-vocabulary audio-visual event localization (OV-AVEL) jointly models audio-visual cues to recognize and temporally localize events, including categories unseen during training. Existing methods primarily learn joint audio-visual representations in Euclidean space, but still face two significant challenges. First, the lack of supervision signals for unseen categories makes it difficult to maintain audio-visual consistency across multiple temporal scales. Second, the lack of hierarchical constraints between segment- and video-level semantics prevents the model from establishing semantic consistency across different levels. To address these challenges, we propose a hierarchical semantic constrained heterogeneous graph (HSCHG) for audio-visual event localization framework. We first construct a heterogeneous hierarchical graph in Euclidean space, which includes audio and visual segment nodes and their corresponding video-level nodes. We use multi-directional temporal edges to capture complete temporal information within each modality. Simultaneously, we employ a dual-threshold filtering gated fusion strategy, introducing cross-modal information only when the alignment confidence is high. Furthermore, we introduce bidirectional semantic constraints between segment- and video-level representations to achieve semantic consistency across different levels. Based on this, we map the multi-level audio-visual representations and text prototypes uniformly into hyperbolic space. We use a hierarchical entailment regularization loss to characterize the hierarchical relationships between videos and segments. Extensive experimental results show that our method outperforms existing methods on the OV-AVEL benchmark. Ablation studies further validate the effectiveness of our method.

摘要：開放詞彙音視訊事件定位（OV-AVEL）共同建模音視訊線索以識別和時間定位事件，包括訓練期間未見的類別。現有方法主要在歐幾里得空間中學習聯合音視訊表示，但仍面臨兩個重大挑戰。首先，對於未見類別缺乏監督信號使得在多個時間尺度上維持音視訊一致性變得困難。其次，段落和視頻層次語義之間缺乏層次約束，阻止模型在不同層次之間建立語義一致性。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了一種層次語義約束異質圖（HSCHG）用於音視訊事件定位框架。我們首先在歐幾里得空間中構建一個異質層次圖，其中包括音訊和視覺段節點及其對應的視頻層次節點。我們使用多方向時間邊來捕捉每種模態內完整的時間信息。同時，我們採用雙閾值過濾門控融合策略，僅在對齊信心高時引入跨模態信息。此外，我們在段落和視頻層次表示之間引入雙向語義約束，以實現不同層次之間的語義一致性。在此基礎上，我們將多層次音視訊表示和文本原型均勻映射到雙曲空間。我們使用層次推理正則化損失來表徵視頻和段落之間的層次關係。大量實驗結果表明，我們的方法在OV-AVEL基準上優於現有方法。消融研究進一步驗證了我們方法的有效性。

##### **Pharmacogenomic Knowledge Graph Augmentation for Graph Neural Network-Based Drug-Drug Interaction Prediction**
2606.07698v1 by Juergen Dietrich

Graph neural networks (GNNs) applied to drug-drug interaction (DDI) prediction rely exclusively on molecular structure encoded as SMILES-derived graphs. Prior work in this series demonstrated that model performance is bounded by the structural information content of training labels -- an Information Ceiling -- that architectural refinements alone cannot overcome. The present study investigates whether pharmacogenomic prior knowledge from the PharmGKB database partially closes this ceiling by providing metabolic pathway context that is independent of, and complementary to, molecular structure. Cytochrome P450 (CYP) enzyme substrate, inhibitor, and inducer annotations for four clinically relevant isoforms (CYP2D6, CYP3A4, CYP2C19, CYP2C9) are extracted and incorporated as a 12-dimensional feature vector concatenated to the molecular embedding prior to interaction prediction. Experiments are conducted under both pair-level and drug-level data splits to quantify generalization to unseen drugs. Results indicate that knowledge graph (KG) augmentation substantially improves DDI type classification under pair-level split conditions (F1-macro: 0.532 vs. 0.241 baseline), while binary interaction detection and drug-level generalization remain bounded by the Information Ceiling (AUC inflation: 0.224 vs. 0.250 baseline). Mechanistic validation on strictly held-out compounds confirms that augmentation preferentially improves CYP2C9-mediated interaction prediction, with probabilities increasing from 0.033-0.117 (baseline) to 0.560-0.586 (KG-augmented). An extension to single-molecule toxicity prediction on the Tox21 benchmark confirms that the effect is contingent on pharmacogenomic annotation coverage. These findings motivate the multimodal framework proposed for the subsequent study in this series.

摘要：圖神經網絡（GNNs）應用於藥物-藥物相互作用（DDI）預測完全依賴於作為SMILES衍生圖編碼的分子結構。先前的研究顯示，模型性能受到訓練標籤的結構信息內容的限制——即信息天花板——而僅僅通過架構改進無法克服。當前研究探討了來自PharmGKB數據庫的藥物基因組學先驗知識是否部分關閉這一天花板，通過提供獨立於分子結構且互補的代謝途徑上下文。提取四種臨床相關亞型（CYP2D6、CYP3A4、CYP2C19、CYP2C9）的細胞色素P450（CYP）酶底物、抑制劑和誘導劑註釋，並將其作為12維特徵向量，在進行相互作用預測之前與分子嵌入進行串接。實驗在配對級別和藥物級別數據拆分下進行，以量化對未見藥物的泛化能力。結果表明，知識圖（KG）增強在配對級別拆分條件下顯著改善DDI類型分類（F1-macro: 0.532對比0.241基線），而二元相互作用檢測和藥物級別泛化仍然受到信息天花板的限制（AUC膨脹: 0.224對比0.250基線）。對嚴格保留的化合物進行的機制驗證確認，增強優先改善CYP2C9介導的相互作用預測，概率從0.033-0.117（基線）增至0.560-0.586（KG增強）。對Tox21基準的單分子毒性預測的擴展確認，這一效果依賴於藥物基因組學註釋的覆蓋範圍。這些發現激勵了為本系列後續研究提出的多模態框架。

##### **TianJi-Environ: An Autonomous AI Scientist for Atmospheric Environmental Research**
2606.07697v1 by Haoluo Zhao, Hongchun Zhang, Nan Li, Jing-Jia Luo, Kaikai Zhang, Mengyang Yu, Nan Chen, Tao Song, Fan Meng

As atmospheric environmental prediction continues to improve, interpretable validation of pollution mechanisms and feedback processes has become a main challenge in atmospheric chemistry. Yet mechanism validation based on complex numerical models still relies heavily on expert knowledge: mechanistic hypotheses must be operationalized into executable experiments, and model outputs must be organized into traceable evidence. We present TianJi-Environ, an auditable AI Scientist for atmospheric-chemistry mechanism validation. TianJi-Environ establishes the first WRF-Chem-based multi-agent framework that autonomously drives complex atmospheric-chemistry simulations, converting mechanistic hypotheses into executable configurations, testing experiments, and evidence criteria. Using ozone response and particulate-matter feedback as two representative examples, we demonstrate TianJi-Environ's capability for mechanism validation. In a summertime ozone case over the North China Plain, the system detects directionally consistent aerosol-radiation-interaction signals in shortwave radiation and boundary-layer height, but judges the evidence for ozone response to NOx control to be incomplete. In a wintertime PM2.5 case over the Guanzhong Basin, it localizes the unsupported link to insufficient propagation from black-carbon perturbation to particulate response and missing diagnostics of vertical absorptive heating. These results show that TianJi-Environ makes expert-driven mechanism validation explicit, structured, and auditable, offering a reproducible paradigm for multi-agent systems coupled with complex atmospheric-chemistry models.

摘要：隨著大氣環境預測的不斷改善，污染機制和反饋過程的可解釋性驗證已成為大氣化學中的一個主要挑戰。然而，基於複雜數值模型的機制驗證仍然在很大程度上依賴於專家知識：機制假設必須轉化為可執行的實驗，模型輸出必須組織成可追溯的證據。我們提出了 TianJi-Environ，一個可審計的 AI 科學家，用於大氣化學機制驗證。TianJi-Environ 建立了第一個基於 WRF-Chem 的多代理框架，自主驅動複雜的大氣化學模擬，將機制假設轉化為可執行的配置、測試實驗和證據標準。以臭氧反應和顆粒物反饋作為兩個代表性例子，我們展示了 TianJi-Environ 在機制驗證方面的能力。在北中國平原的夏季臭氧案例中，系統檢測到短波輻射和邊界層高度中的方向一致的氣溶膠-輻射-相互作用信號，但認為對 NOx 控制的臭氧反應的證據不完整。在關中盆地的冬季 PM2.5 案例中，它將不支持的鏈接定位為黑碳擾動到顆粒反應的傳播不足，以及缺少垂直吸收加熱的診斷。這些結果表明，TianJi-Environ 使專家驅動的機制驗證變得明確、結構化且可審計，為與複雜大氣化學模型耦合的多代理系統提供了一個可重複的範式。

##### **DSFNet: Learning Dual-Domain Spectral Operators for Multi-Modality Spatio-Temporal Forecasting in Urban Transportation Systems**
2606.07695v1 by Yongchao Li, Yang Li, Zhuoxuan Li, Jun Chen, Chu Zhang, Jinde Cao, Leszek Rutkowski

Multi-Modality Spatio-Temporal Forecasting (MoSTF) extends traditional spatio-temporal forecasting by incorporating diverse traffic modalities. Despite significant recent strides in spatio-temporal modeling, existing approaches often fail to explicitly model the coupling relationships between different modality variables. Accurate MoSTF is challenging, as it requires modeling (1) temporal dynamic heterogeneity under exogenous influences and (2) heterogeneous spatial dependencies alongside complex cross-variable couplings. To address these challenges, we propose the Dual-Domain Spectral Filtering Network (DSFNet). Our framework employs dual-domain spectral filtering to capture heterogeneous spatial patterns and explicitly model the relationships between variables. Unlike graph-based message passing or dense attention over node-modality pairs, DSFNet factorizes space-modality interactions into feature-domain and spatial-domain spectral operators, enabling scalable modeling of nonlocal dependencies and cross-modality couplings. Furthermore, we introduce an external gating mechanism to adaptively regulate temporal dynamics under external influences. We validate our method through extensive experiments on five representative real-world traffic datasets. Compared with the second-best baselines, DSFNet reduces MAE by 3.21%-10.16% across these datasets. The results demonstrate that DSFNet significantly outperforms existing state-of-the-art baselines in accuracy while exhibiting efficiency and robustness.

摘要：多模態時空預測（MoSTF）通過整合多樣的交通模態，擴展了傳統的時空預測。儘管在時空建模方面最近取得了顯著進展，現有的方法往往未能明確建模不同模態變數之間的耦合關係。準確的 MoSTF 是一項挑戰，因為它需要建模（1）在外部影響下的時間動態異質性，以及（2）與複雜的跨變數耦合一起的異質空間依賴性。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了雙域頻譜過濾網絡（DSFNet）。我們的框架採用雙域頻譜過濾來捕捉異質空間模式並明確建模變數之間的關係。與基於圖的消息傳遞或對節點-模態對的密集注意力不同，DSFNet 將空間-模態交互因子化為特徵域和空間域的頻譜運算符，使得非局部依賴性和跨模態耦合的可擴展建模成為可能。此外，我們引入了一個外部閘控機制，以自適應地調節外部影響下的時間動態。我們通過對五個具有代表性的真實世界交通數據集進行廣泛實驗來驗證我們的方法。與第二最佳基準相比，DSFNet 在這些數據集中將 MAE 降低了 3.21%-10.16%。結果表明，DSFNet 在準確性上顯著超越了現有的最先進基準，同時展現了效率和穩健性。

##### **Didact: A Cross-Domain Capability Discovery System for Defence**
2606.06942v1 by Aarya Bodhankar, Aditya Joshi, Bao Gia Doan, Thomas Marchant, Oscar Leslie, Flora Salim

Policymakers in defence and defence-aligned sectors must monitor rapidly evolving research alongside sector priorities relevant to operational and strategic needs. ##### **Quantum-Inspired Trace-Augmented Evidence Selection for Reasoning over Structured Hypothesis Spaces**
2606.06941v1 by Laura Wynter, Nirvik Sahoo, Paul Griffin

Large language models (LLMs) now solve a wide range of expert-level exams at or above human level, yet remain brittle on specialised, evidence-intensive domains such as law. On these tasks, errors arise not only from gaps in world knowledge but also from subtle distinctions between pieces of evidence and inconsistent use of supporting evidence. The most common aggregator over sampled chain-of-thought (CoT) traces, majority vote, returns the most popular answer regardless of whether its evidence is actually strongest. We propose to treat the selection of CoT reasoning fragments into a set of evidence as an explicit combinatorial optimisation problem, allowing well-supported but minority hypotheses to override noisy majorities, and to evaluate the approach on legal-reasoning benchmarks that are particularly sensitive to evidence quality. We introduce EP-HUBO (Evidence Pool Higher-Order Binary Optimisation), which generates multiple CoT traces with a small local model, parses fragments into per-hypothesis evidence pools, solves a higher-order unconstrained binary optimisation per pool with quality-derived weights (relevance, specificity, distinctiveness), and delegates a single adjudication call per question to a frontier model. We evaluate EP-HUBO on two evidence-intensive legal benchmarks using both simulated annealing on classical hardware and the Dirac-3 photonic entropy-quantum machine from Quantum Computing Inc. HUBO-style optimisation gives a principled way to aggregate reasoning fragments while preserving minority-but-correct hypotheses, and is most valuable in low-contamination domains where frontier models have not already absorbed the benchmark material.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）現在能夠解決各種專家級考試，達到或超過人類水平，但在法律等專門且依賴證據的領域仍然顯得脆弱。在這些任務中，錯誤不僅源於世界知識的缺口，還來自於證據之間的微妙區別和支持證據的不一致使用。對於採樣的思考鏈（CoT）痕跡，最常見的聚合器——多數投票，會返回最受歡迎的答案，而不考慮其證據是否實際上是最強的。我們建議將CoT推理片段的選擇視為一個明確的組合優化問題，允許支持良好但屬於少數的假設覆蓋嘈雜的多數，並在特別敏感於證據質量的法律推理基準上評估該方法。我們介紹EP-HUBO（證據池高階二元優化），它使用一個小型本地模型生成多個CoT痕跡，將片段解析為每個假設的證據池，並使用質量導出的權重（相關性、特異性、區別性）對每個池進行高階無約束二元優化，並將每個問題的單一裁定呼叫委派給前沿模型。我們在兩個依賴證據的法律基準上評估EP-HUBO，使用經典硬體上的模擬退火和來自Quantum Computing Inc.的Dirac-3光子熵量子機。HUBO風格的優化提供了一種原則性的方法來聚合推理片段，同時保留少數但正確的假設，並且在前沿模型尚未吸收基準材料的低污染領域中最具價值。

##### **Declarative Skills for AI Agents in Knowledge-Grounded Tool-Use Workflows**
2606.06923v1 by M. Danish Lim, I. Danial Bin Sharudin, Wen Han Chen, Cedric Lim, Laura Wynter

We study orchestration mechanisms for tool-using AI agents in realistic customer-service workflows over an unstructured knowledge base. We argue that declarative agents -- AI agents equipped with natural-language skill files appended to the system prompt -- are an effective orchestration paradigm. Concretely, we compare (i) a DeclarativeAgent that reads three domain-specific skill files at inference time and decides its own control flow, (ii) an ImperativeAgent based on a programmatic state machine with explicit phases, and (iii) an unscaffolded baseline agent modeled after the $τ$-Knowledge benchmark agent. Our ImperativeAgent is motivated by externalised-control inference as in Recursive Language Models and graph-based orchestration frameworks. We formalise the three agents as policy classes within a decentralised partially-observable Markov decision process and analyse their information-theoretic and structural properties; we then test the predicted differences empirically on five language models and two retrieval regimes. Our results show that retrieval quality is a dominant bottleneck for AI agents: when evidence is incomplete or skewed, all agents degrade substantially, and skill files cannot recover lost performance. Under high-quality retrieval, however, declarative skills consistently improve accuracy on procedural tasks and reduce orchestration errors, while the imperative state machine's brittleness does not reliably improve task success or compliance.

摘要：我們研究在非結構化知識庫上，工具使用的人工智慧代理在現實客戶服務工作流程中的協調機制。我們主張，聲明式代理——配備有自然語言技能檔案的人工智慧代理，這些檔案附加在系統提示中——是一種有效的協調範式。具體而言，我們比較了 (i) 一個在推理時讀取三個特定領域技能檔案並決定自身控制流程的聲明式代理，(ii) 一個基於具有明確階段的程序狀態機的命令式代理，以及 (iii) 一個未經架構的基準代理，該代理是根據 $τ$-Knowledge 基準代理建模的。我們的命令式代理受到外部控制推理的啟發，這與遞歸語言模型和基於圖的協調框架相似。我們將這三個代理形式化為去中心化的部分可觀察馬可夫決策過程中的政策類別，並分析它們的信息理論和結構特性；然後，我們在五個語言模型和兩個檢索模式上實證測試預測的差異。我們的結果顯示，檢索質量是人工智慧代理的主要瓶頸：當證據不完整或偏斜時，所有代理的表現都會大幅下降，而技能檔案無法恢復失去的性能。然而，在高質量檢索下，聲明式技能在程序性任務上持續提高準確性並減少協調錯誤，而命令式狀態機的脆弱性則未能可靠地提高任務成功率或合規性。

##### **Workflow-to-Skill: Skill Creation via Routing-Workflow-Semantics-Attachments Decomposition**
2606.06893v1 by Yuyang Zhang, Xinyuan Han, Xudong Jiang, Run Wang

Large language model agents increasingly rely on Skills to encode procedural knowledge, yet high-quality Skills remain costly to hand-write. This paper studies automatic Skill construction from heterogeneous interaction evidence, including demonstrations, agent trajectories, tool traces, and execution logs. We argue that trace-to-skill construction is not simple summarization tasks, because traces are fragmented, redundant, and may miss rare but safety-critical behaviors. To address this, we introduce RWSA, a workflow-oriented intermediate representation that decomposes Skills into Workflow structure, execution Semantics, and runtime Attachments, capturing task decomposition, control flow, verification, safety, rollback, and state management. Building on RWSA, we propose W2S, a framework that segments traces, induces local Skill drafts, aligns shared structures, reconciles branches, and compresses redundancy while preserving evidence and confidence annotations. Experiments on 70 Skills show that W2S improves behavioral replay consistency by 10.5% over summarization- and prompting-based baselines, highlighting the need to treat traces as executable runtime specifications rather than compressible text.

摘要：大型語言模型代理越來越依賴技能來編碼程序知識，但高品質的技能仍然需要昂貴的手動撰寫。本文研究了從異質互動證據自動構建技能的過程，包括示範、代理軌跡、工具痕跡和執行日誌。我們認為，痕跡到技能的構建並不是簡單的總結任務，因為痕跡是碎片化的、冗餘的，並且可能缺少稀有但對安全至關重要的行為。為了解決這個問題，我們引入了RWSA，一種面向工作流程的中介表示，將技能分解為工作流程結構、執行語義和運行時附件，捕捉任務分解、控制流、驗證、安全性、回滾和狀態管理。在RWSA的基礎上，我們提出了W2S，一個框架，用於分段痕跡、誘導局部技能草稿、對齊共享結構、調和分支，並在保留證據和信心註釋的同時壓縮冗餘。對70個技能的實驗表明，W2S在行為重放一致性上比基於總結和提示的基線提高了10.5%，突顯了將痕跡視為可執行運行時規範而非可壓縮文本的必要性。
